44002036	Aso kojen ekek kere loka Isirael kabeit ebe etarau Edeke ŋes Ejakait ka Kristo da , ŋes Yesu loipotu kibubukis . ”
44002037	Nakiirariata ŋun koditasi ikecetauon , kobalas Petero ka ikiyakia ice ebe , “ Kekonakis ai , iinacan ? ”
44002038	Kotema Petero atiar , “ Kitoronikinos , kibatisaunos , ŋinituŋanan kayesi , kokiror loka Yesu Kristo , kanuka aisionio naka adiakanaretakus ; kiinakinio ainakinet naka Emoyo Lokalaunan .
44002039	Naarai aisumunet erai kanukus ka ikusidwe da , ka ituŋa kere luelwaka , kere luenyarauni Ejakait Edekewok mamakeŋ . ”
44002040	Kitejenu kes kakiro ace nuipu ka aicor da ebe , “ Kitajarunos katur kana namagul . ”
44002041	Aponi kibatisai ŋul lukecamunete akekirot , kiyatakinos ituŋa kapaaran kaŋin bala ilukumin iuni .
44002042	Kinyikokinito kaisisianakin naka ikiyakia , ka eidicane , ka aibil emugati , ka ailipasia da .
44002043	Kokurianari ŋinituŋanan ; kitwasamai ikiyakia aswam nukaumokin nuipu ka aanyuneta da .
44002044	Kojaas luiyuunito kere nepepe , kimorikikina koboro kere ;
44002045	Kogwelanasi luebeito ka iborokec ka akoranakin ituŋa kere , kwape kipudar ŋinituŋanan .
44002046	Kinyikokinito ŋinipaaran ketau ediopet kotoma oyekalu , ebilete emugati kore , komorete kalakara ka etau loelai ,
44002047	ituritos Edeke kitojokito ituŋa kere . Kiyatanakini Ejakait otiaikec ŋinipaaran lukitajario .
44003001	Kosodete edokarete Petero ka Yokana alosit oyekalu esawa loka ailip , ŋes lokikanyetekaoŋon .
44003002	Ido adakitai etuŋanan Ioeŋwalit ameun kaurioke , lokibwaanakinio ŋinipaaran orute loka eyakalu loenyaritai Lokajokan , tetere ilipitoi nukaitim kama ejaas ituŋa luelomanarete toma oyekalu ,
44003003	Keanyu ŋol Petero ka Yokana elomarete oyekalu , kilip kes nukaitim .
44003004	Kosodi Petero kosesen ŋes nepepe ka Yokana , kotema atiar , “ Kiteoi sio . ”
44003005	Koŋolia kes , komun adumun ibore kamakec .
44003006	Konye Petero kotema atiar , “ Emamei eoŋ epuesa karaida esabu ; konye yenikija keoŋ , kainakini ŋin , Kokiror loka Yesu Kristo loko Nasaret , kosakasak . ”
44003007	Kitiŋ akekan nakoteten , kitonyou ŋes : atipet kodomut akekeje ka ikekurunya agogoŋ .
44003008	Kodetu , kobwo , kogeu alosit ; koloma oyekalu nepepe kakes , elosi , esomanari , iturit Edeke ,
44003009	Koanyut ituŋa kere elosi iturit Edeke .
44003010	Kojenata ebe kerai ŋesi ŋopeŋol lokiboie ilipitoi nukaitim korute Lokajokan loka eyekalu : koumokis noi ŋin naedoikinit ŋes .
44003011	Naperiŋa ŋesi itiŋit Petero ka Yokana , kokerut ituŋa kere mama ejaas toma alomaret naenyaritai naka Solomon , eumokinitos noi .
44003012	Nakeanyunia Petero , Koboŋok ituŋa ebe , “ Yes ikiliok luka Isirael , kanukinyo iwumokinitotor nu , kanukinyo da kiseseniata sio , bala Iem kitolosi ŋes kakosipedor arai bo kakosiyoŋit Edeke ?
44003013	Edeke loka Aburaam , ka loka Isaak , ka loka Yakob , Edeke loka lukapapaawok etopoloo Eketelepat Yesu ; loipotu yesi kijaikis , ka aiŋer kakonyen nuka Pilato , nakekotor aosikin ŋes .
44003014	Konye yes ipotu koŋeroto Lokalaunan Lokadoliton , kilipa ainakinio ekaaran ,
44003015	koarata Ekapolon loka aijar ; lokitajaruni Edeke kotoma okatwak , Kirai isio ikekajenak .
44003016	Kanuka aiyuun ekekiror ainak ekekiror etuŋanan lo agogoŋ , loianyunete loijenete da ; eebo , aiyuun ŋin naejai mamakeŋ ainak lo aŋaleu naeleleba kakonyenekus kere .
44003017	“ Kwana da iinacan , ajeni ebe iswamato ŋun kanu mam ijeniata , kwape eswamaata ikayaitokokus da .
44003018	Konye akiro kwa nukelimonokini Edeke ameun apeŋo kaituk nuka inabin kere ebe ibusakinit Kristoke aiticanio , etodoliki kwaŋin .
44003019	Aso do kitoronikinos , kibelokinos , komwatarai akusidiakanareta , tetere edolete apakio nuka aisikwarunio nuepote kama ejai Ejakait ,
44003020	Ido tetere ijukuni Kristo lokiseikinitai apeŋo , ŋes Yesu :
44003021	loibusakinit akuj aisukunyikin aitodol apakio nuiteteunere akiro kere nukinerit Edeke kaituke nuka inabinoke lukalaunak ameun kageunet naka akwapin .
44003022	Naarai enerit teni Musa ebe , ‘ Kitonyoikini yes Ejakait Edeke enabi kotoma oinacanakus loeputos keoŋ . Ŋol ŋes iirarete kotoma akiro kere nukilimokini yes .
44003023	Kosodi kanen , ŋinituŋanan yenimam iirari enabi ŋol emudiario kotuŋa . ’
44003024	Eebo , inabin kere ameun ka Samuel ka luketupakinete ŋes , kere lukineras , kelimonokinete nuka apaarasia kanu .
44003025	Iraas yesi idwe luka inabin ka aitutuket ŋin nakitutuki Edeke kalukapapaakus , elimokini Aburaam ebe , ‘ Isirereŋio atekerin kere nuka akwapin kotoma aurikon . ’
44003026	Kedau Edeke aitajarun eketelepat Yesu , kijuku ber mamakus , tetere kisirereŋi yes aibelokin ŋinidiopet kayesi kotoma nukaronokokus . ”
44004001	Napineras kituŋa , koponikis isasedotin ka ekapolokiton loka eyekalu ka Isadukayon ,
44004002	ekadakinito noi naarai isisianakinete ituŋa , ka alimono kin ajarun naka lukatwak kotoma Yesu .
44004003	Kikamut kogolokis aidaris kiton tupuruc : naarai kitiboŋit akwap .
44004004	Konye kiyuunito luipu luapotu kiirasi akirot ; etiai da loka ikiliok kodol kwaka ilukumin ikany .
44004005	Kosodi kanen tupuruc , kotukonokinos ikayaitokokec ka imakio ka ikewadikak Yerusalem ;
44004006	ka Anas losasedoti lopeti , ka Kaiapa , ka Yokana , ka Alegesanda da , ka ŋul lukeraas luka ekek loka losasedoti lopeti .
44004007	Kedautu aisibwo kes kokidiŋ , kiŋita ebe , “ Kanuka apedor anyoin , ka okiror enyoin , iswamaata yesi nu ? ”
44004008	Kosodi Petero , kilelebun Emoyo Lokalaunan , kotema kes atiar , “ Yes ikayaitok luka ituŋa , ka imakio ,
44004009	arai kiiŋisi lolo akiro nukajokak nueswamakinio loŋwalas , epone lokitanaleunere ,
44004010	kojenutu yesi kere , ka ituŋa kere luka Isirael ebe , Kokiror loka Yesu Kristo loko Nasaret , lokibubukinete yesi , lokitajaruni Edeke kokatwak , kanuka ŋol ebwoi etuŋanan lo kakonyenekus eŋalei ,
44004011	ŋol ŋes amoru nakinerete yesi ikadukok , naebwaikin araut amoru nati naka agor .
44004012	Kwabo emamei aitajar kotoma ece kere : naarai emamei ecekiror kokwap kakuj loeinakinitai ituŋa , loibusakinitor oni aitajario . ”
44004013	Kosodi keanyutu atitiŋ naka Petero ka Yokana , komisiikis da ebe eraas ituŋa lumam isisianakinitai , luemamei aijen , koumokis ; kojenut da ebe kejaas kaYesu .
44004014	Nakeanyuniata da lokitaŋaleunio ebwoi nepepe kakes , komamuut nueboŋokinete ,
44004015	Konye kicorakis kes alomar kaurianet , kineranakinos ebe ,
44004016	“ Kikonakini ai ituŋa lu ? Naarai idelelei kotuŋa kere luiboiete koYerusalem ebe eswamai aanyunet naejenio kamakec ; kwabo mam kipedori aiŋer .
44004017	Konye kinye akirot na aiyatakin aisiarakin otuŋa , ketukuriana kes , sirikinerata bobo kediotunanan kere kokiror kaŋol . ”
44004018	Konyaraut kes , kicorakis kinyeis einer cut karaida aisisianakin kokiror loka Yesu .
44004019	Konye koboŋokis Petero ka Yokana kotemasi kes atiar , “ Arai edolit kakonyen nuka Edeke aiirar yes aitelekarit Edeke , kotuboto yesi :
44004020	naarai mam kipedori ainyein einer akiro nukianyunit ka nukiirarit da . ”
44004021	Nakedauniata aitukurian bobo , koosikis , mam apedorete aitican kes kanuka ituŋa ; naarai kitopolooritos ituŋa kere Edeke kanuka ŋun nukiswamao .
44004022	Naarai keraas ikar luka etuŋanan lokiswamakinio naanyunet ŋin naka aitaŋaleun luedeparito akaisaoŋon .
44004023	Nakeosikinere koloto neejaas ikecetuŋa , kitatamikis kes akiro kere nukelimokinete isasedotin lupeti ka imakio .
44004024	Nakiirariata , kikeut ikeceporotoi nepepe mama ejai Edeke , kotemasi atiar , “ Wu Ejakait , lokisubi akuj , ka akwap , ka aŋolol , ka kere da luejaas tomakec :
44004025	ibu kiner kotoma Emoyo Lokalaunan kaituk naka papaakosi Daudi ekonitelepat ebe , ‘ Kanukinyo enyunyuratatar lukacekwapin , Ka ituŋa da itetemonoroto aamameak ?
44004026	Etemonokinos ikabakan luka akwapin , Etukonokinos ikayaitok nepepe , Asurokin Ejakait , ka Lokinyonyoikitonoke akinyet . ’
44004027	Naarai abeit etukonokinos Kerode ka Pontio Pilato , nepepe ka Imo ka ituŋa luka Isirael ore lo asurokin ekonitelepat lokalaunan Yesu , loinyonyoikinit akinyet ,
44004028	tetere iswamaete kere nuelosikinit akonikan , ka nuinerunit ŋol ajaun .
44004029	Kwana da , wu Ejakait , kosesen aitukurianakec : koinak ikonibulesin einer akirot katitiŋ kere ,
44004030	nairioria akonikan aitaŋaleun ; kiswamai da aanyuneta ka nukaumokin kanuka ekiror loka ekonitelepat lokalaunan Yesu . ”
44004031	Nakedauniata ailip , kitamaranai aibois kama ketukonokina ; kilelebunos kere Emoyo Lokalaunan , kinerata akirot naka Edeke katitiŋ .
44004032	Kejaas ekodet kere loka luiyuunito ketau ediopet ka aijar adiopet : kwabo emamei idiopet yenikebala ebe ibore kere yenejaatar erai yenike ; dimarai emorikikinito iboro kere .
44004033	Kitejenut ikiyakia ajarun naka Ejakait Yesu kapedor naepol , kojai asianut naepol mamakec kere .
44004034	Amamei yenilwaritoi kotomakec , naarai ituŋa kere lukejaas amanat arai itogoi , apotu kogwelanasi , koyaata etiai loka iboro lukegwelunete
44004035	kibwaikis akejen nuka ikiyakia : kokorakinai ŋinituŋanan kwape kipudar .
44004036	Yosep da , lokenyaraete ikiyakia Baranaba , ( apolouke Okoku loka aitalakaar ) Elebit , lokeurikinio Kupuro ,
44004037	kejai ŋes amana kogwela , koyau apesan kibwaik akejen nuka ikiyakia .
44005001	Konye ekiliokit ediopet , ekekiror Anania , ka akeberu Sapira , abu kogwela ibore yenajaatar ,
44005002	kiŋadak acepesan kotiai , kojeni akeberu da , koyau ace , kibwaik akejen nuka ikiyakia .
44005003	Konye kotema Petero atiar , “ Anania , kanukinyo kisilelebia Satan etaukon aimod Emoyo Lokalaunan , ka aiŋadakin da acepesan kotiai loka amana ?
44005004	Arai kesalakinit mam egwelara , mam kereka kesalit erai nakon ? Nakedaunere agwelar , mam kerai nakakonipedor ? Kikonakini bo ai ibwaikin akirot ŋin otaukon ? Mam imodit ituŋa konye Edeke . ”
44005005	Nakiiraria Anania akiro ŋun , kibiror kotwana . Kokuriakaros ituŋa kere noi lukiirarete ŋun .
44005006	Konyout ikatumunak konunukoto , kodakasi kiŋa , kidaata .
44005007	Ketuboros bala isawan iuni kolom akeberu da komam ejeni nukedoikinete .
44005008	Kotema Petero atiar , “ Kolimokinai , ipotu kereka kogwelasi amana kotiai kaŋol ” Kotema atiar , “ Eebo , kotiai kaŋol . ”
44005009	Kotema Petero atiar , “ Kanukinyo ineruniata akodun Emoyo loka Ejakait ? Koany , akejen nuka luedaete okilenikon ejaas okek , kidakarete jo da . ”
44005010	Atipet kibirokin akejeke kotwana . Kolomut ikatumunak kodumut ketwana , kodakasi kiŋa , kidaata kidunyas kokilenike .
44005011	Kokurianar Ekanisa kere , ka ituŋa kere lukiirarete ŋun .
44005012	Kiswamai aanyuneta ka nukaumokin nuipu kotuŋa kakanin nuka ikiyakia . Kojaenenas kere nepepe kediopetau alomaret naka Solomon .
44005013	Ice da mam apotu kotitiŋikis aimorikikin kakes , konye ituŋa kitopoloorito kes .
44005014	Kiyatanakinos lukiyuunito mama ejai Ejakait , ikepuak , ikiliok ka aŋor ;
44005015	kodakununete lukadekak orotin , ka aiperionokin ojam ka opalisin , tetere naitorio Petero kodolokini etoribeke ice kakesi .
44005016	Kotukonokinos da ituŋa lukoreria lukeapias ko Yerusalem , koyaununete lukadekak ka ŋul lukiticanenete ajokin nueroko ; kitaŋaleunoi kes kere .
44005017	Konye konyou losasedoti lopeti ka lukejaas nepepe kaŋes kere , ŋes erioŋet loka Isadukayon , ileleba ekolo ,
44005018	Kikamut ikiyakia koenikis aidaris naka ituŋa kere .
44005019	Konye kuare koŋaa emalaika loka Ejakait ikekia luka aidaris , kitolom kes kotema atiar ,
44005020	“ Koloto , kobwaata koyekalu kolimokis ituŋa akiro kere nuka Aijar kana . ”
44005021	Nakiirariata kesi , kolomasi oyekalu tupuruc sek , kisisianakis . Konye kobu losasedoti lopeti , ka ŋul lukejaas nepepe kaŋes , konyaraut aurianet , ka imakio kere luka idwe luka Isirael , kiyakiasi ituŋa aidaris tetere eyaunete kes .
44005022	Konye nakedolioto ikejaanakinak mam eanyuna kesi kaidaris ; koboŋut kolimokis kes ebe ,
44005023	“ Kidum aidaris eenen ejok , ebwoete ikedarak da kokekia ; konye nakiŋaaria mam edumuna idiotuŋanan kotoma . ”
44005024	Nakiiraria ekapolokiton loka eyekalu ka isasedotin lupeti akiro ŋun , kobuonokinos noi kanukec ebe , “ Ikonakini bo do akirot na ai ? ”
44005025	Kobu etuŋanan kolimok kes ebe , “ Ituŋa ŋul lukienikinito yesi aidaris ejaas toma oyekalu , ebwoete isisianakinete ituŋa . ”
44005026	Kosodi kolot ekapolokiton nepepe ka ikejaanakinak koomata kes , konye mere kagogoŋ , naarai kekuriaka ituŋa kinyeis aibiribir kes kamor .
44005027	Nakeyauniata , kibwaikis akonyen nuka aurianet . Kiŋit losasedoti lopeti ebe ,
44005028	“ Kipou kecorakis yes kagogoŋ ebe Sirikisisianakis kokiror kalo ; ido koany , ilelebata Yerusalem kaisisianakinikus , ikotosi ayaŋaun aokot nuka etuŋanan kaŋol mamakosi . ”
44005029	Konye koboŋokis Petero ka ikiyakia ebe , “ Kibusakinit arimarit Edeke aitelekarit ituŋa .
44005030	Abu Edeke loka lukapapaawok kitajaru Yesu , lokiarete kaikajakin okitoi .
44005031	Etopoloo Edeke ŋes kakanike nakoteten korau Lokapolon ka Eketajaran , koinak Isirael aitoronokin ka aisionio adiakanareta .
44005032	Kirai isio ikajenak luka akiro kaŋun , nepepe ka Emoyo Lokalaunan , loainak Edeke kere luerimasi ŋes . ”
44005033	Nakiirariata ŋun , konomos noi ikecetauon , kinerut aiar kes .
44005034	Konye etuŋanan ediopet , Eparisayot ekekiror Gamaliel , ekesisianakinan loka ikisila , lokeyonito ituŋa kere , kobwo kaurianet , kicorak kitolomarai ber ikiyakia kiŋa .
44005035	Kotema kes atiar , “ Yes ikiliok luka Isirael , kocoito nuiswamakinete ituŋa ŋul .
44005036	Naarai eroko apaarasia nu edoluno abu Teudas konyou , kituro ebe erai lokapolon ; kimorikikinos ŋes kituŋa bala akwat aoŋon ; konye koarai ŋes , kere da lukerimarete ŋes kisiarakinos , mam eraun ibore .
44005037	Akaulo kaŋol konyou Yuda Egalilayat , kapaarasia nuka aibil akwes , kiria ice kotuŋa atupar ŋes ; ŋes da abu koolio ; kere da lukerimarete ŋes kisiarakinos .
44005038	Kwana da katemari yes atiar , Kinaca ituŋa ŋul , kinyeisi kes ; naarai akirot na arai aswam na , arai erai naka ituŋa , eoliori ;
44005039	konye arai erai naka Edeke , mam ipedorete aitoolior kes ; kinyeis diat atakanun bala itijiete Edeke . ”
44005040	Kocamut akekiro ; nakenyarauniata ikiyakia , kodaata , kicorakis kes kinyeis einer kokiror loka Yesu , koosikis .
44005041	Aso kolomut kesi kaurianet , iyalamasi naarai imaritai luibusakinit aiticanio kanuka Ekiror kaŋol .
44005042	Ido ŋinipaaran , koyekalu ka oreria da mam inyeina aisisianakin ka alimonokin nuka Yesu ebe ŋes Kristo .
44006001	Kapaarasia kaŋun nakiyatakinor etiai loka ikesisiak , kojau aŋuurian naka Iyonanin aluikin Iburanian naarai aponi kopalunai apuserunukec kotoma aijaanakin naka ŋinipaaran .
44006002	Konyaraut lutomon ka luarei ekodet ŋol loka ikesisiak , kotemasi atiar , “ Mam ibusakinit sio ainyein akirot naka Edeke aijaanakin komesan .
44006003	Aso do , iinacan , koseutu ituŋa ikanykaarei kokidiŋikus , luijenete ebe ejokuka , luileleba Emoyo ka acoa , lukipedori adakakin oswam na .
44006004	Konye sio kinyikokini kotoma ailip ka aijaanakin naka akirot . ”
44006005	Kitojokai akirot na kokodet kere , koseut Sitepan etuŋanan loileleba aiyuun ka Emoyo Lokalaunan , ka Pilip , ka Porokoro , ka Nikanor , ka Timon , ka Pamena , ka Nikolao , ekebelokinon loko Antiokia .
44006006	Kibwaikis ŋul akonyen nuka ikiyakia , kosodete nakedauniata ailip , kidokokis kes akecekanin .
44006007	Konyanyaar akirot naka Edeke ; kiyatakin noi etiai loka ikesisiak ko Yerusalem , korimasi luipu lukosasedotin aiyuun ŋin .
44006008	Kilelebun Sitepan asianut ka apedor , kiswama nukaumokin nukos ka aanyuneta kotuŋa ,
44006009	Konye ice kotuŋa lukatukos naanyaritai atukos naka Luaosikinitai , ka luko Kurene , ka luko Alegesanderia , ice da lukoKilikia ka Asia , konyoutu kopegata ka Sitepan .
44006010	Konye mam apedorete abwoikin acoa ka Emoyo lokinerar .
44006011	Kosodete kicora ituŋa , lukebalas ebe , “ Kipou keirasi ŋol inera akiro nukainyanakin Musa ka Edeke . ”
44006012	Kisidiko ituŋa ka imakio ka ikewadikak , koponikis ŋes , kikamut , koyaŋaasi aurianet ,
44006013	kisibwaata ikajenak lukeŋalak luabalas ebe , “ Etuŋanan lo mam inyeinit einer akiro nuka asurokin aibois na nakalaunan ka ikisila da ;
44006014	naarai kipou keirasi ŋes inera ebe ebuni Yesu ŋol Enasarayot amudiar aibois na , ka ailocokin iponesio lukiinakini Musa oni . ”
44006015	Koŋanyakis ituŋa kere lukiboiete kaurianet ŋes akonyen , koanyut ekereet eputosi bala loka emalaika .
44007001	Kotema losasedoti lopeti atiar , “ Ikote kereka akiro ŋun nen ? ”
44007002	Kosodi Sitepan ebe , “ Iinacan ka lukapapa da , kiirarai . Abu Edeke loka aibuses kotakanik papaawok Aburaam , nakejaar Mesopotamia , eroko iboikino Karan ,
44007003	kotema ŋes atiar , ‘ Konyou kotoma akwapukon , ka ajenakon , kolot akwap naketodikini . ’
44007004	Kosodi konyou kakwap naka Ikaludean , kiboikin Karan . Ketwana papake kitonyou Edeke ŋes kanen kiton akwap na naiboito yesi kwana ;
44007005	kwabo mam keinakinit adioirumet , karaida nekicakakina akeju , konye kisumun ainakin ŋes airum , ka aurike naetupanakini , nakerokor ŋes ikoku emamei .
44007006	Kinera Edeke nuikote nen ebe eraun akeur apejonon kotoma akwap naka ituŋa ice , luitubulesenete kes , ikonakinete kes erono apak naka ikar akwat aoŋon .
44007007	Kobala Edeke ebe , ‘ Atubokini eoŋ ateker ŋin naitubulesene kes ; akaulo kaŋun elomunete , kamaete eoŋ kaibois kana . ’
44007008	Koinak ŋes aitutuket naka aikep . Kouri do Aburaam Isaak , kokep kapaaran nakikanyetekauni ; Isaak kouri Yakob , Yakob da kouri lukapapaawok lutomon ka luarei .
44007009	“ Koreata lukapapaawok Yosep , kogwelasi Misiri . Kojai Edeke nenipe kaŋes .
44007010	Kolem ŋes kotoma aiticanioke kere , koinak aminunio ka acoa kakonyen nuka Parao , ekabaka loko Misiri , kitarau ŋes ekayaiton loko Misiri kere , ka eketogo da kere .
44007011	Kosodi kojau ebeli akwap kere nako Misiri ka Kanaan da , ka aiticanio naepol , lukapapaawok da mam edumuna inyamat lukedaunito .
44007012	Konye nakiiraria Yakob ebe ejaas akima Misiri , kijuka lukapapaawok irwan nasodit .
44007013	Kiton alosit nakiareit kitejenikin Yosep ikeinacan , kojenun do ateker naka Yosep kama ka Parao .
44007014	Kijuka Yosep , konyarau Yakob papake , ka akejena kere , ituŋa akaisakanykaarei ka lukany .
44007015	Kijesar Yakob Misiri , Kotwana , ŋes ka lukapapaawok ;
44007016	koyaŋaarai kiton Sekem , kidaikinai toma ates ya nakegwelit Aburaam kotiai loka epuesa kama ejaas odwe luka Kamor koSekem .
44007017	“ Konye nakeapuunia apak naka aisumunet naabu Edeke koinak Aburaam , kipuaros ituŋa , kiyatakinos noi koMisiri ,
44007018	aitodol naanyounio ekabaka ece koMisiri , lomam ajeni Yosep .
44007019	Koŋopik ŋol atekerewok , kikonak lukapapaawok erono , kicorak acakanar ikecemukerun tetere mam ejarete .
44007020	Kouriai Musa kapak kaŋin , kerai ŋesi yenikejok noi kama ejai Edeke . Kosaai ilapio iuni kotogo loka papake ;
44007021	kiton neacakarere , kiraru akoku naka Parao , kitan ŋes kwape ikekoku .
44007022	Kituutooroi Musa kacoa kere nako Misiri , kogogoŋor kotoma akiro ka aswamisio da .
44007023	“ Kedolo ikekaru bala akaisaoŋon , kineru kotauke alosit aanyun ikeinacan idwe luka Isirael .
44007024	Koany ediopet ikonakinio erono , koyu ŋol lokereitai kinyaŋak kinom Emisiriat :
44007025	koomit ebe ejenunete iinacanake ebe ainak Edeke aitajario kakanike ; konye mam apotu kojenut .
44007026	Kapaaran naatupakini kitakanikin kes nakecelatar , kokoto aidiek kes , kobala ebe , ‘ Ikatuŋa , iraas yesi iinacan , kanukinyo ikonanakinotor erono ? ’
44007027	Konye lokikonakini onaceke erono koremo ŋes , kobala ebe , ‘ Iŋai bo kiidakakini jo araut ekayaiton ka ekatubon kamakosi ?
44007028	Ikoto kereka aiar eoŋ da , kwape bian iaria Emisiriat ? ’
44007029	Koker Musa kakirot kaŋin , korau epejonon kakwap nako Midian , kouru kaŋina idwe iarei .
44007030	“ Kosodi ketuboros ikar akaisaoŋon , kitakanikin emalaika loka Ejakait kotoma amodiŋ naka Emoru Sinai , kaipelonoreta nuka akim kotoma okiot .

44007033	Kotema Ejakait ŋes atiar , ‘ Kolaca amuk kakejenekon , naarai aibois naibwoia erai akwap nakalaunan .
44007034	Abeit aany aiticanio naka ikatuŋa luejaas Misiri , eira da eidinyikec , ejesun eoŋ ayuun kes . Aso kwana , kejukari jo Misiri . ’
44007035	“ Musa ŋol lokegirete kobalas ebe , ‘ Iŋai bo kiidakakini jo araut ekayaiton ka ekatubon da ? ’ ŋes kijukari Edeke araut ekayaiton ka ekayuunan kakan naka emalaika lokitakanikin kotoma okiot .
44007036	Ŋol ŋes kitolomuni kes , kedau aswam nukaumokin ka aanyuneta koMisiri ka Aŋolol Nakareŋan , kamodiŋ da apak naka ikar akaisaoŋon .
44007037	Ŋes Musa ŋol lokelimokini Isiraelin ebe , ‘ Kitonyoikini Edeke yes enabi kotoma oinacanakus kwape kaeoŋ . ’
44007038	Ŋol ŋol loajai okanisa toma amodiŋ nepepe ka emalaika Iokineras kaŋes kotoma Moru Sinai , ido kalukapapaawok ; ŋes lokedumuni akiro nuka aijar ainakin oni .

44007040	kolimokis Aaron ebe , ‘ Kosubakinai sio idekesio lukiŋarenikinete ; naarai mam kijeni nuadoikis Musa ŋol , lokiitolomuni kotoma akwap nako Misiri . ’
44007041	Kapaarasia kaŋun kosubut itaok , koinakis asuban mama ejai aput ŋin , kolelakis aswam naka akaninikec .
44007042	Konye kibelokin Edeke , kojalak tetere emaete ajore naka akuj ; kwape kiwadikatere oitabo loka inabin ebe , ‘ Ipotu kereka koinakis eoŋ itiaŋ luearitai ka asuban , Ŋo ekek loka Isirael , ikar akaisaoŋon kamodiŋ ?
44007043	Ipotu kodakasi ewema loka Molok , Ka aacerit naka edeke Repan , Aputosia nuiswamata tetere imaete : Ketwobosi yes koloto neelwana adepar Babulon . ’
44007044	“ Kejaas lukapapaawok ewema loka aitejenunet kamodiŋ , kwape kicorakinia lokineras ka Musa , aswam koriakas kaput nakeanyuni .
44007045	Apotu lukapapaawok , kabeikinikec kitolomut ŋes nepepe ka Yosua , nakebeata airumet naka atekerin , nuereŋear Edeke kakonyen nuka lukapapaawok , kiton apaarasia nuka Daudi ;
44007046	lokedumun asianut kakonyen nuka Edeke , kilip adumakin Edeke loka Yakob eyekalu .
44007047	Konye abu Solomon kodukok ŋes etogo .
44007048	Kwabo Loejai kuju kakuj mam iboie kotogoi luiswamao kakanin ; kwape inerar enabi ebe ,
44007049	‘ Akuj ŋes ekaicoloŋ , Ka akwapin da iicoloŋ yenika akakeje , Ebala Ejakait ebe , Etogo enyoin kidukokinete eoŋ ? Arai aibois anyoin naebworaria ?
44007050	Mere kereka akakan iswamat ŋun kere ? ’
44007051	“ Yes lueninik imurisiŋa , lumam ekepitai itauon ka aki , irebirebete tiritir Emoyo Lokalaunan . Kwape eswamaata lukapapaakus , yes da iswamaete kwape kwaŋin .
44007052	Enabi ali lomam lukapapaakus areito ? Apotu koarata lukedwarete akiro nuka abunore naka Ekadoliton ; lokwana ibilakis yesi ebotet , koarata da ,
44007053	yes luipotu kodumut ikisila kwape icorakinitotor imalaikan , komam iricito . ”
44007054	Kosodi nakiirariata akiro ŋun , konomos noi itauonokec , kiriamanakis ikel asurokinia ŋes .
44007055	Konye Sitepan kileleba Emoyo Lokalaunan , kosesen toma akuj , koany aibuses naka Edeke , ka Yesu da ebwoi kakan nakoteten naka Edeke ;
44007056	kotema atiar , “ Koany , aanyuni akuj eŋaara , ka Okoku loka etuŋanan ebwoi kakan nakoteten naka Edeke . ”
44007057	Konye koresiaros keporoto loepol , kisikakis akeceki , kosomakinos ketau ediopet .
44007058	Kireŋeasi kore , kibiribiroto kamor ; kibwaikis ikajenak ikecenapen akeje nuka ekatumunan loanyaritai Saul .
44007059	Kibiribiroto Sitepan kamor , kilip ŋesi ebe , “ Ejakait Yesu , kiira ekamoyo . ”
44007060	Kokukokin kiworo keporoto loepol ebe , “ Ejakait , sirikimarak kes aronis na . ” Kedau einer ŋun , kojotoor .
44008001	Kitojokit Saul da akeario . Kapaaran kaŋin kodakun aimanit naepol aluikin ekanisa lokejai Yerusalem ; kisiarakinos kere akwap nako Yudaya ka Samaria , dimarai ikiyakia .
44008002	Apotu ituŋa lueyoŋito Edeke kidaata Sitepan , kokuudianata da ŋes noi .
44008003	Konye komuna Saul ekanisa , kolomanari ŋolitogo , kidilidiliununei ikiliok ka aŋor da , kibwaik aidaris .
44008004	Kosodete ŋul lukisiarakinio koloto elimonokinete akirot .
44008005	Kijesar Pilip ore loko Samaria , kolimonok Kristo .
44008006	Kopupokis ikodeta kacoit ketau ediopet nukinera Pilip , naiirariata ka aanyun da aanyuneta nukiswamai .
44008007	Naarai apotu ajokin nuipu nueroko kolomut kama kaŋul lukikamunito , kiworoto keporoto loepol : luipu da lukasenyak ka iŋwalasik kitaŋaleunoi .
44008008	Kojau aiyalama naepol ore ŋol .
44008009	Konye kojai etuŋanan ekekiror Simon , lolem eswamaenenei nukecudet kore kaŋol , kisiwumok ituŋa luko Samaria , kobala ebe ŋes lokapolon .
44008010	Kopupokito kesi kere kacoit , ameun ka yenididi kiton yenikapolon kobalas ebe , “ Etuŋanan lo erai apedor naka Edeke naenyaritai Nakapolon . ”

44008012	Konye nakiyuuniata Pilip elimonokin akiro nukajokak nuka ajakanut naka Edeke , ka ekiror da loka Yesu Kristo , kibatisai , ikiliok ka aŋor da .
44008013	Simon da elopet abu kiyu ; kedau aibatisao koupakinos ka Pilip . Koumok nakeanyunia aanyuneta ka nukapedor nukapolok nukiswamai Pilip .
44008014	Kosodete nakiirariata ikiyakia lukejaas Yerusalem ebe eyuu Samaria akirot naka Edeke , kiyakiasi Petero ka Yokana mama ejaas ,
44008015	lukijesaros kilipakis kes , tetere edumunete Emoyo Lokalaunan :
44008016	naarai mam ber kedoikinit idio kakesi , konye ebatisatai ber kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu .
44008017	Kosodete kidokokis kes akecekanin , kodumut do Emoyo Lokalaunan ,
44008018	Konye nakeanyunia Simon ebe einakinio Emoyo Lokalaunan kanuka aidokokin akanin nuka ikiyakia , kokoto ainakin kes arupian ,
44008019	kobala ebe , “ Koinakinai eoŋ da apedor na , tetere ŋinituŋanan yenedokokini akakanin kodumun Emoyo Lokalaunan . ”
44008020	Konye kotema Petero atiar , “ Koolio epuesakon nepepe kajo ; naarai iwomit ebe idumuni ainakinet naka Edeke kanuka arupian .
44008021	Emamei jo akorakinet karaida ewai kotoma akirot kana ; naarai mam itenara ekonitau kakonyen nuka Edeke .
44008022	Aso kitoronikin aronisikon na , kilip Ejakait , elemuni kisionii aomisioit na naketaukon .
44008023	Naarai kaanyu jo ileleba adwaris kwape kepiu , ido da kienit elomorut loka amamus adolit . ”
44008024	Koboŋok Simon ebe , “ Kilipakinai yesi eoŋ kama ejai Ejakait , kenyeis akiro ŋun nuinerata adolokin eoŋ . ”
44008025	Kosodi nakedauniata aitejenun ka alimonokin akirot naka Ejakait , koboŋos ! Yerusalem , elimonokinete Akiro Nukajokak oreria luipu luka Isamarian .
44008026	Konye kinerata emalaika loka Ejakait ka Pilip , kotema atiar , “ Konyou kobe ari naka eŋalakimak kiton orot loijesar anyoun ko Yerusalem alosit Gasa . ” Ŋes amodiŋ .
44008027	Konyou kolot . Ido koany , etuŋanan loko Etiopia , ebwacit , ejakait loka Kadake akabaka naka Etiopia , loapolokinit abarake kere , kelosit ŋesi Yerusalem aima ;
44008028	eboŋuni ŋesi iboie kagalike , esiomi eitabo loka enabi Isaia .

44008030	Aso koker Pilip mama ejai , kiira ŋes esiomi eitabo loka enabi Isaia , kiŋit ebe , “ Ijeni kereka ijo ŋun nuisiomi ? ”
44008031	Kobala ebe , “ Ekonakini ai ajenuni , arai mam keŋarenikinit ituŋanan ? ” Kiŋaiŋa ŋesi Pilip adokar aiboikin kaŋes .
44008032	Ewai loka nukiwadikatai lokisiomi ŋesi ŋes lota ebe : “ Koyaŋaarai aario kwape kamerekek ; Ido kwape ililiŋia ikoku yenika amerekek kama kekatubon ajul , Kwape kwaŋin mam ŋes eoŋari akeituk ;
44008033	Kaitisilioke aponi kolemarai aketubokinio ; Iŋai bo epedori aitejenikin aketur ? Naarai alemar akeijar kakwap . ”
44008034	Kotema ebwacit Pilip atiar , “ Keŋaiŋait , kinera enabi akiro ŋun kanuka ŋai ? Eraas kereka akekiro , arai bo nuka ece ? ”
44008035	Kooŋ Pilip akeituk , kogeu kanakiwadikatai kaŋin kolimok ŋes akiro nukajokak nuka Yesu .
44008036	Napelosete korot , kodoloto neajaas akip ; kotema ebwacit atiar , “ Koany , akipi nu ; inyo ca kesimikit eoŋ aibatisao ? ” [

44008040	Konye kotakanu Pilip kotoma Asoto , nakitoritor kolimonok akiro nukajokak koreria kere , kiton adolore Kaisarea .
44009001	Konye Saul , kiyatakinite nukaitukurian ka nukaiar ikesisiak luka Ejakait , kolot mama ejai losasedoti lopeti ,

44009006	Konye konyou , koloma ore , kilimokinio nuibusakinit aswam . ”

44009016	naarai etodikini ŋes nuipu nuibusakinit ŋes aiticanio kanuka ekakiror . ”

44009043	Kosodi kosalak Petero Yopa apaarasia nuipu togo loka etuŋanan ekekiror Simon , ekekisikisan imukulen .
44010001	Kojai etuŋanan koKaisarea ekekiror Korunelio , ekapolokiton loka erioŋet loenyaritai Italian ,
44010002	etuŋanan loeyoŋit Edeke , nepepe ka lukokaleke kere , lokekorenenei nukaitim nuipu otuŋa , ka ailipenen da Edeke tir .

44010006	Ipejokinit ŋesi Simon , ekekisikisan imukulen , loejai eketogo ariri kaŋolol . ”

44010018	Konyarata kiŋita arai ipejot Simon loenyaritai Petero nen .
44010019	Napeomoomoi Petero aitapoet , kotema Emoyo ŋes atiar , “ Koany , ejaas ituŋa iuni lukimooto jo .
44010020	Aso konyou , kijesar kwap , koupakinos kakes komam ibuonokin ; naarai eoŋ ejukunit kes . ”
44010021	Kijesun Petero mama ejaas ituŋa , kobala ebe , “ Eoŋ lo lokimooto ; iponitos kanuka akiro anyoika ? ”
44010022	Kotemasi atiar , “ Korunelio , ekapolokiton , etuŋanan loedolit Ioeyoŋit Edeke , loitojokitai kotoma ateker kere naka Iyudayan , abu emalaika lokalaunan kikwenya ŋes anyaraun jo alosit togoke , tetere iirari akiro kamakon . ”
44010023	Kisukunyik kes araut ikepejok . Kapaaran naatupakini konyou kolot kakes , koupakinos da ice koinacan luko Yopa kaŋes .
44010024	Kapaaran naatupakini kolomasi Kaisarea . Kidaret kes Korunelio , kotukokinite lukajenake ka ikepadic da .
44010025	Napelomari Petero , kisiriam Korunelio ŋes , kibirokin akejeke , koma ŋes .
44010026	Konye Petero kitonyou ŋes , kobala ebe , “ Kobwo ; arai eoŋ da etuŋanan . ”
44010027	Napinera , koloma kodum ituŋa luipu etukokina ;
44010028	kotema kes atiar , “ Ijenete yesi ikulepek kwape eraar naketal Eyudayat aimorikikina arai aipejokin etuŋanan kere loka ateker ace ; konye abu Edeke ketodik eoŋ ebe mam ebusakinit anyara idiotuŋanan yeniketal arai yenimam elai .
44010029	Kanuka ŋun nakanyaraunere , abu komam aŋeri , Aso keŋisit anyoin akirot nakinyaritotor eoŋ . ”
44010030	Kotema Korunelio atiar , “ Eraas apaarasia aoŋon atuboros , kwape esawa lo , abu karicite esawa lokikanyetekaoŋon loka ailip kotogoka ; ido koany , kobwo etuŋanan kakonyeneka enapit luimiliasi ,
44010031	kabala ebe , ‘ Korunelio , eirar akoniilip , akoniikor da eitun kakonyen nuka Edeke .
44010032	Aso kiyakia ituŋa Yopa , konyarau Simon loenyaritai Petero ; ipejokinit ŋesi togo loka Simon , ekekisikisan imukulen , kariri naka aŋolol . ’
44010033	Aso abu kanyarau jo atipet , iswama ejok abunore . Aso kwana kija ne kere akonyen nuka Edeke , keirasi kere nukicorakinit Ejakait jo . ”
44010034	Kosodi kooŋ Petero akeituk , kotema atiar , “ Abeit ajenu ebe mam Edeke etiakatiakai ituŋa ,
44010035	konye kotoma ŋiniteker yeneyoŋit , kiswama da nuedolito , ecamuni ŋesi .
44010036	Akirot nakijukakini idwe luka Isirael , elimonokini akiro nukajokak nuka ainapakin kotoma Yesu Kristo , ( ŋes Ejakait loka kere , )
44010037	ijenete yesi akirot naalimoritai anatar Yudaya kere , ageun koGalilaya , akaulo ka aibatisa naalimonokini Yokana ;
44010038	Kwape kinyonyoikinia Edeke Yesu loko Nasaret akinyet naka Emoyo Lokalaunan ka apedor ; lokelosenenei iswamai nuejok , itaŋaleununei kere lukiticani Satan , naarai kejai Edeke nenipe kaŋes .
44010039	Kirai isio ikajenak luka akiro kere nukiswamai ŋesi kakwap naka Iyudayan , koYerusalem da ; koarata ŋol kaikajakin okitoi .

44010041	mere kotuŋa kere , konye mamakosi luabu Edeke koseu sek araut ikajenak , lukinyami ka aimat da nepepe kaŋes kedau ajarun kokatwak .
44010042	Kicorak sio kalimonokis ituŋa , ka aitejenun da ebe ŋol ŋes lekedakakini Edeke araut ekatubon loka ikajarak ka ikatwak da .
44010043	Ŋol ŋes itejenunitos inabin kere ebe kanuka ekekiror ŋinituŋanan yeniyuuni ŋes edumuni aisionio naka adiakanareta . ”
44010044	Naperiŋa Petero inera ŋun , kodoik Emoyo Lokalaunan kere lukiirarete akirot .
44010045	Koumokis lukiyuunito lukekepitai lukeupunos ka Petero , naarai abukokin Imo da ainakinet naka Emoyo Lokalaunan .
44010046	Naarai kiirasi kes ineras kaŋajepa ka aitopoloor Edeke . Kosodi Koboŋok Petero ebe ,
44010047	“ Epedori kereka ituŋanan aisimik akipi nuka aibatis ituŋa lu , luainakin Emoyo Lokalaunan kwape kaoni ? ”
44010048	Kicorak kes aibatisao kokiror loka Yesu Kristo . Kosodete kilipata ŋes asalakin apaarasia nuipupuuto .
44011001	Kosodete kiirasi ikiyakia ka iinacan luajaas Yudaya ebe eyuut Imo da akirot naka Edeke .
44011002	Kosodi nakedolunio Petero Yerusalem , ko pegata lukekepitai nepepe kaŋes ,
44011003	kobalas ebe , “ Ibu kolot otuŋa lumam ekepitai , komorata kakes . ”
44011004	Konye kogeu Petero aitejenun kaisudunyit , kotema atiar ,
44011005	“ Abu kajai ore loka Yopa elipi ; kogelakin ekamoyo kaany aitapoet , ijesun ibore , bala aisuka naepol , ijoliliunio kokuju kowaitin iwoŋon ; kadolok .
44011006	Kerere , kaŋic , ido kaany itiaŋ luka akwap , ka itiaŋ luededeŋ , ka lueliatos , ka akweny nuka apak .
44011007	Keira eporoto ebala ebe , ‘ Petero , konyou ; koar , konyam . ’
44011008	Konye katema atiar , ‘ Mam cut , Ejakait ; naarai ibore yenerai yeniketal karaida yenimam elai mam elomarit cut aitukuka . ’
44011009	Konye Koboŋok eporoto irwan nakiareit ebuni kokuju ebe , ‘ Lukitalauni Edeke mam ibusakinit jo anyarit luketal . ’
44011010	Kiswama akirot na irwan auni , kosodi kiriarai bobo kere toma akuj .
44011011	Atipet ŋipeŋin , kobwaata ituŋa iuni koiŋaren ketogo lokija , lukiyakuunio mama ajai koKaisarea .
44011012	Kalimok Emoyo aupar kakes komam abuonokin . Koloto iinacan lu ikanykape nepepe keoŋ , kalomasi togo loka etuŋanan kaje .
44011013	Kitejenik epone lokeanyunia emalaika lokebwoi kotogoke ka atemar ebe , ‘ Kiyakia ituŋa Yopa , konyarau Simon loenyaritai Petero ;
44011014	lokilimokini akiro nukitaiarete , ijo ka lukokalekon kere . ’
44011015	Konye napageari einer , kodoik kes Emoyo Lokalaunan kwape kiidoikinio oni kageunet .
44011016	Keitu do akirot naka Ejakait , kwape kinerar ebe , ‘ Abu Yokana kibatis kakip , konye yes kibatisao kEmoyo Lokalaunan . ’
44011017	Aso arai ainaki Edeke kes ainakinet ŋin nakiinakinit oni nakiyuunia Ejakait Yesu Kristo , eoŋ bo iŋai lotiapedori airebokin Edeke ? ”
44011018	Nakiirariata akirot ŋin kililiŋata . Kitopoloosi Edeke , kobalas ebe , “ Ainak Edeke kiton Imo da aitoronikin naeyauni aijar . ”
44011019	Kosodete lukisiarakinos kanuka aimanit nakedoikini kanuka akiro nuka Sitepan , koloto kiton Poenike ka Kupuro ka Antiokia , komam elimonokinete akirot dimarai oYudayan bon ,
44011020	Konye ice kaŋul luko Kupuro ka Kurene , nakedolioto Antiokia , kinerata ka Iyonanin da elimonokinete akiro nukajokak nuka Ejakait Yesu .
44011021	Kojai akan naka Ejakait nenipe kakes , kiyuut ituŋa luipu kibelokinos neejai Ejakait .
44011022	Kodol eemut loka ituŋa kaŋul aki nuka ekanisa lokejai toma Yerusalem , kiyakiasi Baranaba Antiokia .
44011023	Nakedolio koany da asianut naka Edeke , kiyalamikin ; kicor kes kere aikokoikin aimorikikina ka Ejakait kikecetauon kere ;
44011024	naarai kerai etuŋanan loejok , loeleleba Emoyo Lokalaunan ka aiyuun . Kiyatakinos ituŋa luipu mama ejai Ejakait .
44011025	Kosodi kolot Baranaba Taruso amoot Saul .
44011026	Nakedumunia koyau ŋes Antiokia . Kosodi kanen kotukonokinos nenipe kekanisa adaun ekaru kere , kisisianakis ituŋa luipu ; ido kotoma Antiokia Ŋes ageunere amaikin ikesisiak Ikristayon .
44011027	Kapaarasia kaŋun kijesaros inabin anyoun koYerusalem kiton Antiokia .
44011028	Kobwo ediopet kakesi ekekiror Agabo , kodwar kanuka Emoyo ebe , ebuni ebeli loepol anatar akwapin kere ; kojau da kapaarasia nuka Kulaudia .
44011029	Kinerut ikesisiak , ŋinituŋanan kwape epedoria , aijukakin iinacan lueboiete ko Yudaya iboro luiŋarakinete ;
44011030	Kiswamata kwaŋin , kijukakis imakio kakanin nuka Baranaba ka Saul .
44012001	Kapak kaŋin korio Kerode ekabaka akekanin aikonakin erono ice lukokanisa .
44012002	Koar Yakob onace loka Yokana kekileŋ ;
44012003	nakeanyunia ebe itojokito Iyudayan , kiyatak aikamun Petero da . Keraas apaarasia ŋun nuka Imugatin lumam itubuunitoi .
44012004	Nakedaunia aikamun , kogolok aidaris , kibwaik akanin nuka irioŋeta iwoŋon luka iserikalei iwoŋon iwoŋon , tetere idarete ; kokoto aitolomun ŋes neejaas ituŋa kedaun Aleleŋ .
44012005	Aso kidarai Petero kaidaris ; konye kinyikokis noi lukokanisa ailip Edeke kanukeŋ .
44012006	Kakuar kaŋin naakotor Kerode aitolomun ŋes , kojotoi Petero kokidiŋ kiserikalei iarei , eenitai kirikoi iarei , kojaas ikedarak okek idarete aidaris ;
44012007	ido koany , kobwo emalaika loka Ejakait aapu kaŋes , kocau aica kagola ; kinom Petero osiep kitwekeny , kobala ebe , “ Konyou atipet . ” Kodooto irikoi kakaninike .
44012008	Kotema emalaika ŋes atiar , “ Konap , kirupak da akonimuk . ” Kiswama kwaŋin , Kotema ŋes atiar , “ Kimukok ekonilou , kotupunai . ”
44012009	Koloma kotup ŋes ; mam abu kojen ebe nueswamai emalaika eraas nukabeit , konye aomit ŋesi ebe aanyu aitapoet .
44012010	Naketuborotor kaidaret nasodit ka nakiareit , kodoloto okek lokasua lolomaret kiŋa toma ore ; koŋaari bon , kolomasi kiŋa kitoroto orot ediopet ; atipet kinye ŋes emalaika .
44012011	Kosodi nakejenunia kotema atiar , “ Kwana ajeni abeit ebe ejuku Ejakait ekemalaika alemun eoŋ kakan naka Kerode ka kere nuemuno ateker naka Iyudayan . ”
44012012	Nakedaunia aomoom ŋun , kolot togo loka Mariam , toto naka Yokana ŋol loerai ekekiror lokiareit Marako ; ketukokina ituŋa luipu nen , ilipete .
44012013	Nakikuŋukuŋio ekek loka erute , kobu apese ekekiror Roda ajaar .
44012014	Nakejenunia eporoto loka Petero , mam eŋaara ekek kanuka aiyalama , konye koker koloma toma , kobala ebe , “ Ebwoi Petero kokek . ”
44012015	Kotemasi ŋes atiar , “ Kikerepiki ca ijo . ” Konye kitogogoŋ noi ebe ikote nen . Kotemasi atiar , “ Erai ekemalaika . ”
44012016	Konye kiyatak Petero aikuŋukuŋ ; kiton neaŋaariata , koanyutu ŋes , koumokis .
44012017	Konye kisililiŋ kes kakekan , kitatamik kes kwape kelemunia ŋes Ejakait kotoma aidaris . Kotema atiar , “ Kolimokis Yakob ka iinacan da akiro ŋun . ” Kosodi konyou kolot aibois ace .
44012018	Nakiwalaria akwap , kobur iserikalei kanuadoikis Petero ,
44012019	Nakemoia Kerode komam edumuni , kiŋitiŋit ikedarak , kicorak aario . Kosodi kijesar anyoun koYudaya alosit Kaisarea , kosalak nen .
44012020	Konyunyurik Kerode ituŋa luko Turo ka Sidon , kolosikis Ŋes ketau ediopet , ido kedaut aipaperikin ka Bulasito , lokedaran agola naperot naka ekabaka , kilipa ainapakin , naarai kedumunit akwapukec inyamat kakwap naka ekabaka .
44012021	Kapaaran naaseunitai konap Kerode ikenapen luka ekabakane , kiboikin oicoloŋ loka ekabakane , kiner akiro kamakec .
44012022	Kocelut ituŋa kobalas ebe , “ Ŋes eporoto loka edeke , mere loka etuŋanan ! ”
44012023	Atipet kinom emalaika loka Ejakait , naarai mam kitubusikinit Edeke ; konyamata ŋes ikur , kotwana .
44012024	Konye kiyatakin akirot naka Ejakait , konyanyaar .
44012025	Koboŋosi Baranaba ka Saul koYerusalem , kedaut aijaanakinikec , kouparos Yokana loenyaritai Marako kakes .
44013001	Ko Antiokia , kokanisa lokejai kanen kojaas inabin ka ikesisianakinak , kes Baranaba , ka Simeon loenyaritai Niger , ka Lukio loko Kurene , ka Manaen Lokitanakio nepepe ka Kerode ekabaka , ka Saul da .
44013002	Kosodi napijaanakinete Ejakait , ka ailuŋ , kotema Emoyo Lokalaunan atiar , “ Kogitakinai Baranaba ka Saul kanuka aswam naanyarakinit kes . ”
44013003	Kosodi kedaut ailuŋ ka ailip , kidokokis kes akecekanin kotwarata .
44013004	Kosodi kijuka Emoyo Lokalaunan kijesaros Seleukia ; kenyoutu kanen kikwaŋaros kiton Kupuro .
44013005	Nakedolioto Salamis , kolimonokis akirot naka Edeke katukosia nuka Iyudayan . Kojaas ka Yokana ijaanakini kes .
44013006	Nakedauniata aitor apujan kere kiton Papo , kodumut ekacudan , enabi lokeŋalan , Eyudayat , ekekiror Bar-Yesu ;
44013007	kejaas etuŋanan ŋol nepepe ka ekayaiton , Serugio Paul , etuŋanan loka acoa . Konyara ekayaiton Baranaba ka Saul , kokoto aiirar akirot naka Edeke .
44013008	Konye Elumayo ekacudan ( ŋes apolou naka ekekiror ) kopegata kakes , kokoto aitapaar ekayaiton ainyein aiyuun .

44013010	kobala ebe , “ Ijo loileleba aimod ka aronis kere , ijo okoku loka Satan , lokasurup loka adolit kere , mam kereka inyeini aitapaar irotin luitenara luka Ejakait ?
44013011	Kwana da , koany , ejai akan naka Ejakait mamakon , imudukanar ijo , komam ianyuni akoloŋ adaun apak . ” Atipet kodoik ŋes elisina ka amuton , koturiaitoi ka amoot luerikete kakan .
44013012	Kosodi kiyu ekayaiton , nakeanyunia nukiswamao , naarai koumok aisisianakin naka Ejakait .
44013013	Kosodete kikwaŋaros Paul ka ikepaup anyoun koPapo , kodoloto Peruga toma Pampulia . Kinye kes Yokana kanen koboŋo Yerusalem .
44013014	Konye kes , konyout koPeruga kitoroto akwap kodoloto Antiokia ere loka Pisidia . Kolomas atukos kapaaran nakasabato , kiboikinos .
44013015	Kedaut asoman ikisila ka inabin , kiyakiasi ikayaitok luka atukos mamakec ebe , “ Iinacan , arai ijaas kakirot nakaicor ituŋa , kolimut . ”
44013016	Kobwo Paul kokwet kakan kobala ebe , “ Ikiliok luka Isirael , ka yes da luiyoŋito Edeke , kiirasi .
44013017	Edeke loka ituŋa kalu luka Isirael abu koseu lukapapaawok , kitopoloo ituŋa nakiboiororoto kakwap nako Misiri , kitolom kakan naerioro .
44013018	Apak bala naka ikar akaisaoŋon kotitiŋik kes kamodiŋ .
44013019	Nakedaunia amudiar atekerin akanykaarei kotoma akwap nako Kanaan , koinak kes akecekwap araut airumet , apak naka ikar bala akwat aoŋon ka akaisakany .
44013020	Akaulo kaŋun koinak kes ikatubok kiton Samuel enabi .
44013021	Kosodete kilipa ekabaka ; koinak Edeke Saul okoku loka Kis , lokateker naka Benyamin , apak naka ikar akaisaoŋon .
44013022	Nakelemaria ŋol , kodakak Daudi araut ekabakakec ; lokitejenuni ŋesi ebe , ‘ Adum Daudi okoku loka Yese etuŋanan loitalakarit ekatau , loebuni aswam nuakoto eoŋ kere . ’
44013023	Kotoma aur naka etuŋanan kaŋol ainu Edeke Isirael Eketajaran , ŋes Yesu , kwape esumunitor .
44013024	Eriŋa ŋesi ebuno abu Yokana koliŋak alimonokin ituŋa kere luka Isirael aibatis naka aitoronikin .
44013025	Napedauni Yokana akelosit , kobala ebe , ‘ Kiwomito eoŋ araut iŋai ? Mam arai ŋol . Konye koany , ebunit kokaukaŋ lomam kebusakinit eoŋ alacar amuk nuka akejeke . ’
44013026	“ Iinacan , idwe luka aur naka Aburaam , ka luiyoŋito Edeke da kotomakus , ejukun akirot naka aitajario mamawok .
44013027	Naarai luiboiete koYerusalem , ka ikayaitokokec , kanu mam ajenuniata ŋes , karaida akiro nuka inabin nuesiomenenoo ŋinisabato , etodolikis kanuka atubokin ŋes .
44013028	Karaida mam eanyunitos akirot naibusakinitor atwanare , konye kilipata Pilato koarai .
44013029	Nakedauniata aitodolikin kere nukiwadikatai kanukeŋ , kijesut kokitoi , kibwaikis ates .
44013030	Konye kitajaru ŋes Edeke kokatwak .
44013031	Apaarasia nuipu kitakanikin ŋul lukedokarete nepepe kaŋes anyoun koGalilaya kiton Yerusalem , lueraas kwana ikajenakake mama ejaas ituŋa .
44013032	Kiinunit isio yes akiro nukajokak nuka aisumunet nakeinakinio lukapapaawok ,
44013033	ebe etodolik Edeke oni ikecedwe aisumunet ŋin , kanuka aitajarun Yesu ; kwape iwadikatere kotoma osabuli lokiareit ebe , ‘ Irai ijo Okokuka , Lolo kawuru jo . ’
44013034	Ido kanuka akirot kaŋin ebe etajaru ŋes kokatwak , kinye bobo aboŋor aibos , inera kwanata ebe , ‘ Kainakini yes arereŋesio nukalaunak ka nuicasito nuka Daudi . ’
44013035	Kanuka ŋun inera kosabuli ece ebe , ‘ Mam icamuni Ekalaunanikon aibos . ’
44013036	Naarai Daudi , kedau aijaanakin ainerun naka Edeke katurike , abu kojotoor , kibwaikinai nepepe ka lukapapaake , kobos ;
44013037	konye ŋol lokitajaruni Edeke mam abu kobos .
44013038	Aso do iinacan , kojenutu ebe , kotoma otuŋanan kaŋol elimonokinio yes aisionio naka adiakanareta ;
44013039	ido kotomakeŋ ŋin yeniyuuni imarakinio adolit kakiro kere , numam epedorere aimarakin adolit kokisila luka Musa .
44013040	Aso kocoito , kinye akirot adoikin yes , nainerito inabin ebe :
44013041	‘ Koanyutu , yes ikamenak , koumokis , kooliosi ; Naarai eswamai eoŋ aswam kapaarasiakus , Aswam namam iyuunete cut , karaida kiilimonok ituŋanan yes . ’ ”
44013042	Napelomarete , kiŋaiŋaata alimokin akiro ŋun kasabato naatupakini .
44013043	Nakisiarakinor atukokin naka atukos , apotu Iyudayan luipu ka ikebelokinok lueyoŋito Edeke kotupasi Paul ka Baranaba , lukinerasi kakes , kisicerededata aiyatakin kotoma asianut naka Edeke .
44013044	Kosodi kasabato naatupakini kotukokinos ituŋa luipu , aapie ere kere , aiirar akirot naka Edeke .
44013045	Konye nakeanyuniata Iyudayan ikodeta , kilelebun ekolo , kitepega nuenera Paul , komoromoroto da .
44013046	Kinerata Paul ka Baranaba katitiŋikin ebe , “ Ibusakinit akirot naka Edeke ainerio ber kamakus . Konye naarai igaguarete kamakus , itubokinos bonik araut lumam ibusakinito aijar namam edaun , koany , kibelokin do mama ejaas Imo .
44013047	Naarai abu Ejakait kicorak sio kwaŋin ebe , ‘ Kebwaik jo araut aica naka Imo , Tetere iyauni aitajario kiton osaŋeta luka akwapin . ’ ”
44013048	Nakiirariata Imo ŋun , kiyalamikinos , kitopoloos akirot naka Ejakait ; ŋul da lukelosikinito aijar namam edaun kiyuut do .
44013049	Kisiarakin akirot naka Ejakait akwap ŋin kere .
44013050	Konye kicecemoto Iyudayan aŋor nueyoŋito nukapolou ka ikeŋarenikinok luka ere , kisidikoto aimanit Paul ka Baranaba , kireŋeasi koikorunokec .
44013051	Konye kilakilakata adai nuka akejekec , koloto Ikonium .
44013052	Kilelebunos ikesisiak aiyalama ka Emoyo Lokalaunan .
44014001	Kosodi kanen kotoma Ikonium , kolomasi nepepe toma atukos naka Iyudayan , ido kanuka ŋun nuenerasi kiyu ekodet loapol loka Iyudayan ka Iyonanin .
44014002	Konye Iyudayan lumam kiyuunito kisidikoto Imo kitolomikis etau loerono asurokin iinacan .
44014003	Kosodete kosala nen apak naepol , inerasi katitiŋ kotoma Ejakait , lokitejenuni akirot naka akesianut , kocamak aanyuneta ka nukaumokin aiswamao kakaninikec ,
44014004	Konye kotiakas ituŋa lukore ; ice owai loka lyudayan , ice da owai loka ikiyakia .
44014005	Kiton neatakanunia asurokin naka Imo ka Iyudayan , nepepe kikayaitokokec , aiswamakin kes erono , ka aibiribir kamor .
44014006	Kejenut kes ŋun , kokereasi Lusitura ka Derube , ireria luka Lukaonia , ka akwapin nuedunyatar ;
44014007	kanen da kolimonokis akiro nukajokak .
44014008	Kanen koLusitura kojai etuŋanan iboie , ilejekekas akekeje , eŋwalas ameun kakoik naka totoke , lomam alosi cut .

44018015	konye arai erai akirot naka aiŋiseta nuka akiro ka ikiroria ka ikisilakus , nukus bo ŋun ; mam eoŋ akoto araut ekatubon kaŋun . ”
44018016	Kireŋea kes kairabis .

44019001	Nakejaar Apolo Korinto , kitor Paul akwap naimukurur , kodol Epeso . Kodum ikesisiak ice kaŋina .
44019002	Kiŋit kes atiar , “ Ipotu kereka ko dumut Emoyo Lokalaunan nakiyuuniata ? ” Kobalas ebe , “ Mam , karaida aiirarit ebe ejai Emoyo Lokalaunan . ”

44019020	Kwaŋin kopoloor akirot naka Ejakait , kitelekarit kagogoŋ .
44019021	Kedaunos akiro ŋun kolosik Paul Komoyo aitor Makedonia ka Akaia alosit Yerusalem , kobala ebe , “ Kadau ajaut ŋina , kebusakinit aanyun Rome da . ”

44019023	Kapak kaŋin kodakun aigurun namere naedit kanuka Erot .
44019024	Naarai etuŋanan ekekiror Demeterio ekatatan epuesa , lokesubenenei abilai nuka epuesa nuka Aratemi , lokedumanakini ikeswamak luepiriaka ameda naepol ;

44019033	Kolemut Alegesanda kotoma okodet , lokisibwoete Iyudayan kakonyen nuka ituŋa . Kokwetu Alegesanda kakanike , kokoto apurokin kakonyen nuka ituŋa .
44019034	Konye nakejenuniata ebe erai ŋesi Eyudayat , kiworoto kere keporoto ediopet bala apak naka isawan iarei ebe , “ Aratemi naka Ipeson ŋes nakapolon ! ”
44019035	Nakedaunia ekewadikan loka ere aisiyamikin ekodet , kobala ebe , “ Okwe ikatuŋa luko Epeso , iŋai bo ituŋanan yenimam ejeni ebe , erai ere loka Epeso ekedaran loka eyekalu loka Aratemi nakapolon , ka loka aput nakedouni kokuju ?

44019041	Kedau einer ŋun kotwar atukot .

44021022	Aso ikwaikinio bo do ai ? Abeit epupunete ebe ibu ijo .

44026026	Naarai ejeni ekabaka nuka akiro kaŋun , eoŋ da enera kaŋes katitiŋ ; naarai etogogoŋit ebe emamei akirot kotoma kaŋun naimunonikinitai ŋes , naarai mam nu eswamas kagor .
44026027	Ekabaka Agiripa , iyuunit tope ijo inabin ? Ajeni ebe iyuunit . ”
44026028	Kotema Agiripa Paul atiar , “ Kanaesupaana ikoto aituluor eoŋ da Ekristayot ! ”
44026029	Koboŋok Paul ebe , “ Arai kanaesupaana , arai kanaepol elipi Edeke mere ijo bon , konye kaŋul da kere lukapupete lolo , koraut kwape keoŋ-dimarai aeneta nu . ”
44026030	Kosodi kobwo ekabaka , ka ekayaiton ka Berenike , ka ŋul lukiboiete kakes ;
44026031	napenyounete , kineranakinos ebe , “ Mam etuŋanan lo iswamat akirot naibusakinitor atwanare karaida aenio . ”

44027001	Kosodi nakicorakinere sio aikwaŋar kiton Italia , kijaikis Paul ka ienan ice mama ejai ekapolokiton erioŋet loka Augusito , ekekiror Yulio .
44027002	Kadokas ataker naka Aduramutio , nakekapakina alosit kiton oreria luka oitolima luka Asia , kekwaŋasi , kauparos ka Arisitariko Emakedoniat loko Sesalonika .
44027003	Apaaran naatupakini kadolo Sidon ; kikonak Yulio Paul asianut , kocamak ŋes alosit mama ejaas ipaperoke tetere imukeo .
44027004	Kanyoutu kanen kekwaŋaros kediata keririto Kupuro , naarai kemeunito ikwamin kakonyen .
44027005	Ketoro aŋolol naka Kilikia ka Pampulia , kadolo Mura nako Lukia .
44027006	Kanen kodum ekapolokiton ataker naka Alegesanderia idiai Italia , kadokikis ŋin ,
44027007	Kekwaŋaros motimot apaarasia nuipu , kadolo Kinido kationis , ido naarai kitikokinit ekwam , keririata Kurete katereikina Salumone ,
44027008	Ketoroto kationis aapu koitolima , kadolo aibois naenyaritai Odoketa Lukajokak naidunyas ka ere Lasea .
44027009	Kiilonya apaarasia , kojau aronis alosit naarai atuboros apaarasia nuka Ailuŋ , kidelu Paul ,
44027010	kobala kes ebe , “ Lukipa , aanyunit eoŋ ebe ejaun amunaar ka atwaniar alosit na , mere iboro bon ka ataker , konye aijarawok da . ”
44027011	Konye abu ekapolokiton kopupok ekekwaŋan lokapolon ka elopet ataker aitelekarit ŋun nuenera Paul .
44027012	Ido da mam ebusakinit edoket ŋol aiboio apak naka aaterot , kidelut luipu kakesi aikwaŋar anyoun kanen , tetere elemuni edolete Poenike , edoket loka Kurete , loetereikina agolitome nakokide , ka egalakimak nakokide , kasala nen kapak naka aaterot .
44027013	Kosodi napekusi ekwam lokeŋalakimak kiyamakina , koomitos ebe adumutu nukekotos , kibwosut edobo lokitapaikinet , kikwaŋaros aapu koitolima loka Kurete .
44027014	Ketubor apak naedit kokut ekwam lokagogoŋ , loenyaritai Eurakulon ebuni kaneonit ,
44027015	Kokutar ataker , mam epedoro atereikina ekwam , kajalakisi kikutario ,
44027016	Kanen ketoro atipet ariri naka apujan naedit naenyaritai Kulauda , kekurautu ajen itaker .
44027017	Kekiasi ŋes , kitwasamata aisigalikineta , koenikis kwap ataker ; ido naarai kokuriaka aipok koSuritis , kijoliliosi iboro , kwaŋin kokutarai .
44027018	Naarai kiiliilit ekwam , apaaran naatupakini kogeut acakar iboro aŋolol ;
44027019	apaaran nakiwuniet da kocakanasi kakaninikec ikulepek iboro luka ataker .
44027020	Mam atakani akoloŋ karaida aacer apaarasia nuipu , kokuta sio ekwam loededeŋ , kokau kodaun amun kere naka aitajario .
44027021	Nakiboioto apak naapol mam enyamete , kosodi kobwo Paul kokidiŋikec , kotema atiar , “ Lukipa , ti ebusakinit yes aiirar eoŋ , amamus aikwaŋar anyoun koKurete , adumun amunaar ka atwaniar na .
44027022	Aso kwana kecori yes kolakaros ; naarai emameun yenetwaniari akeijar , dimarai ataker bon .
44027023	Naarai kakuar kana abu emalaika loka Edeke , loarai eoŋ lokeŋ , loamaenenei da , kobwo aapu keoŋ ,
44027024	kalimok eoŋ ebe , ‘ Paul , sirikikurianar ; ibusakinit ijo aibwo kakonyen nuka Kaisar ; ido koany , kiinak Edeke ituŋa lu kere luiupatar . ’
44027025	Aso , lukipa , kolakaros , naarai eyuunit eoŋ Edeke , ebe ejaun kwape kalimokinitere .
44027026	Konye ibusakinit aipok kapujan . ”
44027027	Kosodi kedol apaaran nakitomonet kaoŋon , nakikaleleor aŋolol naka Adiria , bala kidiŋ ebai koomitos ikekwaŋak ebe aapikis neeonit .
44027028	Kitemo , kodumut aidules akaisaarei ; kiyatakis edit kitemo bobo , kodumut aidules atomon kakany .
44027029	Kokuriakaros aipok katiban , koosikis idoboi iwoŋon lukitapaikinet kokori , kilipa akwap aiwalar .
44027030	Nakekototor ikekwaŋak aisii kataker , apotu kijoliliosi itaker toma aŋolol , kijoseikinito bala eosikinete idoboi lukitapaikinet kokume .
44027031	Kolimok Paul ekapolokiton ka iserikalei ebe , “ Dimikito esalete ituŋa lu ataker , mam ipedorete aitajario . ”
44027032	Kosodete iserikalei aitub aunoi nuka itaker , kojalakis kodo .
44027033	Napiwalari , kiŋaiŋa Paul kes kere ainyam inyamat , kobala ebe , “ Lolo ŋes apaaran nakitomonet kaoŋon aidaret kailuŋ , komam inyamete ibore .
44027034	Aso keŋaiŋait , konyamata ; naarai eraun mamakus aitajario , naarai emamei karaida etimat loka akwesikus loeoliori . ”
44027035	Kedau einer ŋun , kolem emugati , kimala Edeke kakonyenekec kere , kobil , kogeu ainyam .
44027036	Kosodete kolakaros kere , konyama kesi da .
