44027038	Kedaut aimonikin , kitebebenata ataker , kocakakis akima aŋolol .
44027039	Kiwala akwap , mam ejenuna akwap ŋin , dimarai apotu koanyutu agule naejai oitolima , kinerut aisukunyar ataker ŋina arai epedor .
44027040	Kocakasi idoboi lukitapaikinet , kinyeis kes kaŋolol , nepepe kaijarijar aunoi nueenis aiteteneta ; kikeut egoe tetere ekutari ekwam kobeasi oitolima .
44027041	Konye kodoloto neiriamata akailan kipok ataker kokwap , kiminaikin ekume , kosalak komam ijaŋijaŋa , konye kobila akailan ekori .
44027042	Kinerut iserikalei aiar ienan , kinye idiokakesi aiduor ka aisi ;
44027043	konye kokoto ekapolokiton aituku Paul , kitikok kinyeis aswam nuenerunitotor . Kicorak luapedorete aidu kisiaut aibironokin aŋolol kobeata neeonit ,
44027044	lukesalete da kabaoi ka oboro ke luka ataker . Kwaŋin kokuasi ituŋa kere neeonit .
44028001	Nakidaunia aiku , kajenut ebe apujan ŋin kenyaritai Melita .
44028002	Kiswamakis sio ikulepek akwap asianut namam etapit , naarai apotu kinokokis akim , kisukunyikis sio , kanuka edou loketepi , ido kanuka aterot da .
44028003	Nakeraraa Paul ekesit loka akito , kibwaik akim , kolom emusaga kanuka amwanis , kidolakin akanike .
44028004	Nakeanyuniata ikulepek akwap emun edelideli kakanike , kotemanaros ebe , “ Abeit erai etuŋanan lo ekaaran , Karaida kekuit kaŋolol , mam Etube isiikit ŋes aijar . ”
44028005	Konye ŋes kilakilakak emun akim komam edumunit amusuŋut .
44028006	Kidarito , komunosi ŋes abuun arai aibiror atwanare eŋeso ; konye kedaut aidar apak naepol koanyut ebe amamei adiomusuŋut kere , kibelokinos kotemasi ebe erai edeke .
44028007	Aapu kaibois kaŋin kejaas amanat nuka ekapolon loka apujan , ekekiror Publio , kisukunyik ŋol sio ketau loka eipaperone apaarasia auni .
44028008	Kosodi kanen kedeka papa loka Publio ekamidi ka aleporit aokot , koloma Paul mamakeŋ , kilip , kidokok ŋes akekanin , kitaŋaleu ,
44028009	Akaulo kaŋun , kopotu ice lukedekas kapujan kaŋin kitaŋaleunoi .
44028010	Kosodete kitubusikis sio kainakineta nuipu ; ido nakikwaŋaror kibwaikis iboro kere lukipuda ataker .
44028011	Akaulo naka ilapio iuni , kediata kataker naka Alegesanderia , nakesalakinit apujan apakio nuka aterot , aanyuneteke kerai Iinacan Imwatok ,
44028012	Kadolo Surakusa , kasalakis nen apaarasia auni .
44028013	Anyoun kanen kerimosi kadolo Regium ; ketubor apaaran adiopet kokut ekwam lokeŋalakimak , kadolo Puteoli apaaran nakiareit .
44028014	Kanen kadumut iinacan , kiŋaiŋaata sio asalakin mamakec apaarasia akanykaarei . Kwaŋin kadolo do Rome .
44028015	Kiirasi iinacan lukaŋina nukosi , kopotu kiton Agwelanaret naka Apius ka Iswamin Iuni aisiriam sio . Nakeanyunia Paul kes , kimal Edeke , kotitiŋior .
44028016	Nakilomaria Rome , kocamakinai Paul aiboi bon nepepe ka eserikalet loidari ŋes .
44028017	Akaulo kapaarasia auni konyarau lukeraas ikapolok koYudayan ; kedaut atukokin , kotema kes atiar , “ Iinacan , karaida mam eswamat aronis kotuŋa karaida koponesio luka lukapapaawok , aponi kejaikin ko Yerusalem toma akanin nuka Iromayon aenio .
44028018	Kaadaut aiŋitanar , kakotosi alacakin , naarai kemamei adiokirot kamakaŋ naaret .
44028019	Konye nakepegatar Iyudayan , ketiŋaikin aiyatakin mama ejai Kaisar-kwabo amamei nakiwosaet ituŋa luka atekereka .
44028020	Aso kanuka ŋun kanyarautu yes aponare aanyun eoŋ keiner keoŋ , naarai kanuka amun naka Isirael ŋes kaenitere korikot kalo . ”
44028021	Kotemasi kesi ŋes atiar , “ Mam sio kidumunit ebalua anyoun koYerusalem kakirokon , ido emamei onace edio da loebunit ne loelimorit ka ainerit akirot naerono kanukon .
44028022	Konye kikoto apupun kamakon nuiwomit ; naarai kanuka akiro nuka erioŋet kalo ejenikina kamakosi ebe ereitai noi kaŋinikibois . ”
44028023	Kedaut aseikin ŋes apaaran kopotu luipu noi mamakeŋ togo lokiboio . Kitetemik kes ka aitejenun ameun tupuruc kiton eboŋ nuka ajakanut naka Edeke , ikujokini akiro nuka Yesu kanuka ikisila luka Musa ka inabin da .
44028024	Apotu ice kiyuut nuenerai , kwabo ice mam iyuuna .
44028025	Namam kecamanarotor , koloto do , kedau Paul einer akirot adiopet na ebe : “ Abu Emoyo Lokalaunan kinera kotenan kama ka enabi Isaia mama ka lukapapaakus ebe :
44028026	‘ Kolot mama ejaas ituŋa lu , kolimok kes ebe : Kiiranarete konye mam ijenunete , Koanyuŋunete da konye mam imisiikinete ,
44028027	Abaŋaakata itauon luka ituŋa kalu , Ijikititas akiikec , Itumudakito akecekonyen , Kinyeis aanyun kakonyenekec , Ka aiirar kakeceki , Kojenut kotauonokec , Kibelokinos ketaŋaleu kes . ’
44028028	Aso kojenutu ebe ejukakin aitajario na naka Edeke Omo : iirarete kesi da . ” [
44028029	Kedau einer ŋun koloto Iyudayan , epeganakinos noi . ]
44028030	Kodau Paul ikar iarei kotogoke loketacanakini , kisukunyanakinenei kere lukeponenenete mamakeŋ ,
44028031	elimonokini ajakanut naka Edeke , ido ka aisisianakin katitiŋ akiro nuka Ejakait Yesu Kristo , komam itikokinio .
45001001	Paul ebulesit loka Kristo Yesu , Iokenyaraunio araun : ekiyakia , Iokegitakinio alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke ,
45001002	nuesumunit Edeke kolo kama ka inabinoke kotoma nukiwadikatai nukalaunak ,
45001003	kes akiro nuka okokuke Yesu Kristo Ejakaitiwok , lokeurio kaur naka Daudi kwape ejaar akuan ,
45001004	loedakakinitai araut Okoku loka Edeke kapedor kwape ejaar Emoyo loka Alaunit , kanuka ajarun kokatwak ,
45001005	kotomakeŋ ŋes kipou kadumuniata asianut ka eiyakiane tetere erimarete lukatekerin kere aiyuun kanuka ekekiror ,
45001006	kotomakec yes da kinyaritai araut luka Yesu Kristo .
45001007	Mama ejaas ŋul kere luejaas Rome luminan luka Edeke luenyaritai araut ikalaunak : Asianut kojai mamakus ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo .
45001008	Esiauni aimal Ekadeke kotoma Yesu Kristo kanukus kere , naarai elimonokinio akusiiyuun anatar akwapin kere .
45001009	Naarai Edeke , loamai komoyoka kotoma Akiro Nukajokak nuka Okokuke , ŋes ekajenanika ebe alimununei yes kailipika komam apalari .
45001010	Ecebokinit ailip arai motoko kanuka akoteke kesipedori Edeke arurukun mama ijaas .
45001011	Naarai kemuit aanyun yes tetere kekopakin yes adioinakinet naka emoyo nakiticasi yes ,
45001012	ŋes atemar ebe aitalakanario bonik ka bonik kanuka aiyuunikus , ka nakaŋ da .
45001013	Konye iinacan , akoto yes ajenun ebe irwan ipu alosikinit abunore mamakus , tetere adumuni adioraito kamakus kwape kama kImo ice , konye ketikokinitai kiton kwana .
45001014	Keburaete Iyonanin ka lukacekwapin da , keburaete lukacoa ka lueolito da :
45001015	kanuka ŋun akapakina eoŋ kowaika alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak kiton mamakus da luijaas Rome .
45001016	Naarai mam Akiro Nukajokak kesurumito ileic : naarai erai apedor naka Edeke ainun aitajario mama ejai ŋinituŋanan yeniyuuni , mama ejai Eyudayat ber , ka Eyonanit da .
45001017	Naarai tomakec epukoritai adolit naka Edeke , anyoun kaiyuun kiton aiyuun ; kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Ebusi ikadoliton kanuka aiyuun . ”
45001018	Naarai epukoritai anyunyura naka Edeke abunore kokuju mama ejai epali kere ka amamus adolit naka ituŋa luitikokinete abeit kanuka amamus adolitekec .
45001019	Naarai ejenas akiro nuka Edeke ideleleete kotomakec , naarai abu Edeke kisideleleu mamakec .
45001020	Naarai ameun kaisub akwap , atakanut iboroke lumam etakanete , ŋes atemar akepedor namam enaŋi , ka Eidekeoneke , kotoma oboro lukesubi . Aso emamei kes aiyar :
45001021	naarai apotu kojenut Edeke , mam kes itubusikinito ŋes kwape Edeke , karaida aima ŋes , dimarai kooliosi kotoma aomisiokec , kitumutoroi ikecetauon luemamei ajenun .
45001022	Kineras ebe eraas lukacoa , kobaŋaakaros ,
45001023	kisiecata aibuses naka Edeke lomam etwani aituputoor aputosia nuka ituŋa kaluetwakete , arai nuka akweny , arai nuka itiaŋ , arai nuka lueliatos .
45001024	Kanuka ŋun abu Edeke kojalak kes toma oraŋasia luka itauonokec mama ejai amamus aila , ka aitisilio da naka awatekec bonik ka bonik ,
45001025	naarai apotu kisiecata abeit naka Edeke araun aiŋal , koyoŋito komaata da isubat itia Ekasuban loituritoi ikar kere ! Amen .
45001026	Kanuka ŋun abu Edeke kojalak kes ainekit naka ileic , naarai apotu aŋorokec da kilocokis einono lokaurunet aituluor lomere lokaurunet ,
45001027	ikiliok da kwape kwaŋin kinyeis einono lokaurunet loka aberu kibworo kotoma oraŋakec ŋolituŋanan mama ejai locekeŋ , ikiliok kiswamanakis ikiliok nukileic , ido koinanakinos eropit loebusakinit apaarikec .
45001028	Ido kwape mam apotu kocamuniata ajenun Edeke , abu Edeke kojalak kes aomisio numam ajokis , kiswamata numam ibusakinito .
45001029	Ileleba amamus adolit kere , nukaronok , airaŋaanut , ameŋeranut ; ileleba ekokote , earit , aŋolopa , aiŋal , aomisio nueroko , ikedeideok ,
45001030	ikasiomak , luelaito Edeke , lukepali , luepogaka , luituros , ikapwakak nueroko , luiulakinito ikauriakakec ,
45001031	luemamei acoa , luejalete aitutuket , lumam eminanara , luemamei aitim ,
45001032	luejenete aitepesenit naka Edeke , ebe luiswamaete nuikote nen ibusakinit atwanare , mam bon iswamaete ŋun , konye itojokito da ŋul lukiswamaete ŋun .
45002001	Aso emamei jo aiyar , ijo ituŋanan yenitubokini yenice ; naarai ŋun nuitubokini yenice , itubokin ilopet aitelekar , naarai jo yenitubi , iswamai da ŋupeŋun ,
45002002	Kijeni oni ebe aitub naka Edeke erai nakabeit mama ejaas ŋul luiswamaete nuikote nen .
45002003	Ijo ituŋanan , yenitubokini luiswamaete nuikote nen , iswamai ijo da ŋupeŋun , iwomit ebe ikui tope kaitub naka Edeke ?
45002004	Imwaŋit kereka ijo abar naka ajokisike , ka aŋirikin , ka atitiŋikinitike da ? Mam kereka ijeni ebe ajokis naka Edeke kiriuni jo aitoronikin ?
45002005	Konye kanuka aninikukon , ka etaukon loemamei aitoronikin , iŋadakin bon anyunyura kapaaran naka anyunyura ka apukorio naka etube loedolit loka Edeke ,
45002006	loetacakini ŋinituŋanan kwape ejaatar aswamisioke ;
45002007	mama ejaas ŋul luemoete aibuses ka ayoŋio , ka aibut , kotoma atitiŋ naka aswamisio nuejok einakini aijar naka ikar kere .
45002008	Ido kaŋul kalueŋolopaka , luiulakinito abeit , luerimasi amamus adolit , edumunete anyunyura ka adedeŋ .
45002009	Ejaunete ican ka aridakinio toma aijar naka ŋinituŋanan yeniswamai nueroko , aisiaun lyudayat , ka Iyonanit da ,
45002010	konye aibuses ka ayoŋio ka ainapakin mama ejai ŋinituŋanan yeniswamai nuejok , aisiaun Iyudayat , ka Iyonanit da .
45002011	Naarai emamei aitiak ituŋa kama ejai Edeke .
45002012	Naarai lukediakarete kere komameete ikisila , emudiaros da komameete ikisila , ŋul da kere lukediakarete kojaas kikisila , etubokinio kokisila .
45002013	Naarai mere ŋul luiirarete ikisila kes eraas ikadolitok kakonyen nuka Edeke , konye ikeswamak ikisila kes luitojokio araut ikadolitok .
45002014	Naarai naiswamaata Imo luemameete ikisila koinono loka ikisila , karaida emameete ikisila eraas kesi ikulepek ikisila .
45002015	Itodikinete ebe iwadikatai aswam naka ikisila toma otauonokec itejenikini da etaukec , iwosaete akeceomisio nuepegasi bonik ka bonik , arai bo eiyaros ;
45002016	kapaaran naetubokinia Edeke nukaiyeiyea nuka ituŋa kama ka Yesu Kristo kwape ejaatar Akiro Nukajokak nuketitiŋitai eoŋ .
45002017	Konye jo , arai kinyaritai Eyudayat kogoŋakina okisila , iwoloboboi kama ejai Edeke ,
45002018	kojeni nuekoto ŋesi , icamuni da nuitelekarito ajokis , kituutooritai kotoma okisila ,
45002019	itogogoŋit bon araut ekeŋarenon loka imudukiok , aica da naka ŋul kaluejaas amuton ,
45002020	eketetenan loka ibaŋiok , ekesisianakinan loka imukerun , ijai kaput naka aijen ka abeit toma okisila ,
45002021	aso jo loisisianakini loce , mam tope isisianakini bon ? Jo loilimonokini ebe Sirikokoi , ikokoi kereka ijo ?
45002022	Jo loibala ebe Siridote , idotei ijo ? Jo loisacit aputosia , iŋasi ijo abilai ?
45002023	Jo loiwolobobot kotoma okisila , itisili kereka Edeke kanuka apaar kokisila ?
45002024	Naarai kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Einyanakinio ekiror loka Edeke katekerin kanukus . ”
45002025	Naarai ejai akepio ajokis arai iswamai ikisila ; konye arai irai ijo loipaarit kokisila , arau akonikepio amamus akepio .
45002026	Aso arai erici lomam ekepep aicorakineta nuka ikisila , mam kereka amamus akepioke imarakinio araut akepio ?
45002027	Ŋol da lomam ekepitai koinono loerici ikisila , mam kereka kitubokini jo loijaas kaiwadikaet ka akepio da , loipaari kokisila ?
45002028	Naarai ŋol loerai Eyudayat kokuju mere ŋol Eyudayat cut , karaida akepio nakokuju toma akuan ;
45002029	dimarai ŋol loerai Eyudayat kotoma , ka akepio nakotau kotoma omoyo kwabo mere aiwadikaet . Akeiturio mam ebuni kotuŋa dimarai kama ejai Edeke .
45003001	Itelekarit kereka Eyudayat kinyo ? Arai anyoin bo ajokis naka akepio ?
45003002	Itelekarit noi kaŋolipone . Nasodit , naarai isiŋadikinitai Iyudayan akiro nuka Edeke .
45003003	Anyoika bo arai ice kakesi araas lumere lumunon ? Amamus amunonutukec itapalauni tope amunonut naka Edeke ?
45003004	Madi akuj ! Korai Edeke lokabeit , ŋinituŋanan da ikeŋalan , kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Tetere itojokio araut loedolit kakirokon , Ipikori da kotoma atubokiniokon . ”
45003005	Konye arai amamus adolitewok iticasi adolit naka Edeke , kenera anu ? Ebe Mam Edeke erai loedolit aitican oni kanyunyura ? ( Enera kopone loka etuŋanan . )
45003006	Madi akuj ! Kanuka ŋun ikonakini ai Edeke etubokini akwapin ?
45003007	Konye arai kanuka aiŋalaka iyatanakini abeit naka Edeke aitodiar akeibuses , kanukinyo eriŋa katubokinitere eoŋ kwape ekadiakanaran ?
45003008	Ido kanukinyo mam kibalar ebe , “ Keswamata nukaronok tetere epote nukajokak ” ? kwape kisabanakiniata icetuŋa sio ebe kinera isio kwaŋin , Edolit atubokiniokec .
45003009	Biai bo do ? Kijokuka oni aitelekarit ice ? Mam cut , nepepec da ; naarai kidau aosan Iyudayan ka Iyonanin da kere ebe eyait adiakanar kes ,
45003010	kwape iwadikatere ebe : “ Emamei ikadoliton , karaida idiopet ;
45003011	Emamei yenejenuni , emamei da yenemoot Edeke .
45003012	Apaasi kere , emamei kes kere ajokis ; Emamei yeniswamai nuejok , emamei karaida idiopet . ”
45003013	“ Elogorotokec ŋes ailit naeŋaara ; Ijodijodete kaŋajepakec , Ejai aisorit naka emusaga kwap kaŋajepakec . ”
45003014	“ Ileleba aitukekec elamit ka adwaris . ”
45003015	“ Erurukito akejenekec abukor aokot .
45003016	Ejai amudiar ka aburun orotinikec .
45003017	Mam apotu kojenut erot loka ainapakin . ”
45003018	“ Emamei ayoŋit Edeke kakonyenekec . ”
45003019	Aso kijeni ebe akiro kere nuelimito ikisila , inerasi mama ejaas ŋul lueyaito ikisila , tetere itubutario ŋiniituk , akwap kere da kojau otube loka Edeke .
45003020	Kanuka ŋun emamei yenejai akuan yenitojokio araut yenedolit kakonyeneke kanuka aswamisio nuka ikisila , naarai kanuka ikisila ŋes ejenunor adiakar .
45003021	Konye kwana edeleleu adolit naka Edeke komameete ikisila , itejenunitai kokisila ka inabin da ,
45003022	ŋes adolit naka Edeke naejai kanuka aiyuun Yesu Kristo , mama ejaas kere luiyuunito . Naarai emamei atiaketait ;
45003023	naarai adiakasi kere , komam edolokinito aibuses naka Edeke ,
45003024	akesianut naeinakini atitai ŋes itojokit kes araut luedolito , kanuka alakunio naejai toma Kristo Yesu ,
45003025	loibwaikinit Edeke araut aitupucet kanuka aiyuun akeokot , tetere itodikini akedolit kanuka ajalakin adiakanareta nukolo nueŋirikinit Edeke ;
45003026	kosodi kitodik adoliteke kapak kana , tetere eraun loedolit ka loitojoki da ŋin yeniyuuni Yesu araut loedolit .
45003027	Aso ai bo ejai aolobobot ? Agolor kiŋa , Kanuka ikisila inyoika tope ? Luka aswamisio ? Mam cut , konye kanuka ikisila luka aiyuun .
45003028	Naarai kitogogoŋit ebe itojokio ituŋanan araut yenedolit kanuka aiyuun , komameete aswamisio nuka ikisila .
45003029	Erai kereka Edeke loka Iyudayan bon ? Mam kereka erai loka Imo da ? Eebo , loka Imo da ,
45003030	naarai erai Edeke ediopet ; loitojoki luekepitai kotoma aiyuun , ka lumam ekepitai da kanuka aiyuun ŋipeŋin .
45003031	Aso kitapalauni kereka ikisila kanuka aiyuun ŋin ? Madi akuj ! Konye kiticasi ikisila .
45004001	Aso kinera anyoika nuka Aburaam papaakosi kwape ejaar akuan ?
45004002	Naarai arai kitojokitai Aburaam kanuka aswamisioke , ejai naeolobobaa , konye mere kakonyen nuka Edeke .
45004003	Naarai inerasi biai nuiwadikatai ? Ebe , “ Abu Aburaam kiyu Edeke , kimarakinai ŋes araun adolit . ”
45004004	Konye mama ejai ekeswaman , mam ekeropit imarakinio kanuka asianut , dimarai iburao .
45004005	Kwabo mama ejai yenimam iswamai , konye iyuuni ŋol loitojoki luetumaaka , imarakinio akeiyuun araun adolit .
45004006	Kwape inerar Daudi ebe isirereŋitoi ituŋanan yenimarakinit Edeke araun ikadoliton komameete aswamisio ;
45004007	Ebe , “ Isirereŋitoi luisionio aronisio , ka luerapitai da adiakanareta ;
45004008	Isirereŋitoi etuŋanan lomam Ejakait imarakinit adiakar . ”
45004009	Aso ca isirereŋitoi ŋol loekepitai arai bo ŋol lomam ekepitai da ? Naarai kinera ebe , Kimarakinai aiyuun naka Aburaam araun adolit .
45004010	Kimarakinio biai ? Kedaun aikep , arai bo eroko kekepa ? Mere kedaun aikep , dimarai eroko ekepa .
45004011	Abu ŋesi kodum akepio araun aanyunet arai nakaipucakinet naka adolit naka akeiyuun eroko ekepa , tetere eraun papa loka lukeyuunak kere karaida mam ekepitai , tetere imarakinio kes adolit .
45004012	Eraun da papa loka akepio mere mama ejaas ŋul luekepitai bon , konye mama ejaas ŋul da luetupito ikukut luka aiyuun naka papaakosi Aburaam nakejaatar eriŋa ekepa .
45004013	Naarai aisumunet ŋin mama ejai Aburaam ka aurike da ebe eraun ekeruman loka akwapin , mam kebuni kokisila , dimarai kanuka adolit naka aiyuun .
45004014	Naarai arai luka ikisila kes ikerumak , eraun aiyuun atitai , aisumunet da itapalaunio .
45004015	Naarai eyaŋaunete ikisila anyunyura , konye naemameatar ikisila emamei apaar .
45004016	Kanuka ŋun ebuni aisumunet kotoma aiyuun , tetere egoŋakina aisumunet asianut , kitogogoŋoi da mama ejai aur kere , mere mama ejaas ŋul luka ikisila bon , dimarai mama ejaas ŋul luka aiyuun naka Aburaam , ( loerai papaawok kere ,
45004017	kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Kadakaki jo araun papa loka atekerin nuipu , ” ) kakonyen nuka Edeke loiyuunit ŋesi , loeinakini lukatwak aijar , loenyarauni da iboro luemameete bala luejaas .
45004018	Kemamei amun abu kiyuu kotoma amun , tetere eraun papa loka atekerin nuipu ; kwape kelimokinere ebe , “ Kwape kwaŋin ejaun akoniwur . ”
45004019	Mam abu akeiyuun kononokiar , naaomitor ejautene loka akuanake naketwanit , nakeraar loka ikar bala akwatat , ka akoik da naka Sara nakerakakinit ,
45004020	konye mam abu kobuonokin kanuka aisumunet naka Edeke kamamus aiyuun , dimarai kogogoŋor kaiyuun , kitopoloo Edeke ,
45004021	kojeni cut ebe epedori Edeke aswam nuisumunit .
45004022	Kanuka ŋun , “ kimarakinai ŋes adolit . ”
45004023	Konye mam kiwadikatai kanukeŋ bon ebe , “ Kimarakinai ŋes ” ,
45004024	dimarai kanuwok da , Kiponio aimarakin oni da lukiyuunit ŋol lokitajaruni Yesu Ejakaitiwok kokatwak ,
45004025	lokeinakinio kanuka aibucanaretawok , kitajarunai da aitojok oni araun luedolito .
45005001	Aso naarai kitojokitai araun luedolito kanuka aiyuun , kajaut kainapakin mama ejai Edeke kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo .
45005002	Kanukeŋ kidumu erot loka aiyuun lokitodoli asianut ŋin nakibwoia , kiwoloboboi da kotoma amun aibuses naka Edeke .
45005003	Kwabo mere ŋun bon , dimarai kiwoloboboi da kotoma aiticanio , kajenete ebe aiticanio eyaŋauni atitiŋikin ,
45005004	atitiŋikin da eyaŋauni aitogogoŋio , aitogogoŋio da eyaŋauni amun ,
45005005	amun da mam itisili , naarai ekwamakinitai amin naka Edeke otauonowok kanuka Emoyo Lokalaunan lokiinakinitai oni .
45005006	Naarai nakirokor kikalanyaka , kedol apak abu Kristo kotwanik luetumaaka ,
45005007	Naarai etiono ituŋanan atwanikin ikadoliton , konye diat eluŋakin ituŋanan aŋirikin atwanikin yenejok .
45005008	Konye iturit Edeke akemin mamawok , naarai nakirokor kirai ikadiakanarak abu Kristo kotwanik oni .
45005009	Aso aitelekarit noi kiidau kwana aitojokio kotoma akeokot , kitajario da kanukeŋ alemunio kama ejai anyunyura .
45005010	Naarai arai nakiraar kolo lukasurup kitupucitoi kEdeke kanuka atwanare naka Okokuke , aitelekarit noi kiidau aitupucio , kitajario kotoma aijarake .
45005011	Kwabo mere ŋun bon , konye kiwoloboboi da kotoma Edeke , kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo , lokidumunia kwana aitupuciowok .
45005012	Kanuka ŋun kwape kelomunia adiakanar akwapin kanuka etuŋanan ediopet , kolom da atwanare kanuka adiakar , kwaŋin kodolok atwanare otuŋa kere , naarai apotu kere kodiakasi —
45005013	naarai ajai adiakar toma akwap aliŋakin ikisila , konye mam emaritai adiakar naemameatar ikisila .
45005014	Konye erumit atwanare ameun ka Adam kiton Musa , erumit da ŋesi lumam apotu kodiakasi kopone loka apaar naka Adam , loerai aput naka ŋol kaloebunit .
45005015	Konye ainakinet mam eputos kaibucaret . Naarai arai apotu luipu kotwaka kanuka aibucaret naka ediopet , aitelekarit noi epoloor asianut naka Edeke ka ainakinet naejai toma asianut naka etuŋanan ediopet Yesu Kristo , kanuka luipu .
45005016	Ido ainakinet mam eputos kanaayau loadiakaa . Naarai etube loabu kobu kanuka ediopetuŋanan abu koyau atubokinio , konye ainakinet naabu kobu kanuka aibucanareta nuipu ayau aitojokio .
45005017	Aso , arai kanuka aibucar naka ediopetuŋanan abu atwanare kirum kanuka etuŋanan ŋol , aitelekarit noi ŋul luedumunete aipadara naka asianut ka ainakinet naka adolit irumete toma aijar kanuka etuŋanan ŋol ediopet , Yesu Kristo .
45005018	Aso ca kwape iriaria aibucaret adiopet ituŋa kere atubokinio , kwape kwaŋin iriaria aswamisioit adiopet nakadolit ituŋa kere aitojokio ka aijar da .
45005019	Naarai kwape keraunotor luipu ikadiakanarak kanuka epali loka ediopetuŋanan , kwape kwaŋin itaraunio luipu ikadolitok kanuka arima naka etuŋanan ediopet .
45005020	Apotu ikisila kolomut tetere iyatanakin aibucar ; konye nekiyatakinor adiakar , abu asianut kodepa noi noi ,
45005021	tetere kwape erumitor adiakar kotoma atwanare , kwape kwaŋin irumi asianut kanuka adolit kiton aijar naka ikar kere kanuka Yesu Kristo Ejakaitiwok .
45006001	Aso do kinera anu ? Kasalakis kereka adiakanar , tetere iyatakin asianut ?
45006002	Madi akuj ! Oni lukitwaka kama kadiakar kikwaikini ai kirina kibusi kotomakeŋ ?
45006003	Arai bo mam ijenete ebe oni kere lukibatisatai kotoma Kristo Yesu , aponi kibatisai kotoma atwanareke ?
45006004	Aso aponi kidaai nepepe kaŋes kanuka aibatis kotoma atwanare , tetere kwape kitajarunere Kristo kokatwak kanuka aibuses naka Papa , kwape kwaŋin oni da kilosenenei kaijar nakitetet .
45006005	Naarai arai kirotakinitai kaŋes kotoma aput naka atwanareke , kwape kwaŋin kirotakinio kotoma aput naka ajarunike .
45006006	Kijeni na ebe aponi etuŋananiwok lokolo kibubukinoi kaŋes , tetere itapalaunio akuan nakadiakanar , komam bobo adiakanar kitubuleseni oni .
45006007	Naarai yenatwana eosikinitai anyoun kadiakar ,
45006008	Konye arai kipou katwaka nepepe ka Kristo , kiyuunit ebe kijari da nepepe kaŋes .
45006009	Kijeni ebe kedau Kristo ajarun kokatwak , mam etwani bobo , mam bobo atwanare eyait ŋes .
45006010	Naarai atwanare naketwani , abu kotwanik adiakar irwan atipet bon , konye aijar naejari , ejari mama ejai Edeke .
45006011	Yes da kwape kwaŋin koomito bonik araut lukatwak kama ejai adiakar , konye ikajarak mama ejai Edeke kotoma Kristo Yesu .
45006012	Aso kinye adiakar airum awatekus nuetwakete , yes arimar aiŋobelekec .
45006013	Kwabo sirijaikinete akusitutubeta mama ejai adiakar aitwasamaa amamus adolit , dimarai kijaikis bonik mama ejai Edeke , kwape ikajarak luanyout kokatwak , akusitutubeta da mama ejai Edeke aitwasamaa adolit ;
45006014	naarai mam adiakar kiyait yes , naarai mere ikisila kiyaito yes , dimarai asianut .
45006015	Biai bo do ? Kadiakasi , naarai mam ikisila kiyaito oni , dimarai asianut ? Madi akuj !
45006016	Mam kereka ijenete ebe loijaikinos bonik arimar kwape ibulesin , iraas do ibulesin luka ŋol kaloirimarito , arai adiakar naeyauni atwanare , arai bo arima naeyauni adolit ?
45006017	Konye kimalai Edeke , naarai iraas kolo ibulesin luka adiakar , konye ipotu korimasi kotauonokus aput naka aisisianakin nakiinakinio yes ,
45006018	ido nakiwosikinere anyoun kadiakar koraut ibulesin luka adolit .
45006019	Enera eoŋ kopone loka etuŋanan kanuka akalanyanut naka awatekus . Naarai kwape kijaikiniata kolo atutubetakus aitwasamao kotoma amodokok , ka epali loeyauni epali , kwape kwaŋin kijaikis do kwana atutubetakus aitwasamao kotoma adolit naeyauni aitalaunio .
45006020	Naarai nakiraatar ibulesin luka adiakar , kiwosikinitai anyoun kadolit .
45006021	Anyoika kereka araito nuipotu kodumut kapaarasia kaŋun , kakiro kaŋun nukisurumito kwana ileic ? Naarai awasia naka akiro kaŋun ŋes atwanare .
45006022	Konye kwana kidaut aosikinio anyoun kadiakar iraut ibulesin luka Edeke , idumut araito nueyaunete alaunit , awasiakec da ŋes aijar naka ikar kere .
45006023	Naarai eropit loka adiakar ŋes atwanare , konye ainakinet naka Edeke erai aijar naka ikar kere kotoma Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok .
45007001	Iinacan , mam kereka ijenete-naarai enera kaŋul kaluejenete ikisila ebe eyaito ikisila etuŋanan eroko ejari ?
45007002	Naarai eenito ikisila aberu naemanyitai eroko okilenike ejari ; konye ketwana ekiliokit , eosikinitai ŋin kokisila luka okilenike .
45007003	Kanuka ŋun enyarao naadote arai kedumun kecekiliokit , apak naeriŋar okilenike ejari . Konye arai ketwana okilenike , eosikinitai anyoun kokisila , mam da erai naadote arai kemany ekiliokit ece .
45007004	Ikainacan , yes da kwape kwaŋin ipotu kotwakata kama kikisila , kanuka akuan naka Kristo , tetere iraunos luka ece , ŋes ŋol loitajarunitai kokatwak , tetere kidumakini Edeke araito .
45007005	Naarai nakiraar kolo luka akuan , abu airaŋaanut naka adiakar kiswama kotoma atutubetawok kanuka ikisila , kasodete adumakin atwanare araito .
45007006	Konye kwana kiwosikinitai anyoun kokisila , kitwaka kama ejai ŋin nakijoreorit , kasodete kejaanakis komoyo lokitetet kwabo mere kaiwadikaet namojoŋ .
45007007	Aso do kinera anu ? Eraas kereka ikisila adiakar ? Madi akuj ! Konye timam kajenu adiakar kedim ikisila . Naarai timam kajenu aiŋobel kedim ikisila atemar ebe , “ Siriŋobelei . ”
45007008	Konye adiakar , naabu kodum apak kanuka aicorakinet , kiswama kotomakaŋ ŋolipone loka aiŋobel , Naarai etwanit adiakar emameete ikisila .
45007009	Abu eoŋ karai kolo loajari komameete ikisila , konye nakebunio aicorakinet kojaru adiakar , katwana do eoŋ .
45007010	Kerai aicorakinet naeyauni aijar kosubite ŋin kamakaŋ naeyauni atwanare .
45007011	Naarai abu adiakar , naabu kodum apak kanuka aicorakinet , keŋala eoŋ , kaaria da .
45007012	Kwaŋin eraas ikisila lukalaunak , ka aicorakinet da nakalaunan , ka naedolit ka naejok da .
45007013	Aso do koraun kereka ajokis atwanare kamakaŋ ? Madi akuj ! Konye adiakar , tetere etakanuni araut adiakar , abu kiswama atwanare kotomakaŋ kanuka ajokis , tetere iyatakin adiakar araut adiakar naerono noi kanuka aicorakinet .
45007014	Naarai kijeni ebe eraas ikisila luka emoyo ; konye eoŋ arai lokakuan , kagwelaritai ayait naka adiakar .
45007015	Naarai mam ajeni nueswamai , Naarai nuakoto , mere kes nueswamai , konye eswamai nualait .
45007016	Konye arai eswamai numam akoto , acamunit ebe ejokuka ikisila .
45007017	Aso kwana mere eoŋ eswamai ŋun dimarai adiakar naiboie kotomakaŋ .
45007018	Naarai ajeni ebe emamei ibore yenejok yeniboie kotomakaŋ , ŋes atemar ebe toma akuanaka . Naarai ejai akote diekaŋ , konye aswam ajokis be .
45007019	Naarai mam eswamai ajokis naakoto , konye aronis namam akoto , ŋes eswamai .
45007020	Konye arai eswamai numam akoto , mam bobo eoŋ eswamai dimarai adiakar naiboie kotomakaŋ .
45007021	Kwaŋin adumuni ekisil ebe naakotor eoŋ aswam nuejok , kaapikin aronis .
45007022	Naarai alelakinit ikisila luka Edeke kotoma otuŋanan lokotoma .
45007023	Konye aanyuni ekisil ece kotoma atutubetaka ejiosi kekisil loka aomisioka , ka aituluor eŋatara loka ekisil loka adiakar loejai toma atutubetaka .
45007024	Itukwi eoŋ lokican ! Iŋai bo kayuuni eoŋ kakuan kana nakatwanare ?
45007025	Emalai Edeke kanuka Yesu Kristo Ejakaitiwok ! Aso do eoŋ elopet ejaanakini ekisil loka Edeke kaomisioka , kwabo ekisil loka adiakar kakuanaka .
45008001	Aso do kwana emamei ŋul luejaas toma Kristo Yesu atubokinio .
45008002	Naarai kaosikis eoŋ ikisila luka Emoyo loka aijar loejai toma Kristo Yesu anyoun kokisila luka adiakar ka atwanare .
45008003	Naarai ŋun numam apedorito ikisila , kanuka akalanyanut naka akuan , abu Edeke , naejukunia Okokuke elopet kaput naka akuan nakadiakaran ido kanuka adiakar , kotubok adiakar kotoma akuan ,
45008004	tetere aicorakineta nuka ikisila itodolikinio kotomawok , lumam kilosenenei atupar akuan dimarai atupar Emoyo .
45008005	Naarai ŋul luetuparete akuan eomitos nuka akuan , konye ŋul luetuparete Emoyo , eomitos nuka Emoyo .
45008006	Naarai aomit naka akuan ŋes atwanare , konye aomit naka Emoyo ŋes aijar ka ainapakin .
45008007	Kanuka ŋun aomit naka akuan ŋes aitusurup Edeke ; naarai mam enonokikinit ikisila luka Edeke , kwabo mam epedori anonokikin ;
45008008	kes da luejaas toma akuan mam epedorete aisiyalamikin Edeke .
45008009	Konye arai iboie Emoyo loka Edeke kotomakus , mam ijaas toma akuan dimarai toma Omoyo . Arai da emamei ituŋanan Emoyo loka Kristo , mam ŋin erai yenike .
45008010	Konye arai ejai Kristo kotomakus , atwakata awatekus kanuka adiakar , konye ejarete ikusimoyon kanuka adolit .
45008011	Konye arai iboie Emoyo loka ŋol lokitajaruni Yesu kokatwak kotomakus , ŋol lokitajaruni Kristo Yesu kokatwak einakini da akusiwat nuetwakete aijar kanuka Ekemoyo loiboie kotomakus .
45008012	Aso do , iinacan , kija kapesen , mere mama ejai akuan atupar aijar naka akuan ,
45008013	naarai arai ijarete atupar akuan , ikotosi atwakare , konye arai kitwataniasi aswamisio nuka akuan kanuka Emoyo , ijarete do .
45008014	Naarai kere luiŋarenikinit Emoyo loka Edeke , ŋul kes odwe luka Edeke .
45008015	Naarai mam idumunito emoyo loka ebulesene aboŋor bobo akurian , dimarai idumunito emoyo loka araun odwe . Kanuka ŋol kimonya ebe , “ Abba ! Papa ! ”
45008016	Emoyo elopet itejenikini imoyonowok ebe kirai idwe luka Edeke ,
45008017	arai kirai idwe , kirai da ikerumak , ikerumak luka Edeke , luirumete nepepe ka Kristo , arai ca kiiticani nepepe kaŋes , tetere kitubusikinio da kaŋes .
45008018	Aomit eoŋ ebe aiticanio naka apak kana mam ibusakinit aitiirianio kaibuses naekoto apukokinio oni .
45008019	Naarai idarete isuban keimiel noi apukokinio naka odwe luka Edeke ;
45008020	naarai kitononokikinai isuban aamameak , mere kanuka eipudikec , dimarai kanuka ŋol lokitononokikini kotoma amun ;
45008021	naarai eosikinio isuban da anyoun kobulesene loka aibos , alomar aosikinio naka aibuses naka idwe luka Edeke .
45008022	Naarai kijeni ebe idinyasi isuban kere , eriebasi da nepepe kiton tinenikwana ;
45008023	kwabo mere ŋul bon , dimarai oni da ikulepek luejaas araito nugeet nuka Emoyo , kidinya oni da kotomawok , kedareto araut odwe , ŋes atemar ebe alakun naka awatewok
45008024	Naarai kiponi kitajari kanuka amun . Konye ketakanu ibore yenikemunoi emamei bobo amun . Naarai iŋai tope emunokina ibore yenetakani ?
45008025	Konye arai kimunokina yenimam etakani , kidaret katitiŋikin .
45008026	Kwape kwaŋin da isigalikini Emoyo akalanyanutuwok ; naarai mam kijeni kwape ibusakinitor ailip , konye kinainaanakin Emoyo oni keidiny lomam inerio .
45008027	Ŋol da loirerei itauon ejeni aomisio nuka Emoyo , kwape ejaatar , naarai iŋaiŋaaŋakini lukalaunak kwape ekotor Edeke .
45008028	Kijeni ebe iswamaete iboro kere nepepe kanuka ajokis mama ejaas ŋul lueminasi Edeke , ŋes atemar ŋul lukenyaraunio kanuka alosikiniteke .
45008029	Naarai ŋul luabu kojenu sek , abu koseu da sek aituput kes aput naka Okokuke , tetere erauni ŋesi ekiyai kotoma oinacan luipu .
45008030	Ŋul da luabu koseu sek , konyarau da kes ; ŋul da luabu konyarau , kitojok da kes ; ŋul da luabu kitojok , kitubusik da kes .
45008031	Aso do kinera anu kaŋun ? Arai ejai Edeke kanuwok iŋai tope kisurokini oni ?
45008032	Ŋol lomam abu kimik Okokuke elopet , konye koinak ŋes kanuwok kere , mam kereka kikorakini iboro kere da nepepe kaŋes ?
45008033	Iŋai bo iwosai luseuna luka Edeke ? Edeke itojokit ;
45008034	iŋai bo etubokini ? Kristo Yesu loketwani , konye aitelekarit lokitajarunio , loejai akan nakoteten naka Edeke , loiŋaiŋaanakini oni .
45008035	Iŋai bo kitiaki oni kamin naka Kristo ? Arai bo ican , arai aridakinio , arai areio , arai ebeli , arai amujalal , arai aronis , arai ekileŋ ?
45008036	Kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Kanukon kiario aitiwar akwap , Kimario bala amerekekin nutubutubo . ”
45008037	Konye kotoma ŋun kere kipikori noi kanuka ŋol lokimina oni .
45008038	Naarai etogogoŋi ebe karaida atwanare , karaida aijar , karaida imalaikan , karaida lueyaito , karaida nuejaas , karaida nuejaunete , karaida lukapedor ,
45008039	karaida amukurur , karaida aidules , karaida isubat kere , mam kipedorete aitiak oni kamin naka Edeke naejai toma Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok .
45009001	Enera abeit kotoma Kristo , mam eŋalai ; itejenunete akaomisio kotoma Emoyo Lokalaunan ,
45009002	ebe kakadakinit noi ka ariebo da namam enaŋi kotauka .
45009003	Naarai tikapedo ailip eoŋ elopet aikenio atiakario kama ka Kristo kanuka ikainacan , lukatekerika kwape ejaar akuan ,
45009004	kes luka Isirael , lukeinakinio araut odwe , ka aibuses , ka aitutuketa , ka ainakinio ikisila , ka aijaanakin Edeke , ka aisumuneta da ;
45009005	eraas lukapapaa lukec , ido kotomakec alomunia Kristo kwape ejaar akuan . Kituritete Edeke loeyait kere ikar ka ikar . Amen .
45009006	Kwabo mere ebe ekarun akirot naka Edeke . Naarai luelomunete kotoma Isirael , mere kere luka Isirael obe ,
45009007	karaida keraas lukaur naka Aburaam , mam kere eraas idwe ; konye “ toma Isaak ŋes enyaritere akoniwur . ”
45009008	Ŋes atemar ebe idwe luka akuan mere ŋul idwe luka Edeke , dimarai idwe luka aisumunet imaritai araut akeur .
45009009	Naarai akirot na ŋes ebalar aisumunet ebe , “ Kedol apak , aboŋuni , ido ejaunete Sara da kikoku . ”
45009010	Kwabo mere ŋin bon , konye Rebeka da kedum akoik kokiliokit ediopet , ŋes Isaak papaawok ,
45009011	karaida mam ber euruunitai idwe ŋul , komam iswamato adiokirot naejok arai naerono , tetere icasit alosikinit naka Edeke naka aseun , mere kanuka aswamisio , dimarai kanuka anyariteke ,
45009012	aponi kolimokinai ŋin ebe , “ Ijaanakini lokapolon lodidi . ”
45009013	Kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Abu kamina Yakob , konye kala Esau . ”
45009014	Aso kinera anu ? Ejai kereka amamus adolit kaneejai Edeke ? Madi akuj !
45009015	Naarai ebala ŋesi Musa ebe , “ Etimi yenakoto aitim , ido ekonakini asianut yenakoto aikonakin asianut . ”
45009016	Aso do mere kanuka loekot karaida loekeri , dimarai kanuka aitim naka Edeke .
45009017	Naarai ebala nakiwadikatai Parao ebe , “ Kanuka nu ŋes ketonyounio jo tetere etodikini akapedor mamakon , ido tetere elimorio ekakiror kakwapin kere . ”
45009018	Aso do itimi loekot , ido itininiki loekot .
45009019	Aso kitemari eoŋ ebe , “ Kanukinyo eriŋar ŋesi itoronitor ? Naarai iŋai kereka enyoikini nuelosikinit ŋesi ? ”
45009020	Ijo ba ituŋanan , iŋai bo ijo yeniboŋokini Edeke ? Epedori kereka ibore yenisubuna alimokin yenikesubuni ebe , “ Kanukinyo kiisubia eoŋ kwana ? ”
45009021	Emamei kereka ekajean apedor kama kelupe , asubun ibore yenibus ka ibore da yenesil kaluŋuret ŋipeŋin ?
45009022	Konye anyoika bo arai ekoto Edeke aitodikin anyunyura ka aitejenun da akepedor , abu kotitiŋikin katitiŋ kanaepol iboro luka anyunyura luasubitai amudiario ,
45009023	tetere itejenuni abarara naka akeibuses kotoma oboro luka aitim , luetemonokinit apeŋo kodumut aibuses ,
45009024	kes oni lukiinyarauni mere Iyudayan bonik , dimarai Imo da ?
45009025	Kwape kineritor da kama ka Kosea ebe , “ Ŋul lumam araas ikatuŋa , anyarai ikatuŋa , ŋin da namam kerai naminataka , anyarai naminat . ”
45009026	“ Bobo da toma aibois ŋin nakelimokinitere kes ebe , ‘ Mam yes iraas ikatuŋa , ’ Nepenen enyaraere idwe luka Edeke lokajaran . ”
45009027	Kiworo Isaia da nuka Isirael ebe , “ Karaida kerai etiai loka odwe luka Isirael kwape asiŋe naka aŋolol , aatoŋotokec bon itajario ;
45009028	naarai iswamai Ejakait akekirot kakwap aitodol ka atubutub da . ”
45009029	Ido kwape kegeunia Isaia einer ebe : “ Arai kemam Ejakait loka ajoresio kinyeinitor oni aur , Ti kiirau bala Sodom , ti kiiputokin ka Gomora . ”
45009030	Aso do kinera anu ? Ebe Imo lumam atupito adolit apotu kodumut adolit , ŋes adolit naelomuni kaiyuun .
45009031	Konye do luka Isirael luetupito ikisila luka adolit , mam edolokinito ikisila ŋul .
45009032	Kanukinyo ? Naarai mam apotu kotupata korot loka aiyuun , dimarai korot loka aswamisio . Kitiguikinos kamoru naketiguikinan ,
45009033	kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Koany , ebwaikini toma Sion amoru naketiguikinan ka atiiba nakebiroron ; Yeniyuuni ŋes mam isurumio ileic . ”
45010001	Ikainacan , nuemiela kotauka , ido nuelipi Edeke kanukec ŋes aitajariokec .
45010002	Naarai etejenuni kanukec ebe edunyaka kanuka Edeke , konye mere kotoma aijen .
45010003	Naarai kanumam ejeniata adolit naka Edeke , kokotos aitogogoŋ adolitekec kikulepek , mam apotu korimasi adolit naka Edeke .
45010004	Naarai Kristo ŋes aŋetakinet naka ikisila , tetere ŋin yeniyuuni itojokio araut ikadoliton .
45010005	Naarai abu Musa kiwadik ebe ituŋanan yeniswamai adolit naelomuni kokisila ejari kotoma ŋin .
45010006	Konye adolit naelomuni kaiyuun inera kwanata ebe , Sirikiner kotaukon ebe , “ Iŋai bo yenekot adokari toma akuj ? ” ( Ŋes atemar ebe , ayaun Kristo kwap . )
45010007	Arai bo ebe , “ Iŋai bo yenekot aijesar toma aipany ? ” ( Ŋes atemar ebe , ayaun Kristo kuju anyoun kokatwak . )
45010008	Konye inera anu ? Ebe , Eapie akirot kamakon , kaitukukon , kotaukon da , ( ŋes atemar ebe akirot naka aiyuun nakilimonokini isio ) .
45010009	Naarai arai ilimori kaitukukon ebe Yesu ŋes Ejakait , iyuuni da kotaukon ebe abu Edeke kitajar ŋes kokatwak , kitajario .
45010010	Naarai iyuuni ituŋanan kotauke kiton adumun adolit , elimori da kaitukuke kiton adumun aitajario .
45010011	Naarai ineras nuiwadikatai ebe , “ Ŋin yeniyuuni ŋes mam irumete ileic . ”
45010012	Naarai emamei atiaketait , Eyudayat ka Eyonanit ; naarai erai ŋesi Ejakait loka kere , ekabaran mama ejaas kere luiwoneete ŋes .
45010013	Naarai “ Ŋin yeniwonei ekiror loka Ejakait itajario . ”
45010014	Aso iwoneete biai ŋol lomam iyuunito ? Ido da iyuunete biai ŋol lomam iirarito ? Iirarete da biai komamei ekalimonokinan ?
45010015	Elimonokinete biai komam iyakiaritai ? Kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Ejokuka cama akeje nuka ŋul kaluelimonokinete Akiro Nukajokak ! ”
45010016	Konye mam kes kere apotu korimasi akiro nukajokak . Naarai inera Isaia ebe , “ Ejakait , iŋai bo iyuunit akiro nueirarit kamakosi ? ”
45010017	Aso aiyuun elomuni kotoma aiirar , aiirar da kanuka akirot naka Kristo .
45010018	Konye abala eoŋ ebe , mam kereka apotu kiirasi ? Eebo , eirasi ; “ Anata ekeceporoto akwap kere , Akecekiro da kiton osaŋeta luka akwapin . ”
45010019	Konye abala eoŋ ebe , mam kereka luka Isirael ajenunito ? Nugeet inera Musa ebe , “ Kesurumi yes ekokote kama kaŋul lumam eraas ateker ; Ketunyunyurikini do yes kanuka ateker naemamei aijen . ”
45010020	Isaia da etitiŋ noi einer ebe , “ Abu kadumun kama kaŋul lumam kamooto ; Abu ketejenun mama kaŋul lumam keŋisito . ”
45010021	Konye nuka Isirael ebala ebe , “ Abu kariorite akakanin aitiwar akwap mama ejaas ituŋa lukepali ka luirebirebete . ”
45011001	Aso abala ebe , Aŋer kereka Edeke iketuŋa ? Madi akuj ! Naarai arai eoŋ da loka Isirael , loka aur naka Aburaam , loka ateker naka Benyamin .
45011002	Mam Edeke enerit iketuŋa luabu kogeu ajenun , Mam kereka ijenete nuineras nuiwadikatai kanuka Eliya , kwape iwosaa luka Isirael kakonyen nuka Edeke ?
45011003	Ebe , “ Ejakait , aarata inabinokon , atiyanakis da itemwanakon , eoŋ bon asal , ido emoete akaijar . ”
45011004	Konye aboŋokinet naka Edeke ebala biai ? Ebe , “ Etasalit kanukaŋ ikiliok ilukumin ikanykaarei , lumam ekukokinos Baal . ”
45011005	Aso kwape kwaŋin apak na , naka kwana , ejai aatoŋot naeseunitai kanuka asianut .
45011006	Konye arai erai kanuka asianut , mam bobo elomuni kanuka aswamisio ; arai timam asianut eroko erai asianut .
45011007	Biai bo do ? Ibore ŋin yenikemoot Isirael , mam edumuna . Luseuna apotu kodumut , konye ice kere aponi kitininikai ,
45011008	kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Abu Edeke koinak kes emoyo loka ajo , Akonye numam eanyunete , Aki da numam iirarete , Kiton apaaran naka lolo . ”
45011009	Ebala Daudi da ebe , “ Korau emesakec eic ka akuluma , Ka ibore yenikitiguikinet , ka yenikitegelet kes .
45011010	Kitumudakai akonyekec , tetere mam esesenete , Kitukukum ipuranakec apaarasia kere . ”
45011011	Aso abala ebe , eguikis kereka kiton aibiror cut ? Madi akuj ! Konye kanuka aibucarikec adolok aitajario Imo , tetere isurumio luka Isirael ekokote .
45011012	Aso arai eraun aibucarikec abar naka akwapin , atwaniarikec da araun abar naka Imo , itelekarit cama aitodolikiniokec !
45011013	Konye enera kayes Imo . Aso naarai arai eoŋ ekiyakia loka imo , etopoloori aijaanakinika ,
45011014	tetere esurumi lukatekerika ekokote , ka aitajar da ice kakesi .
45011015	Naarai arai acakariokec ayau aipuc naka akwapin , anyoin aisukunyuniokec dimarai aijar anyoun kokatwak ?
45011016	Arai araito nageet erai nakalaunan , kwape kwaŋin aluŋuret da ; arai da aliasit erai nakalaunan , kwape kwaŋin atenieik da .
45011017	Konye arai epakanaritai ace katenieik , ijo da , eseitun loka ais kiraikinitai kidiŋikec , korau ikamoran yenika ajokis naka aliasit ,
45011018	sirikiwolobob katenieik kaŋun . Arai kiwolobob , mere jo idakit aliasit dimarai aliasit kidakit jo :
45011019	Aso itemari atiar , “ Kepakario atenieik ŋun tetere keraikinio eoŋ . ”
45011020	Abeit ŋun . Epakanaritai kes kanuka amamus aiyuunikec , ido da icasi kanuka aiyuunikon . Sirikiturokin , konye koyoŋ .
45011021	Naarai arai mam Edeke itimit atenieik akulepek , mam kitimi jo da .
45011022	Aso koany ajokis ka adedeŋ naka Edeke ; adedeŋ mama ejaas luibiroros , konye ajokis naka Edeke mamakon , arai kisalak ajokis ŋin ; arai mere kwaŋin jo da kijepario .
45011023	Ka ŋul da , arai mam esalito toma amamus aiyuun , iraikinio , naarai epedori Edeke airaikin kes bobo .
45011024	Naarai arai kijepunitai jo katorom naka eseitun loka ais , kiraikinitai oseitun lokoriot lomam erai einono , itelekarito cama atenieik akulepek airaikinio ainyakakin oseitunikec .
45011025	Naarai iinacan , akoto yes ajenun aiyeiyea na kinyeis aomit bonik araut lukacoa ; ebe , aninikiar atutubet naka Isirael aitodol naelomunia etiai kere loka Imo ,
45011026	kwaŋin itajario luka Isirael kere ; kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Ebuni Ekalakunan koSion , Isiyekari amamus ayoŋit Edeke kotoma Yakob ” ;
45011027	“ Na da ŋes akaitutuket kakes , Naalemaria adiakanaretakec . ”
45011028	Aso kotoma Akiro Nukajokak araut lukasurup luka Edeke kanukus ; konye kotoma aseunio araut lueminai kanuka lukapapaakec .
45011029	Naarai mam Edeke iitokini ainakinetake ka anyariteke da .
45011030	Naarai kwape kolo kipaliikinioto yesi Edeke , konye kwana idumut aitimio kanuka aipaliikinikec ,
45011031	kwape kwaŋin epaliikinioto kesi kwape kwana tetere edumunete aitimio kanuka aitim naipotu yesi kodumut .
45011032	Naarai agoloki Edeke kere nepepe toma aipaliikin , tetere itimi kere .
45011033	Eiliili cama abar ka acoa ka aijen naka Edeke Mam ireikinos itubesiake , irotinike da mam ibwapunos !
45011034	“ Naarai iŋai tope ejeni aomisio nuka Ejakait , Arai iŋai bo kerai ekapetan akiroke ? ”
45011035	“ Arai iŋai bo keinakinit ber ŋes ainakinet , Etacakinio ŋes bobo ? ”
45011036	Naarai epote iboro kere kamakeŋ , ejaas da kanukeŋ , ido eboŋorete mamakeŋ . Kojai aibuses mamakeŋ ikar kere . Amen .
45012001	Kanuka ŋun , iinacan , keŋaiŋait yes , kanuka aitimeta nuka Edeke , kijaikis akusiwat koraut asubanit naejari , nakalaunan , naisiyalamikinit Edeke , ŋes erai aimakus naibus .
45012002	Kwabo sirikiputo nuka ikar kalu , konye kanuka aisiteteunio naka aomisiokus kijulakinos , tetere igimorete nuekoto Edeke , nuejok , ka nuisiyalamikinito , ka nuedolito da .
45012003	Naarai kanuka asianut nakainakinitai alimokini ŋinituŋanan kayesi ebe siriwomiara adepar naibusakinit aomit , konye koomito kacoit , kwape ekorakinitor Edeke aitemis naka aiyuun .
45012004	Naarai kwape kijaar katutubeta nuipu toma akuan adiopet , kwabo mam atutubeta kere iswamaete aswam adiopet ,
45012005	kwape kwaŋin oni da lukipu , kirai akuan adiopet kotoma Kristo , ka atutubeta da nuka lucewok bonik ka bonik .
45012006	Aso naarai kija kainakineta nuegelegela kwape ejaar asianut nakiinakinitai , ketwasamata kes ; arai adwaranut , kwape ejaar aiyuuniwok ;
45012007	arai aijaanakin , kotoma aijaanakiniwok ; yenisisianakini , kotoma aisisianakinike ;
45012008	yenicori , kotoma aicoroke ; yenekori , kotau loliogot ; yeniŋarakini , kadunyanut ; yenitimi da , kaiyalama .
45012009	Korau amina naemamei aisoswanut . Kolaata aronis , kiketakinos kotoma kanuejok .
45012010	Kotoma amin naka einacane , kominanaros bonik ka bonik ; kotoma aibuses kitopoloorite ŋinituŋanan aupake .
45012011	Kotoma adunyanut sirikalanyaka , kokokito komoyo , kijaanakis Ejakait .
45012012	Kolelakinito amun kotitiŋioto kocan , kicebokinito ailip .
45012013	Kokoranakisi lukalaunak nuipudasi , kisukunyanakisi ipejok .
45012014	Kilipanakisi arereŋ lukimanito yes ; kilipanakisi arereŋ kwabo sirikilamata .
45012015	Kolelata kaluelelete , komonyata kaluemonyete .
45012016	Koomito adiopekirot bonik ka bonik . Siridakara , konye koupanaros kaluitasonos . Siriraas lukacoa kakonyenekus ikulepek .
45012017	Siritacakis aronis kanuka aronis , kocoito nuejok kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere .
45012018	Arai epedoros kowaikus , kinapakina kituŋa kere .
45012019	Luminan , sirinyaŋanakinos , konye kinac anyunyura ; naarai iwadikatai ebe , “ Ebala Ejakait ebe , Enyaŋit ekaŋ , eoŋ atacakini . ”
45012020	Konye “ arai eriebi lokasurupikon eteŋei , kitanyam , arai ejakit akur , kitamat ŋes ; naarai naiswamaa kwaŋin inokokini atotole akouke . ”
45012021	Sirikiipiko aronis , konye kipiko aronis kanuka ajokis .
45013001	Kononokikinite ŋinituŋanan ikapolok lueyaito , naarai emamei apolou dimarai naebuni kama ejai Edeke , ka ŋin da naejai icorakinit Edeke .
45013002	Kanuka ŋun yenitepegi apolou etepeg aicorakinet naka Edeke , ido luitepegete itudumikinos etube .
45013003	Naarai ikayaitok mere luitukurianete kotoma aswamisioit naejok , dimarai kotoma naerono . Ikoto kereka ijo kinyek akurian apolou ? Kiswama do nuejok , kituri ŋesi jo .
45013004	Naarai erai ŋesi ekejaanakinan loka Edeke kamakon kanuka ajokis , Konye arai kiswama naerono , kokuriana , naarai mam edakit ekileŋ atai ; erai ŋesi ekejaanakinan loka Edeke , loinyaŋi kanyunyura yeniswamai nueroko .
45013005	Kanuka ŋun ibusakinit anonokikin , mere kanuka anyunyura bon , dimarai kanuka aomisio nuilepilepete .
45013006	Naarai kanuka ŋun itacete da esolo , naarai eraas kesi ikejaanakinak luka Edeke , icebokinito ŋipeŋin .
45013007	Kotacanakisi kere nuebeito , loitelemi esolo loka ituŋa , esolo loka ituŋa ; loitelemi esolo da loka iboro , esolo loka iboro ; kotacanakisi ayoŋit luebeito ayoŋit , aibuses da mama ejaas lukaibuses .
45013008	Sirijaas kapesen mama ejai ituŋanan kere , dimikito aminanara ; naarai yenemina aupake etodol ikisila .
45013009	Naarai na ebe , “ Siridote , Siriari , Sirikokoi , Siriŋobelei , ” ka aceicorakinet kere , imorikikinitai toma akirot na ebe , “ Komina ikoniidunyet kwape iminar bon . ”
45013010	Amin mam ikonakini iidunyet erono ; kwaŋin amin ŋes aitodolikinet naka ikisila .
45013011	Ka ŋun da , ijenete apak , ebe adol esawa yes akwenyun kajoo . Naarai kwana eapie aitajariowok aitelekarit nakigeunia aiyuun ;
45013012	aeka akuar , eapie da apaaran . Aso kalacasi aswamisio nuka amuton , kanapa lujiis luka aica .
45013013	Kalosenenete kebusak kwape paaran , mere kotoma aboliasio ka emeret , mere kotoma adoteu ka abenyanut , mere kotoma aŋolopa ka ekokote ,
45013014	konye konapa Ejakait Yesu Kristo , kwabo siribuakinito akuan aitodol nuimiela .
45014001	Kisukunyut yenekalanyana kaiyuun , kwabo mere atubokin abuonokinike .
45014002	Ituŋanan yeniyuunit enyami kere , konye yenekalanyana enyami ikui .
45014003	Kinyek yenenyami aimen yenimam enyami , karaida yenimam enyami siriketuboki yenenyami ; naarai isukunyikinit Edeke ŋes .
45014004	Iŋai bo jo yenitubokini ebulesit loka yenice ? Ebwoi ŋesi arai ibirori kama kejakaitike elopet . Eebo , isibwoio naarai epedori Ejakait aisibwo ŋes .
45014005	Eomit ice apaaran adiopet adepar apaaran ace , eomit ice apaarasia kere araut nueriakanara . Kitogogoŋite ŋinituŋanan kaomisioke ilopet .
45014006	Yenericit apaaran , ericit kanuka Ejakait . Yenenyami da , enyami kanuka Ejakait , naarai imalai Edeke . Yenimam enyami da , mam enyami kanuka Ejakait , imalai da Edeke .
45014007	Naarai emamei ituŋanan kotomawok yenejari kanuke bon , emamei da yenetwani kanuke bon .
45014008	Aso arai kijari , kijari kanuka Ejakait , arai kitwaki da , kitwaki kanuka Ejakait . Aso arai kijari , arai kitwaki da , kirai luka Ejakait .
45014009	Naarai abu Kristo kotwana kojaru da tetere eraun Ejakait loka lukatwak ka lukajarak da .
45014010	Konye jo , kanukinyo itubokinia onacekon ? Ijo da , kanukinyo imenitor onacekon ? Naarai kibwoi rwaru kere kakonyen nuka eicoloŋ loka aitub loka Edeke .
45014011	Naarai iwadikatai ebe , “ Ebala Ejakait ebe , Kwape ajaria , ekukokini ŋinikuŋ mamakaŋ , Elimori da ŋiniŋajep Edeke . ”
45014012	Aso do inera ŋinituŋanan kaoni akekiro ilopet kakonyen nuka Edeke .
45014013	Kanuka ŋun kenyeis bobo atubonokin bonik ka bonik , konye aitelekarit kitogogoŋoto na ebe sirikibwaikis ekomio karaida aitiguikinet orot loka onacekon
45014014	Ajeni eoŋ bobo da etogogoŋit noi kotoma Ejakait Yesu ebe emamei ibore yeniketal kotoma oinonoke . Konye ŋin yeneomit ibore araut yeniketal , erai yeniketal kamakeŋ .
45014015	Naarai arai ekadakinit onacekon kanuka inyamatakon , mam bobo ilosi kwape ejaar amin . Sirikimudia yenabu Kristo kotwanik kanuka inyamatakon .
45014016	Aso kinyek yenejok kamakus ainyanakinio .
45014017	Naarai ajakanut naka Edeke mere ainyam ka aimat , dimarai adolit ka ainapakin ka aiyalama da kOmoyo Lokalaunan ;
45014018	naarai ŋin yenijaanakini Kristo kotoma akiro kaŋun , isiyalamikinit Edeke , ecamunito da ituŋa .
45014019	Aso do katupasi akiro nuka ainapakin ka nuka adukonor bonik ka bonik .
45014020	Sirikimuna aswam naka Edeke kanuka inyamat . Abeit elaete kere , dimarai erono ituŋanan yenenyami kitiguikinia ice ;
45014021	ejok ainyein ainyam karaida aimat ebino , karaida aswam akirot kere naitiguikini onacekon ,
45014022	Aiyuun naijaatar , kojaut kaŋin ijo elopet kakonyen nuka Edeke . Isirereŋitoi ŋin yenimam etubokin ilopet kotoma akirot naceamunit .
45014023	Konye yenebuonokin arai enyami etubokinio aitelekar , naarai mam enyamit kaiyuun ; naarai ŋiniswamisioit namam elomuni kaiyuun erai adiakar ,
45015001	Kibusakinit oni lukagogoŋok aibwok akalanyanut naka luemamei agogoŋ , kwabo mere aisiyalamikina bonik .
45015002	Kesiyalamikisi oni ŋinituŋanan ikeidunyet kodum ajokis kodukoi da .
45015003	Naarai Kristo da mam esiyalamikina elopet bon ; dimarai kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Amorosito nuka lukimoromoroete jo , apotu kadoikis eoŋ . ”
45015004	Naarai nuewadikatai sek , ewadikatai kanuka aisisianakinia oni , tetere kanuka atitiŋikin ka aitalakara naka nukiwadikatai kidumuni amun .

45015010	Bobo da ebe , “ Kolelata , yes atekerin , nepepe kiketuŋa . ”

45015014	Ikainacan , etogogoŋit eoŋ elopet kanukus ebe ileleba yes da ajokis , isilelebitai acoa kere , bobo da ipedorete aikwenyanar bonik ka bonik .

45015020	kwabo alosikinit alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak , mere neelimoritere ekiror loka Kristo , kenyek adukokin apetetait naka icetuŋanan ,
45015021	konye kwape iwadikatere ebe ,
45015022	Kanuka ŋun ŋes ketikokinitere irwan ipu kenyek abunore mamakus ,
45015023	konye kwana , naarai emamei bobo eoŋ aibois katutubeta kanu , bobo da ameun ikar luipu emiela abunore mamakus ,
45015024	amuno aanyun yes naetorio alosit Sipain , yes da kinyamakinete eoŋ korotoka , kadau ber aipejokin yes adaun aimue .
45015025	Konye kwana alosi Yerusalem , ejaanakini lukalaunak .
45015026	Naarai isiyalamikinito luko Makedonia ka Akaia atukonokin iboro akorakin lukican lukotoma lukalaunak luejaas Yerusalem .
45015027	Naarai isiyalamikinito kesi , ido da ejai kes apesen kamakec , naarai arai imorikikinete Imo arereŋesiokec nuka emoyo , ibusakinit da kes aijaanakin ŋul karereŋesiokec nuka akuan .
45015028	Aso kadau eoŋ ŋun , kepucak kes araito ŋin , etori mamakus alosit Sipain ;
45015029	ido ajeni ebe naabunio mamakus , abuni kaileleba naka arereŋ naka Kristo .
45015030	Keŋaiŋait yes , iinacan , kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo , kanuka amin da naka Emoyo , koutas nepepe keoŋ kotoma ailipikus kanukaŋ mama ejai Edeke ,

45015033	Edeke loka ainapakin kojai nepepe kayes kere . Amen .
45016001	Eturit Poibe kinaciwok kamakus , naerai akejaanakinan naka ekanisa loka Kenekerea ,
45016002	tetere isukunyikinete ŋes kotoma Ejakait kwape ibusakinitor lukalaunak , kisigalikis ŋes kotoma akirot kere naipuda kamakus , naarai arau ŋesi akeŋarakinan naka ituŋa luipu , ka eoŋ da elopet .
45016003	Kiyogata Pirisika ka Akuila ikeswamak lukaupaka kotoma Kristo Yesu ,

46001001	Paul , lokenyarao araut ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kanuka akot naka Edeke , ka Sosetene onace .
46001002	Mama ejai ekanisa loka Edeke loejai Korinto , ŋul lukitalaunio kotoma Kristo Yesu , lukenyarao koraut lukalaunak , nepepe kaŋul kere luiwoneto ekiror loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo kaŋiniibois , loerai Ejakaitikec ka lowok da :
46001003	Kojai asianut mama ijaas , ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo .
46001004	Emalaenenei Edeke tiritir kanukus , kanuka asianut naka Edeke nakiinakinio yes , kotoma Kristo Yesu .

46001006	kwape kitogogoŋere aitejenunet naka Kristo kotomakus ,

46001009	Erai Edeke lomunot , lokinyarauni yes alomun oidicane loka Okokuke , Yesu Kristo Ejakaitiwok .
46001010	Aso iinacan , keŋaiŋait yes , kokiror loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo , ebe kinerata kere adiopekirot , kinye atiakatiakaun ajaun kidiŋikus , konye kidicakina ketau ediopet ka ainerun da adiopet .
46001011	Naarai , ikainacan , kalimokis eoŋ lukokale loka Kloe , ebe ejai aŋolopa kidiŋikus .
46001012	Aso naabala nata ebe , ebala ŋinidiopet kayesi ebe , “ Arai eoŋ yenika Paul , ” ice da ebe , “ Konye eoŋ yenika Apolo , ” ka ice da ebe , “ Arai eoŋ yenika Kepa , ” ka ice da ebe , “ Arai eoŋ yenika Kristo . ”
46001013	Okwe , etiakatiaka kereka Kristo ? Ibubukinitoi kereka Paul kanukus ? Arai bo iponi kibatisai kokiror loka Paul ?
46001014	Emalai naarai mam ebatisat idio kayesi dimarai Keresipo ka Gaio ;
46001015	kinyek idiotuŋanan atemar ebe aponi kibatisai kokirorikaŋ .

46001018	Naarai akirot naka emusalaba erai abaŋaanut kama ejaas lueoliorete , konye mama kija oni lukitajario erai apedor naka Edeke .
46001019	Naarai iwadikatai ebe , “ Amudiari acoa naka lukacoa , Etapalauni da apirianut naka luepiriaka . ”
46001020	Ai bo ejai lokacoa ? Ai bo ejai ekewadikan ? Ai bo ejai eketepegan loka ikar kalu ? Mam kereka Edeke abu kitababaŋ acoa naka akwap ?
46001021	Naarai kotoma acoa naka Edeke , mam akwap abu kojen Edeke kanuka acoa , abu kisiyalamik Edeke aitajar luiyuunito kotoma abaŋaanut naka akirot naelimonokinio .
46001022	Naarai ekotosi Iyudayan aanyuneta , Iyonanin da emootos acoa ,

46001024	konye mama ejaas ŋul luenyaritai , Iyudayan ka Iyonanin da , erai Kristo apedor naka Edeke , ka acoa da naka Edeke .
46001025	Naarai abaŋaanut naka Edeke erai acoa aitelekarit naka ituŋa , akalanyanut da naka Edeke egogoŋ aitelekarit naka ituŋa .
46001026	Naarai , iinacan , koomito anyarauniokus , ebe mam luipu kayesi keraas lukacoa kwape ejaar aitemis naka akwap , mam ipu lukapedor , mam ipu lukapolou da luenyaraunitai ,
46001027	konye abu Edeke koseu lukabaŋaanut luka akwap tetere isurumi lukacoa ileic ; bobo da abu Edeke koseu luekalanyaka luka akwap tetere isurumi lukagogoŋok ileic ;
46001028	bobo da abu Edeke koseu imukopin , ka luemwaŋitai kotoma akwap , eebo , ka iboro da luemameete , tetere itamamauni ŋul luejaas ,

46001031	kanuka ŋun kwape iwadikatere ebe , “ Yeneolobobot , koolobobote kotoma Ejakait . ”
46002001	Eoŋ da , iinacan , naabunio mamakus , mam abunit alimonokin yes nukaiyeiyea nuka Edeke kakiro nuejijim karaida kacoa .

46002010	Konye kipukok Edeke oni kanuka Emoyo . Naarai irerei Emoyo kere , kiton nuidulok nuka Edeke .
46002011	Naarai iŋai tope kotuŋa yenejeni aomisio nuka ituŋa , dimarai emoyo loka ituŋanan loejai kotomakeŋ ? Kwape kwaŋin emamei yenejeni aomisio nuka Edeke dimarai Emoyo loka Edeke .
46002012	Konye oni , mam kidumunit emoyo loka akwap , dimarai Emoyo loebuni kama ejai Edeke , tetere kijenuni ainakineta nukiinakini Edeke oni atitai .

46002016	“ Naarai iŋai kereka ejenunit aomisio nuka Ejakait , tetere ituutoori ŋes ? ” Konye kijaa oni kaomisio nuka Kristo .
46003001	Eoŋ da , iinacan , mam apedorit einer kayes kwape luka emoyo , dimarai luka akuan , kwape imukerun kotoma Kristo .

46003004	Naarai naebalar idiopet ebe , “ Arai eoŋ yenika Paul , ” ice da ebe , “ Arai eoŋ yenika Apolo , ” mam kereka iraas ituŋa atai ?

46003006	Abu eoŋ kera , kicoco Apolo , konye kitopolo Edeke .

46003010	Kwape ejaar asianut naka Edeke nakainakinitai eoŋ , abu kapesik apetetait kwape ekadukon lokapolon lokacoa , konye eduki ece . Konye kocoite ŋinidiopet kwape edukio .
46003011	Naarai emamei yenepedori apesikin apetetait ace , dimarai ŋin naedaunitai apesikin , ŋes Yesu Kristo .
46003012	Konye arai keduk ituŋanan toma apetetait ŋin esabu , arai epuesa , arai amor nuketiai , arai akito , arai anya , arai ariaŋ da ,

46003016	Mam kereka ijenete ebe iraas yesi eyekalu loka Edeke , ebe da iboie Emoyo loka Edeke kotomakus ?
46003017	Arai kemuna ituŋanan eyekalu loka Edeke , emunaari Edeke ituŋanan ŋin . Naarai erai eyekalu loka Edeke lokalaunan , ŋes yesi .
46003018	Sirikemodakin ituŋanan . Arai ejai kotomakus ituŋanan yeneomit ilopet araut yenikacoa kokar kalu , korau ŋesi yenibaŋ , tetere eraun yenikacoa .
46003019	Naarai acoa naka akwap kana ŋes abaŋaanut kama ka Edeke . Naarai iwadikatai ebe , “ Ikamuni ŋesi lukacoa koboteikec . ”
46003020	Bobo da ebe , “ Ejeni Ejakait aomisio nuka lukacoa , ebe eraas aamameak . ”
46003021	Kwaŋin kinyek ituŋanan aolobobot kotoma otuŋa . Naarai eraas kere lukus ,
46003022	arai Paul , arai Apolo , arai Kepa , arai akwap , arai aijar , arai atwanare , arai nuejaas kwana , arai nuepote , kere eraas nukus ,
46003023	iraas yesi da luka Kristo , Kristo da loka Edeke .
46004001	Koomit ituŋanan sio kwanata , kwape ikejaanakinak luka Kristo , ka ikeŋadak da luka nukaiyeiyea nuka Edeke .
46004002	Bobo da iburao ikeŋadak atakan eraas lumunon .
46004003	Konye kamakaŋ erai akirot naedit noi yes , arai airabet kere naka etuŋanan , atubokin eoŋ . Mam da atubokin bon .
46004004	Naarai mam ajeni nuewosakin bon , konye mam kemarakinio adolit kanuka ŋun , konye Ejakait ŋes katubokini .
46004005	Aso sirikitubo akirot eroko apak , aitodol naebunio Ejakait , loitacauni nuibwaitai nuka amuton , ido isideleleuni ainerun naka itauon . Kosodi edumuni ŋinituŋanan akeiturio kama ejai Edeke .
46004006	Aso iinacan , etuputoo ŋun aputokaŋ ka Apolo da kanukus , tetere kanukosi isisiaete ainyein adepar nuiwadikatai , kinye idio kayesi adakanun kanuka ediopet aitelekarit loce .
46004007	Naarai iŋai kitegelikinit jo kama kaluce ? Inyoin kereka ejai jo yenimam kiinakinitai ? Konye arai kiinakinitai , kanukinyo iwolobobotor bala mam kiinakinitai ?
46004008	Idaut aimonikin ! Idaut adumun abar ! Iyaitos kamameete isio ! Eebo , arai tiiyaito , tetere kimori ayait kayes !
46004009	Naarai aomit ebe etodia Edeke sio ikiyakia awasia , kwape ituŋa luetubokinitai aario : naarai kiraun isio ibore yenisesena kakwap , kama ka imalaikan ka ituŋa da .
46004010	Kirai isio ibaŋiok kanuka Kristo , konye iraas yesi lukacoa kotoma Kristo , Kikalanyaka isio , konye igogoŋ yesi . Kitubusikinitai yes , konye sio kitisilitoi .
46004011	Kiton osawa lo da , kiriebi eteŋei ka akure da , kimujalal , kibuŋao , bobo da emameete sio ireria ,
46004012	kitaaritoi aswam kakaninikosi . Nakimoromoroere , kilipanakini arereŋ ; nakiticanere , kititiŋikinit ;
46004013	nakisabanakinere , kiŋaiŋai ; kitusubi bala asusuj nuka akwap , ediirit da loka iboro kere , kiton kwana .
46004014	Mam ewadikai nu aisurumia yes ileic , konye aikwenyar yes kwape idweka luminan .
46004015	Karaida kejaas yes ikesisianakinak ilukumin itomon kotoma Kristo , konye emameete lukapapa luipu . Naarai eoŋ ŋes kaurit yes kotoma Kristo Yesu kanuka alimonokin Akiro Nukajokak .
46004016	Aso keŋaiŋait yes koputoorito eoŋ .
46004017	Kanuka ŋun ejuk Timoteo mamakus , loerai okokuka lominat , lomunot da kotoma Ejakait , lokisiituni yes irotinika luejaas toma Kristo , kwape esisianakinia kaŋiniibois kotoma ŋolikanisa .
46004018	Konye edakanunos ice kayesi ebe mam abuni mamakus .
46004019	Konye abuni atipet mamakus , arai ekot Ejakait , abuni eoŋ ajenun mere akiro nuka ŋul kaluedakanunos dimarai apedorikec .
46004020	Naarai mam ajakanut naka Edeke ejai toma akirot , dimarai toma apedor .
46004021	Ikotosi anyoika ? Kabu kereka mamakus kebela , arai bo kabu kamin komoyo loiyapepera ?
46005001	Isiarakina eemut ebe ejai adoteu kotomakus , adoteu da namam ejauna kotoma atekerin ; ebe etuŋanan ajaut kaberu naka papake .
46005002	Yes da idakanunos , kwabo mam kikadakinit , tetere elemario kokidiŋikus ŋol lokiswamai akirot ŋin .
46005003	Naarai , karaida amamei kakuan , konye ajai komoyo , adau eoŋ elopet atubokin ŋol lokiswamai akirot ŋin kwape tikajaar ,
46005004	kotoma okiror loka Ejakait Yesu , naitukonokinotor nepepe ka ekamoyo , ka apedor da naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu ,
46005005	kijaikis ŋol Satan tetere emudiario akuanake , tetere itajario emoyoke kotoma apaaran naka Ejakait Yesu .
46005006	Mam aolobobokus ejok . Mam kereka ijenete ebe aitubuunet naedit itubuuni aluŋuret kere ?
46005007	Kitesegaaros do kaitubuunet namojoŋ , tetere iraunos aluŋuret nakitetet , kwape iraatar lumam itubuuno . Naarai aponi Kristo Aleleŋewok koinakinai araut asubanit .
46005008	Aso karicata epucit , mere kaitubuunet namojoŋ , karaida kaitubuunet naka ameŋeranut ka aronis , dimarai ka namam itubuuno naka aipioror naka emoyo ka abeit .
46005009	Abu kewadikak yes kotoma obaluaka ebe sirikimorianakinos kidotea ;
46005010	mam abala ebe kinacata cut idotea luka akwapin kanu , arai ikeraŋak , arai ikaŋatak , karaida ŋul luemaete aputosia , naarai arai kerai kwaŋin ti ibusakinit anyoun kakwapin kanu .
46005011	Konye kwana kewadikakini yes ebe sirikimorianakinos kaloenyaritai onac arai erai edote , arai ekeraŋan , arai loemai aputosia , arai ekamoromoron , arai ekameran , arai ekaŋatan ; etuŋanan loikoni kwaŋin mam acamunit yes karaida aimor kaŋes .
46005012	Naarai anyoin ajokis kamakaŋ atubokin luejaas kiŋa ? Mam kereka yes itubokinito luejaas toma okanisa ?
46005013	Konye etubokini Edeke ŋul luejaas kiŋa , Kireŋeasi yesi ekaronon ŋol loejai kidiŋikus .
46006001	Arai ejai edio kayesi akirot kama ka onaceke , ijecekini kereka ŋesi aosan ŋes kakonyen nuka lumam edolito , kwabo mere kakonyen nuka ikalaunak ?
46006002	Arai bo mam ijenete ebe etubokinete ikalaunak akwapin ? Aso arai itubokinete yesi akwapin , mam kereka ipedorete aitub akiro nuedisiak noi ?
46006003	Mam kereka ijenete ebe kitubokini imalaikan ? Kikurwokinito biai akiro nuka aijar kana !
46006004	Aso arai ijaas kaitub akiro nuka aijar kana , idakakinete kereka lumam eomitai kokanisa araut ikatubok ?
46006005	Enera ŋun aisurumia yes ileic . Emamei kereka kotomakus lokacoa ediopet , loepedori aitub akiro nuka iinacanake ,
46006006	konye iwosanakinos iinacan bonik , bobo da kakonyen nuka lumam iyuunito .
46006007	Aso kwana ejai aŋwal kotomakus , naarai iwosanakinos bonik , Kanukinyo gwai mam kikonakinere erono ? Kanukinyo gwai mam kinasere iborokus .
46006008	Konye yes ikonakinete erono , ido iŋasete , kiton iinacanakus da .
46006009	Mam kereka ijenete ebe lumam edolito mam irumete ajakanut naka Edeke ? Sirikiŋalas ; karaida idotea , karaida luemaete aputosia , karaida lueeloko , karaida ikiliok luituluoros bala aŋor , karaida iketepak ikiliok ,
46006010	karaida ikokolak , karaida ikeraŋak , karaida ikamerak , karaida ikamoromorok , karaida ikaŋatak , mam irumete ajakanut naka Edeke .
46006011	Ice kayesi da ipotu koraas kwaŋin ; konye aponi kilotar , konye aponi kitalaun , konye aponi kitojoki araut luidolito , kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu Kristo , kotoma Emoyo da loka Edekewok .
46006012	“ Ibus iboro kere kamakaŋ ” ; konye mam iboro kere isigalikinete . “ Ibus iboro kere kamakaŋ ” ; konye mam ketubulesene idiobore .
46006013	“ Eraas inyamat luka akoik , akoik da naka inyamat ” itapalauni Edeke kere , ŋin ka ŋul da . Mam akuan erai naka adoteu , dimarai naka Ejakait , Ejakait da loka akuan .
46006014	Konye abu Edeke kitajar Ejakait , kitajari oni da kapedorike .
46006015	Mam kereka ijenete ebe eraas awatekus atutubeta nuka Kristo ? Aso kalema kereka atutubeta nuka Kristo , ketaraut atutubeta nuka naadote ? Madi akuj !
46006016	Arai mam kereka ijenete ebe lokirotakinos kanaadote eraas adiopetekuan ? Naarai ebala ebe , “ Ŋul luarei eraunos adiopetekuan . ”
46006017	Konye ŋol lokirotakinos ka Ejakait , erai emoyo ediopet kaŋes ,
46006018	Kinacata adoteu , ŋinidiakaret naiswamai ituŋanan erai nakokiŋa akuanake ; konye ŋin yenedotei adiaka kotoma akuanake alopet .
46006019	Mam kereka ijenete ebe awatekus kes eyekalu loka Emoyo Lokalaunan loejai tomakus , lokiinakini Edeke ? Mam iraas kanukus ;
46006020	naarai kigwelitai kakais nuipu . Aso kitopolooritos Edeke kotoma awatekus .
46007001	Konye nuka akiro nuipotu kiwadikakis eoŋ . Ejok kama kekiliokit kinyek atiror aberu .
46007002	Konye kanuka adoteu , kojau ŋolikiliokit kakeberu , ŋiniberu da kokilenike .
46007003	Kotacak ŋolikiliokit akeberu nuibusakinito ŋes , kwape kwaŋin da kotacak ŋiniberu nuibusakinito okilenike .
46007004	Mam aberu alopet eyait akekuan , dimarai okilenike ; kwape kwaŋin da mam ekiliokit elopet eyait akekuan , dimarai akeberu .
46007005	Sirimikanaros bonik , alemar diat icamanaros adaun apak , tetere iluŋakinos ailip ; kosodete konyet aimorikikin bobo , kinyek Satan acodun yes kanuka amamus ayaikina .
46007006	Enera ŋun kacamun , kwabo mere kaicorakinet .
46007007	Konye emiela ituŋa kere araut kwape kaeoŋ elopet . Konye ejai ŋinidiopet ainakineteke naebuni kama ejai Edeke , idiopet kopone ece , idiopet da kopone ece .
46007008	Konye alimokini lumam edukokina ka apuserun da , ebe ejok kamakec arai esalito kwape kaeoŋ .
46007009	Konye arai mam epedorete ayaikina bonik , kodukokinos . Naarai ejok adukokin itia ainok .
46007010	Ecorakini luedukokina , kwabo mere eoŋ , dimarai Ejakait , ebe , kinyek aberu aisac okilenike .
46007011	Konye arai esaci , kosal mam edukokina , arai bo kopuco kokilenike . Bobo da kinyek ekiliokit aireŋear akeberu .
46007012	Alimokini ice , eoŋ mere Ejakait , ebe , arai ejaas onace kaberu namam iyuunit , ecamuni ŋin da aiboienen kaŋes , kinyek aireŋear ŋin .
46007013	Arai da ejaas aberu kekiliokit lomam iyuunit , ŋes da ecamuni aiboienen kaŋin , kinyek anyoun kama kokilenike .
46007014	Naarai italaunitai ekiliokit lomam iyuunit kanuka akeberu , aberu da namam iyuunit italaunitai kanuka okilenike . Arai mere kwaŋin tieraas ikusidwe lumam elaete , konye kwana eraas lukalaunak
46007015	Konye arai enyouni lomam iyuunit , konyou do ŋesi ; kakiro nuikote nen mam onac arai kinac eenitai . Naarai abu Edeke konyarau oni toma ainapakin .
46007016	Ijo aberu , ijenuni biai , wolo bo itajari okilenikon ? Ijo da ekiliokit , ijenuni biai , wolo bo itajari akoniberu ?
46007017	Konye na bon , kolosenenei ŋinidiopet kwape kekorakinitor Ejakait , ŋinidiopet da kwape kenyaraunitor Edeke . Ecoranakini kwaŋin kotoma okanisan kere .
46007018	Kenyaraunitai kereka etuŋanan ekepitai ? Kinyek araun lomam ekepitai . Kenyaraunitai kereka etuŋanan lomam ekepitai ? Kinyek akepio .
46007019	Naarai akepio mam erai ibore , amamus akepio da mam erai ibore , dimarai aricit aicorakineta nuka Edeke .
46007020	Kosalak ŋolituŋanan kanyaraunio nakenyaraunere .
46007021	Irai kereka ebulesit nakinyaraunere ? Siripodo ŋun , Konye arai ipedori araun loeosikinitai , kitwasama gwai kwaŋin .
46007022	Naarai lokenyaraunio erai ebulesit , erai loeosikinitai loka Ejakait ; kwape kwaŋin da lokenyaraunio erai loeosikinitai erai ebulesit loka Kristo .
46007023	Aponi kogweli yes kakais nuipu ; sirikiraut ibulesin luka ituŋa .
46007024	Aso iinacan , kosal ŋinidiopet nepepe ka Edeke kwape kenyaraunere .
46007025	Nuka abekon emamei eoŋ aicorakinet naka Ejakait , konye kapesikis yes akiro kwape etuŋanan lomunot kanuka aitim naka Ejakait .
46007026	Aomit eoŋ ebe kanuka ican luka tinenikwana ejok arai kesal ituŋanan kwape ejaar .
46007027	Kirotakinitai kereka jo kaberu ? Sirimoot alacakinio , Emamei kereka jo aberu ? Sirimoot aberu .
46007028	Konye arai imanyi , mam idiakit , arai da edukokin apese , mam ŋin ediakit . Konye luikote nen eanyunete ican luka akuan , ido akoto aiyar yes ŋul .
46007029	Enera na , iinacan , ebe eŋoŋar apak ; kanuka ŋun koraut luejaas kaŋor kwape kaluemameete ,
46007030	luemonyete da kwape kalumam emonyete , ka luiyalamasi kwape kalumam iyalamasi , luegwelete da kwape kaluemameete iboro ,
46007031	luitwasamaete akwap koraut kwape kalumam itwasamaete , Naarai etubor epone loka akwapin kanu .
46007032	Akoto yes koraut lumam iyaloŋoŋoete . Lomam emanyi iyaloŋoŋoi akiro nuka Ejakait , kwape epedoria aitelel Ejakait ;
46007033	konye loamanyit iyaloŋoŋoi akiro nuka akwapin , kwape epedoria aitelel akeberu ,
46007034	ido ejai atiaket . Aberu namam edukokinitai , arai bo apese , iyaloŋoŋoi akiro nuka Ejakait , tetere eraun nakalaunan toma akuanake ka omoyoke da . Kwabo naedukokina iyaloŋoŋoi akiro nuka akwapin , kwape epedoria aitelel okilenike .
46007035	Enera ŋun kodumut yes ajokis , mam akoto ailok yes koic , dimarai aitetemikin nuibusakinito , kijaanakinete Ejakait komamei yenitapaari aomisiokus .
46007036	Arai eomit etuŋanan ebe mam ikonakinit ejok naisinerit , arai imiela noi , ido ibusakinit , aso kiswama ŋesi kwape ekotor , komany ŋes , mam ediaki .
46007037	Konye loicasit kotauke , komamei ibore yenitinaikinit , loepedori ayait akoteke , itogogoŋit da kotauke aricit naisinerit , iswamai ejok .
46007038	Kwaŋin loemanyi naisinerit , iswamai ejok ; lomam emanyi da iswamai ejok aitelekarit .
46007039	Irotakinio aberu kokilenike apak kere naejaria ŋol . Konye arai ketwana okilenike , eosikinitai adukokin loekot , konye toma Ejakait .
46007040	Konye aomit eoŋ ebe iyalama aitelekarit arai esali kwaŋin , Ido aomit ebe ajai kEmoyo loka Ejakait .
46008001	Nuka asuban nueinakinitai aputosia ; kijeni ebe , “ Ejai sio kere aijen . ” Edakunun aijen , konye do eduki amin .
46008002	Arai eomit ituŋanan ebe ejeni akirot , eriŋa ejenuna kwape ibusakinitor ajenun .
46008003	Konye arai emina ituŋanan Edeke , ejeni Edeke ŋin .
46008004	Aso nuka inyamat lueinakinitai aputosia , kijeni ebe , “ Aput mam erai ibore kakwap , ” ido ebe , “ Emamei Edeke dimarai ediopet . ”
46008005	Ido karaida ejaas luemaikinitai idekesio arai toma akuj arai toma akwap , kwape ejaatar “ idekesio ” luipu ka “ ijaka ” luipu ,
46008006	konye kamawok ejai Edeke ediopet bon , ŋes Papa , loeponiata iboro kere kamakeŋ , oni da kirai lukeŋ , ejai da Ejakait ediopet , Yesu Kristo , lokejauniata iboro kere , oni da kirai kanukeŋ .
46008007	Konye ajenun ŋin mam ejai otuŋa kere . Konye ice luenaikinito aputosia kiton kwana , enyamete bala iboro lueinakinio araut asuban mama ejaas aputosia ; ido naarai ekalanyaka aomisiokec , emunaaros .
46008008	Mam inyamat kitojokaarete oni kakonyen nuka Edeke , Arai mam kinyami , mam kitwaniari , arai kinyami da mam kiyatakinio .
46008009	Konye kocoito kinyek akusipedor araun aitiguikinet mama ejaas luekalanyaka .
46008010	Naarai arai keanyu ituŋanan jo loijai kaijen , iboikin ainyam toma abila naka aput , mam kereka aomisio nuka ŋol nuekalanyaka etitiŋikinete ainyam lueinakinio aputosia ?
46008011	Kwaŋin eoliori loekalanyana kanuka akoniijen , ŋope ŋol onace loabu Kristo kotwanik .
46008012	Ido kwaŋin naidiakanariata kama ejaas iinacanakus , ka aimusuŋ akeceomisio nuekalanyaka , idiakanaretc kama ejai Kristo .
46008013	Kanuka ŋun arai itiguikinete inyamat onaceka , abeit mam anyami akiriŋ ikar kere , kenyek aitiguikin onaceka .
46009001	Mam kereka eoŋ ejakakai ? Mam kereka arai ekiyakia ? Mam kereka eoŋ abu kaany Yesu Ejakaitiwok ? Mam kereka yes iraas akaswam toma Ejakait ?
46009002	Naarai arai mam eoŋ arai ekiyakia kama ka ice , konye arai ekiyakia kamakus ; naarai iraas yesi aipucakinet naka ekiyakianekaŋ kotoma Ejakait .
46009003	Ŋin ŋes aboŋokineteka mama ejaas ŋul lukeŋisete .
46009004	Emamei kereka sio apedor ainyam ka aimat ?
46009005	Emamei kereka sio apedor aup kaberu naerai inac , kwape kikiyakia ice , ka iinacan luka Ejakait , ka Kepa da ?
46009006	Arai bo eoŋ bon ka Baranaba emamei apedor ainyein aswam ?
46009007	Eserikalet enyoin elosi ejie kotacakin ŋes elopet ? Iŋai tope irai emusabibu komam enyami araitoke ? Iŋai tope icokiei esipan komam emasi akile nuka esipan ?
46009008	Okwe enera kereka ŋun kotuŋanane ? Arai bo mam inerasi ikisila ŋupe ŋun ?
46009009	Naarai iwadikatai toma okisila luka Musa ebe , “ Sirikien emoŋ loipudapudai aicom akima . ” Epodo kereka Edeke imoŋin ?
46009010	Arai bo inera ŋun kanuwok ? Eebo , iwadikatai kanuwok , naarai ibusakinit ekakorion akor kamun , ekecoman da aicom kamun ebe edumuni ewaike .
46009011	Aso arai kiraikinit yes akiro nuka emoyo , erai ca akirot naepol arai kiidweny nukakuan kamakus ?
46009012	Arai emorete ice apedor ŋin kamakus , mam kereka sio kitelekarit ? Konye mam kitwasamata apedor ŋin , dimarai kiŋirikinit akiro kere , kenyeis aitikokin Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo .
46009013	Mam kereka ijenete ebe luiswamaete aswam naka eyekalu enyamete koboro luka eyekalu , ka ŋul da luijaanakinete kotem ejaas kewaikec kotoma oboro luka etem ?
46009014	Kwape kwaŋin icorakinit Ejakait ebe ŋul luelimonokinete Akiro Nukajokak , ejarete kanuka Akiro Nukajokak .
46009015	Konye mam eoŋ etwasamat akiro ŋun karaida adiopet . Kwabo mam ewadikat ŋun tetere ejaunete kwaŋin kamakaŋ . Naarai ejok eoŋ atwanare itia idiotuŋanan aitapalaun aoloboboteka .
46009016	Naarai arai alimonokini Akiro Nukajokak , emamei eoŋ naaolobobotor . Naarai ketiŋaikinitai . Itukwi eoŋ arai mam eoŋ alimonokini Akiro Nukajokak !
46009017	Naarai arai eswamai ŋun kakoteka , ejai aropio , konye arai mere akoteka , kamunoi kotoma ajokon .
46009018	Aso enyoin kereka ekaropit ? Ŋes lota , ebe , kalimonok Akiro Nukajokak atai , komam etwasamai akapedor kere nakijaar kotoma Akiro Nukajokak .
46009019	Naarai karaida kaosikinitai kotuŋa kere , etuluoro ebulesit loka kere , tetere eriuni luipu aitelekarit .
46009020	Abu karau bala Eyudayat kama ejaas lyudayan , tetere eriuni Iyudayan ; kama kaŋul kalueyaito ikisila , abu karau loeyaito ikisila-karaida mam eoŋ elopet kayaito ikisila-tetere eriuni lueyaito ikisila .
46009021	Kama kaŋul kaluemameete ikisila abu karau loemameete ikisila-mere ŋes amamuut kikisila kama ejai Edeke , konye aricit ikisila luka Kristo-tetere eriuni ŋul luemameete ikisila .
46009022	Abu karau ekalany kama ka luekalanyaka , tetere eriuni luekalanyaka . Karau lokiponesio kere kotuŋa kere , tetere korotin kere ketajar ice .
46009023	Eswamai ŋun kere kanuka Akiro Nukajokak , tetere kimori ka ice kotomakec .
46009024	Mam kereka ijenete ebe lueboloboloete , eboloboloete kere , konye ediopet edumuni ainakinet ? Aso koboloboloete tetere idumunete .
46009025	Yenepega kabolobol eyaikina kakiro kere . Iswamaete ŋul kwaŋin tetere edumunete aboko naemunaar , konye oni namam emunaar .
46009026	Eoŋ da mam aboloboloi atitai , mam anaŋi da bala loenaŋi apak ;
46009027	konye eticani akakuan , ketubulesen ŋes , kenyek kadau alimonokin ice , araun eoŋ elopet loeneritoi .
46010001	Naarai iinacan , akoto yes ajenun ebe abu edou kiteriborite lukapapaakos kere , kitoroto kere aŋolol ,
46010002	aponi kibatisai da kere kama ka Musa kotoma odou kotoma aŋolol da ,
46010003	konyamata da kere inyamat luka emoyo ,
46010004	ido komata kere numatan nuka emoyo . Naarai apotu komata kAtiiba naka emoyo naatupit kes , Atiiba ŋin da kerai Kristo .
46010005	Konye mam Edeke abu kolelakinite luipu kakesi ; naarai aponi komudiarai kamodiŋ .
46010006	Aso keraas akiro ŋun aput mamawok , tetere mam kiraŋai nueroko , kwape kiraŋaata ŋul .
46010007	Sirikiraut luimaete aputosia , kwape ice kakesi ; kwape kiwadikatere ebe , “ Kiboikinos ituŋa ainyam ka aimat , kosodete konyout abolia . ”
46010008	Kwabo sirikidoteata , kwape ice kakesi , kibiroros da ituŋa ilukumin akaisaarei ka luuni kapaaran adiopet .

46015014	Konye arai mam Kristo itajarunitai , aso erai akosilimonokin atitai , akusiiyuun da atitai .
46015015	Ido kitakani kirai ikajenak luka Edeke lukeŋalak , naarai kitejenunit nuka Edeke ebe abu kitajar Kristo , lomam abu kitajar arai mam ikatwak itajarunio .
46015016	Naarai arai mam ikatwak itajarunio , Kristo da mam itajarunitai .
46015017	Ido arai mam Kristo itajarunitai , erai akusiiyuun atitai , isalakinito toma adiakanaretakus .
46015018	Ido ŋul da lukejotooros kotoma Kristo aoliosi .
46015019	Arai kimunokina Kristo kotoma aijar kana bon , kirai lukitimitoi adepar ituŋa kere .
46015020	Konye kwana adau Kristo aitajarunio kokatwak , ŋes araito nugeet nuka ŋul kaluejotooros .
46015021	Naarai kwape ajaunia atwanare kanuka etuŋanan , kwape kwaŋin ajau da ajarun naka lukatwak kanuka etuŋanan ,
46015022	Naarai kwape etwakiata kere kotoma Adam , kwape kwaŋin ejarete da kere kotoma Kristo .
46015023	Konye ŋinituŋanan kwape ebeikinia : Kristo ŋes araito nugeet ; kosodete naebunio ŋesi ŋul lueraas luka Kristo .
46015024	Kosodi edoluni esaŋe , naijaikinia ŋesi Edeke Papa ajakanut ; naedaunia aitapalaun airumit kere , ka apolou kere ka apedor da .
46015025	Naarai ibusakinit ŋes airumit aitodol naicakakinia lukasurupoke kere kwap kakejeneke .
46015026	Lokasurup lokawasia amudiario ŋes atwanare .
46015027	“ Naarai itononokikini Edeke iboro kere kwap kakejeneke . ” Konye naetemaria ebe itononokikinio iboro kere , idelelei ebe mam elimunitoi ŋol lokitononokikini iboro kere .
46015028	Naitononokikinitere iboro kere , ŋes konyet itononokikinitere Okoku da elopet mama ejai ŋol lokitononokikini iboro kere , tetere eraun Edeke loka kere kotoma kere .
46015029	Ikonakinete bo do ai luibatisauna kanuka lukatwak ? Arai mam cut itajarunio ikatwak , kanukinyo kibatisaere kes kanukec ?
46015030	Kanukinyo do kijaar sio ationis ŋolisawa ?
46015031	Iinacan , etogogoŋit kanuka aoloboboteka kanukus nakijaar toma Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok , ebe , atwani ŋinipaaran
46015032	Arai apotu kajioto kitiaŋ kotoma Epeso , kwape etuŋanan , ajokis anyoin ? Arai mam itajarunio ikatwak , aso , “ Kanyama , kamata , naarai kitwaki moi . ”
46015033	Sirikiŋalas ; “ Aup kalueroko emunaari iponesio luejok . ”
46015034	Kikwarut kadolit , ido siridiakanarete , Naarai ejaas ice lumam ejenete Edeke . Enera ŋun aisurumia yes ileic .
46015035	Konye etemari ituŋanan atiar , “ Ikwaikini ai itajarunio lukatwak ? Ido epote kakuan anyoin ? ”
46015036	Ibaŋaana ijo , ŋin yeniyei mam ejari dimikito ketwana .
46015037	Ŋin da yeniyei , mam iyei akuan naejauni , nabarai ikinyomit bon , motoko akimait , arai yenika epone ece .
46015038	Konye Edeke einakini ŋes akuan kwape akotor , einakini ŋolikinyomit akuanake bon .
46015039	Naarai akiriŋ kere mam eputonoro ; konye ejai akiriŋ naka ituŋa , ace naka itiaŋ , ace da naka ikweny , ace da naka lukecor .
46015040	Ejaas da awat nuka akuj , ka awat nuka akwap ; konye aibuses nakokuju erai ace , aibuses da nakokwap erai ace .
46015041	Ejai aibuses naka akoloŋ , aibuses ace naka elap , ka aibuses ace da naka aacer : naarai egelegela aacerit adiopet kaacerit ace kotoma aibuses .
46015042	Ikoni nen ajarun naka lukatwak .
46015043	Eyeio komamei aibuses ; itajarunio kaibuses ; eyeio kakalanyanut ; itajarunio kapedor .
46015044	Eyeio akuan naka akiriŋ ; itajarunio akuan naka emoyo .
46015045	Iwadikatai kwanata ebe , “ Korau etuŋanan losodit Adam ekesa loejari . ” Korau Adam lokawasia emoyo loeinakini aijar ,
46015046	Konye lokemoyo mam kerai losodit , dimarai lokakiriŋ ; kosodi konyet ŋol lokemoyo .
46015047	Abuni etuŋanan losodit kotoma alup , ŋes lokapua ; etuŋanan lokiareit abuni kotoma akuj .
46015048	Kwape ejaar etuŋanan loka apua , ikote nen luka apua ; kwape ejaar da loka akui , ikote nen luka akui .
