50003015	Aso oni kere lukipoloor , kaomitos ŋun ; ido arai iwomitos yesi nuegelara , kipukokini da Edeke yes ŋin .
50003016	Konye ca nukidoloki , kalosenenete kaŋun .
50003017	Iinacan , koputorito eoŋ nepepe , ido kosesenete ŋul luelosete kwape ejaar yes aanyunet kamakosi .
50003018	Naarai elosete luipu , luabu kalimonok yes irwan ipu , kwana da kalimokini kamonyi , ebe kes lukasurupo luka emusalaba loka Kristo .
50003019	Esaŋekec ŋes amudiar , edekekec ŋes akoik , aibusesukec da ejai toma oleic , eomitos nuka akwap .
50003020	Naarai obuwok ejai toma akuj , ŋina da kidareo Eketajaran , Ejakait Yesu Kristo ,
50003021	loilocokini awatewok nuesilok , aputoor akekuan nakaibuses , kwape ejaar aswam naka akepedor aitononokikin iboro kere kwapukeŋ .
50004001	Aso iinacanaka luminan , lukemuit da , akaiyalama ka akaboko da , kobwaata kwaŋin kicasito kotoma Ejakait , luminan ,
50004002	Eŋaiŋait Euodia , eŋaiŋait da Suntuke , kojaas kaomit adiopet , kotoma Ejakait .
50004003	Eebo , kelipit jo da , ekiŋariŋaret ajookot lokabeit , kiŋarak aŋor ŋun , nuetaaritos nenipe keoŋ toma Akiro Nukajokak , ka Kelement da , ka ikeswamak ice da lukaupaka , luejaas ikiroriakec toma oitabo loka aijar .
50004004	Kiyalamas kotoma Ejakait apaarasia kere ; abala bobo ebe kiyalamas .
50004005	Kojenun akusiiyapaara kotuŋa kere . Eapie Ejakait .
50004006	Siriyaloŋoŋoete akirot kere , konye kotoma akiro kere toma ailip ka aiŋaiŋa nepepe kaimal , kitejenut Edeke nuikotosi .
50004007	Ainapakin da naka Edeke naedeparit ajenun kere , kidarenenei itauonokus ka aomisiokus kotoma Kristo Yesu .
50004008	Nuesalito iinacan , nueraas nukabeit kere , nuibusakinito kere , nuedolito kere , nukalaunak kere , nutemela kere , nuisupete kere , arai ejai ajokis kere , ido arai ejai aiturit , koomoomoete ŋun .
50004009	Akiro da nuipotu kisisiata kamakaŋ , kodumutu da , kopuputu da , koanyutu da kamakaŋ , kiswamaenenete ŋun ; ejaenena da Edeke loka ainapakin kayes .
50004010	Konye eyalama noi kotoma Ejakait , naarai kwana atubor apak ekwarutu da akusiwomisio kanukaŋ , kwabo ipotu koomitos ŋun konye kemamei yes apak .
50004011	Mere ebe enera kanuka eipud ; naarai abu kesisia adauna kwape ajaar kere .
50004012	Ajeni aitisilio , ajeni da alitoro ; kaŋinikirot , ido kotoma akiro kere , ketuutooritai aiyeiyea naka aimonikin ka ariebo eteŋei da , alitoro ka aiŋonara da .
50004013	Apedorit kere kotoma kaŋol kaloketogogoni .
50004014	Konye ipotu kiswamata ejok naimorikikinotor kaiticaniokaŋ .
50004015	Ijenete yesi da Ipilipin ebe , kotoma ageunet naka Akiro Nukajokak , naanyounio koMakedonia , amamei ekanisa loemorikikina keoŋ kotoma akirot naka aikor ka aijaun , dimarai yes bonik ,
50004016	naarai koSesalonika da ipotu kijukakis eoŋ irwan atipet ka nakiareit kanuka eipudika .
50004017	Mere naarai amoot ainakinet , konye amoot araito nuiyatanakinos otiaikus .
50004018	Konye ajai kiboro kere , alitoro da ; etekoro , kadau aijaun lukijukunete kama ka Epapurodito , aures naeuru maa , asubanit naecamunitai naitojokit Edeke .
50004019	Ekadeke da itekori luipudasi kere kwape ejaar akebar kotoma aibuses toma Kristo Yesu .
50004020	Kojai aibuses mama ejai Edeke Papawok ikar ka ikar . Amen .
50004021	Kiyogaete ŋinikalaunan kere kotoma Kristo Yesu . Kiyogaete yes iinacan luejaas keoŋ .
50004022	Kiyogaete yes lukalaunak kere , aitelekarit ŋul lukokal loka Kaisar .
50004023	Asianut naka Ejakait Yesu Kristo kojai kimoyonokus .
51001001	Paul ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kanuka akot naka Edeke , ka Timoteo onacewok .
51001002	Mama ejaas lukalaunak ka iinacan luiyuunito lukotoma Kristo luejaas Kolosai : Asianut ka ainapakin kojaas mama ijaas nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papawok .
51001003	Kimalaenenei Edeke Papa loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo apaarasia kere nakilipanakinia yes ,
51001004	naarai kipou keirasi nuka aiyuunikus kotoma Kristo Yesu , ka aminakus mama ejaas lukalaunak kere ,
51001005	naejai kanuka amun naiŋadakinio toma akuj kanukus . Ipotu kiirasi ŋin kolo toma akirot naka abeit naka Akiro Nukajokak ,
51001006	nuadolokis yes ; ido kwape eraiata araito , iyatanakinos da kotoma akwapin kere , kwape kwaŋin kotomakus da , ameun kapaaran naipupioto , kojenut da asianut naka Edeke kabeit ,
51001007	kwape isisiaata kama ka Epapurasi ebulesit aupawok lominat . Erai ŋesi ekejaanakinan lomunot loka Kristo kanukosi ,
51001008	lokitejenik da sio akusimin kotoma Omoyo .
51001009	Kanuka ŋun sio da , ameun kapaaran nakipupunio , mam kinyeinenei ailipanakin yes kaiŋaiŋa ebe , kilelebikin ajenun nuekoto Edeke , kacoa kere , ka acoit naka emoyo ,
51001010	kolosenenete kwape luibusakinito Ejakait aisiyalamikin ŋes kakiro kere , koraete araito kotoma kaŋiniswam kere naejok , kiyatanakinos da ajenun Edeke .
51001011	Kitogogoŋoi kapedor kere , kwape ejaar agogoŋ naka aibusesuke , kiton atitiŋikinit kere , ka aikany da nepepe kaiyalama ,
51001012	kimalaenenete Papa lokitubusikinit oni aimor kairumet naka lukalaunak kotoma aica .
51001013	Abu ŋesi kolaku oni alemar kapolou naka amuton , kisibwot alomar ajakanut naka Okokuke lominat .
51001014	Kija kalakunio kotomakeŋ , ŋes aisionio naka adiakanareta .
51001015	Erai ŋesi aput naka Edeke lomam etakani , ekiyai loka isuban kere ;
51001016	naarai kotomakeŋ ŋes kesubere iboro kere , luejaas toma akuj , ka luejaas toma akwap , luetakanete ka lumam etakanete , arai iicoloŋo lukajakanuto , arai ijaka , arai ikayaitok , arai lukapolou , kesubio iboro kere kotomakeŋ ido kanukeŋ .
51001017	Egeikinit ŋesi iboro kere , icasito da iboro kere nepepe kotomakeŋ .
51001018	Erai ŋesi da akou naka akuan , ŋes ekanisa ; erai ŋesi ageunet , ekiyai kotoma okatwak , tetere eraun ŋesi elopet losodit kotoma kere .
51001019	Naarai kotomakeŋ kitojokit aitekoro naka Edeke aiboienen ,
51001020	kotomakeŋ da aitupuc iboro kere mamakeŋ , arai luejaas akwap , arai da luejaas akuj , kisinapik kanuka aokot nuka emusalabake .
51001021	Ka yes da lukolo igelara , lukasurup da kaomisiokus , kaswamisio nueroko , konye kwana abu ŋesi kitupuc yes
51001022	kotoma akekuan naka etuŋanan , kanuka aketwanare , tetere kitodiari yes lukalaunak , luemamei akemer ka luemamei aitoronet da kakonyeneke ,
51001023	arai bo isalenenete kotoma aiyuun , iketakina apetetaitikus , icasito komam iriaŋiriaŋas , ainyein amun naka Akiro Nukajokak nuipotu kopuput , nuaponi kolimonokin ŋinisubat kere yenejai kwap kakuj , nuabu karaunor eoŋ , Paul , ekejaanakinanikec .
51001024	Kwana eyalamikin arieboka kanukus , etodoli da nuikadidio nuka aiticanio naka Kristo toma akuanaka kanuka akuanake , ŋes ekanisa ,
51001025	lokaraunor eoŋ ekekejaanakinan kwape ejaar aijokokinet naka Edeke nakainakinitai kanukus , aitodolikin akirot naka Edeke ,
51001026	aiyeiyea nakibwaitai ameun kikar ka aturio da , konye kwana ikujokinitai mama ejaas lukalaunakake .
51001027	Abu Edeke kokoto kes aitejenikin Imo abar kwape ejaar naka aibuses naka aiyeiyea kaŋin , naerai Kristo kotomakus , amun naka aibuses .
51001028	Kilimonokini ŋes , kekwenya ŋinituŋanan , kisisianakini da ŋinituŋanan kacoa kere , tetere kitodiari ŋinituŋanan epol kotoma Kristo .
51001029	Kanuka ŋun ŋes etaaritor aut kwape ejaar akegogoŋ naiswamai kotomakaŋ kapedor .
51002001	Naarai akoto yes ajenun aut naetia nen naauta kanukus , kanuka ŋul da luejaas Laodikia , ka ŋul kere lumam eanyunito akakonyen toma akuan ;
51002002	tetere italakario ikecetauon , inicakina kotoma amin , koanyut abar kere naka acoit naitogogoŋitoi , kojenut cut aiyeiyea naka Edeke , ŋes Kristo ,
51002003	loibwaitai kotomakeŋ iboro kere luketiai loepol luka acoa ka ajenun da .
51002004	Enera ŋun kinyek idiotuŋanan aitapaar yes kakiro nuka aijodijod .
51002005	Naarai karaida amamei eoŋ kotoma akuan , konye ajai kayes kotoma omoyo , eyalama da aanyun ekusipone loeteni ka aicasit naka aiyuunikus kotoma Kristo .
51002006	Aso kwape ijauniata Kristo Yesu Ejakait , kolosenenete kwaŋin kotomakeŋ ;
51002007	kicasito aliasiokus , kodukokina kotomakeŋ , ido kitogogoŋitete kotoma aiyuun , kwape kisisianakinere , kilapara kaimal .
51002008	Kocoito kinyek idiotuŋanan aŋatar yes kanuka aminacoa ka aiŋal naatai , kwape ejaatar iponesio luka ituŋa , kwape ejaatar nugeet nuka akwapin , kwabo mere kwape ejaar Kristo .
51002009	Naarai kotomakeŋ iboie aitekoro kere naka Eidekeone kakuan ,
51002010	yes da itekoro kotomakeŋ , loerai akou naka ayait kere ka apolou da .
51002011	Kotomakeŋ da kikepitai yes kakepio namam iswamatai kakanin , ilacata akuan naka etuŋanan kotoma akepio naka Kristo ;
51002012	kinukio nepepe kaŋes kaibatis , kaŋin da aponi kitajarun nepepe kaŋes , kanuka aiyuun aswam naka Edeke lokitajaruni ŋes kokatwak .
51002013	Yes da lukitwakito kotoma aibucanareta , ka amamus akepio naka awatekus , abu Edeke koinak yes aijar nepepe kaŋes , kedau ŋesi aisioni oni aibucanaretawok kere ,
51002014	kedau aimwatar aitutuket naewadikatai toma okisila nakitusurupi oni ; abu kolema awai , kibubuk omusalaba .
51002015	Kolaca ŋesi ikayaitok ka lukapolou kitodia kes katitiŋ , kipiko kes komusalaba .
51002016	Aso kinyek idiotuŋanan atubokin yes kakiro nuka inyamat , arai numatan , arai bo kakiro nuka epucit , karaida ailamun naka elap , karaida nuka apaaran nakasabato .
51002017	Eraas nu etoribe loka nuepote ; konye akuan ŋes naka Kristo .
51002018	Kinyek idio ademar ainakinetekus , yenekoto aitisilikin , ka aima imalaikan , kitogogoŋooro kaitapoeta , iturokina atai kanuka aomisioke nuka akuan ,
51002019	kwabo mam iketakina Akou , lokotomakeŋ akuan kere isigalikinio ka ainicakinio kanuka ailenyeta ka amoori , iyatanakin keiyas loka Edeke .
51002020	Arai ipotu kotwaka nepepe ka Kristo ainyein nugeet nuka akwapin , kanukinyo inonokikinitotor ikisila bala iroko ijarete kotoma akwapin ,
51002021	ebe , “ Sirikitiŋ , Sirikiir , Sirikitiro ” ,
51002022	( ŋul kere eoliorete toma aitwasamao ) atupar aicorakineta ka aisisianakin naka ituŋa ?
51002023	Akiro ŋun kere ejai aput naka acoa kotoma aima naepwakunete ituŋa bonik , ka aitisilikin , ka aitican akuan ; emamei ŋun ajokis nepetai da aitikokinia aiŋobel naka akuan .
51003001	Aso arai kitajarunitai nepepe ka Kristo , komoenenete nuejaas kuju , neejai Kristo , iboie kakan nakoteten naka Edeke .
51003002	Koomoomoete nuejaas kuju , kwabo mere nuejaas akwap .
51003003	Naarai ipotu kotwaka , ibwaitai da akusiijar nepepe ka Kristo , toma Edeke .
51003004	Naetakanunia Kristo , ŋes aijarawok , kosodete yesi da itakanunete nepepe kaŋes kotoma aibuses .
51003005	Aso kitwataniasi akusitutubeta nuejaas akwap ; adoteu , asilianut , ainekit , eimiel loerono , ka airaŋaanut , ŋes aima aputosia .
51003006	Kanuka ŋun ŋes ebunokinia anyunyura naka Edeke odwe luiulaka .
51003007	Ipotu yesi da kolosenenete kolo kaŋun , naijariata kotomakec .
51003008	Konye yes da kwana kolemasi ŋun kere awai ; anyunyura , adedeŋ , aronis , ainyanakin , einer nukileic kaitukekus .
51003009	Siriŋalaŋalas , naarai ipotu kolacasi etuŋanan lokolo nepepe kaswamisioke ,
51003010	konapa da etuŋanan lokitetet loisiteteununio kiton ajenun kwape ejaar aput naka ŋol lokesubi ŋes .
51003011	Emamei kanen Eyonanit , karaida Eyudayat , akepio ka amamus akepio , imoit , Esukusit , ibulesit , karaida yenijakakai , konye Kristo ŋes kere , ejai da kotoma kere .
51003012	Aso konapenenete etau loka aitim , asianut , aitasono , aiyapepera , atitiŋikin , kwape luseuna luka Edeke , lukalaunak ka luminan da ;
51003013	koŋirionokinos , kisionionoros , arai ejai ituŋanan kere aŋurian kayenice , ido kwape kisionio yes Ejakait , yes da kisioniete kwape kwaŋin .
51003014	Ido aitelekarit ŋun kere konapa amin , naerai elomorut loka adolior .
51003015	Kodiekenenei ainapakin naka Kristo kotoma otauonokus , nakinyarakinio da toma akuan adiopet , kimalaenenete da .
51003016	Kiboienenei akirot naka Kristo kabarara kotomakus , kacoa kere : kisisianakinete ido kikwenyanaros kisabulin , ka ikososio , ka nupwakan nuka emoyo ; iyeonokinete Edeke kasianut kotoma otauonokus .
51003017	Ido nuiswamaenenete kere kakirot arai kaswam , kiswamaenenete kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu , kimalaenenete Edeke Papa kotomakeŋ .
51003018	Yes aŋor , kononokikis ikusikiliok , kwape ibusakinitor kotoma Ejakait .
51003019	Yes ikiliok , kominas akusiŋor , siridedeŋanakinete kes .
51003020	Yes idwe , korimasi ikusikauriak kotoma akiro kere , naarai ŋin itojokit Ejakait .
51003021	Yes lukapapa , sirikitunyunyuranakis ikusidwe , kinyeis ajuruŋuŋ .
51003022	Yes ibulesin , korimasi ikusijaka luka akuan kotoma akiro kere ; mere kaijaanakin nakokuju kwape luitojokito ituŋa , dimarai kaipioror nakotau , koyoŋito Ejakait ,
51003023	Yeniswamaete kere , kiswamaenenete kaijar kere , bala iswamanakinete Ejakait kwabo mere ituŋa ,
51003024	Kojenete ebe kiinakini Ejakait eropit loka airumet ; ijaanakinete Ejakait Kristo .
51003025	Naarai yeniswamai erono , etacakinio bobo kwape ejaar akeronis , ido emamei atiakit ituŋa .
51004001	Yes ijaka , kokorakis ikusibulesin nukadolit ka aitiirian , kojenete ebe ejai yes da Ejakait toma akuj .
51004002	Kicebokinito kotoma ailip , kokwenyenenete kotomake kaimal .
51004003	Kilipanakinete sio da , ebe koŋaik Edeke sio ekek kanuka akirot , einer aiyeiyea naka Kristo , nakaenitere eoŋ kanukeŋ ;
51004004	tetere etodiari kwape kebusakinitor einer .
51004005	Kolosenenete kacoa mama ejaas ŋul lukokiŋa , koyuununete apak .
51004006	Kinerenenasi apaarasia kere kasianut , kokonyite abalaŋ , tetere ijenete kwape ibusakinitor aboŋonokin ŋinituŋanan .
51004007	Kitejenikini yes Tukiko nukadoikis kere ; erai ŋesi onace lominat ka ekejaanakinan lomunot , ido ebulesit aupakosi kotoma Ejakait .
51004008	Ejuk ŋes mamakus kanuka akirot kana , tetere ijenunete nukidoikis sio , ido kitalaka ŋesi ikusitauon ,
51004009	nepepe ka Onesimo , onace lomunot ka lominat da , lokobukus . Kitejenikinete kesi yes akiro kere nukane .
51004010	Kiyogai yes Arisitariko , ekijoreoritono aupaka , ka Marako ecen loka Baranaba , ( Ioaponi kicorakin yes kanukeŋ ; arai ebuni mamakus , kisukunyikis ŋes ) ,
51004011	ka Yesu loenyaritai Yusito , Eraas lu lukotoma luekepitai , kes bonik ikeswamak lukaupaka kanuka ajakanut naka Edeke , luapotu ketalakasi eoŋ noi .
51004012	Kiyogai yes Epapurasi , loerai lokobukus , ebulesit loka Kristo Yesu , euta apaarasia kere kanukus kotoma ailipike , tetere ibwoenenete kopolok , kitogogoŋito da kere nuekot Edeke .
51004013	Naarai etejenaara kanukeŋ ebe itaaritoi ŋesi noi kanukus , kanuka luko Laodikia da , kanuka luko Kierapoli da .
51004014	Kiyogai yes Luka emurwon lominat , ka Dema da .
51004015	Kiyogaete iinacan luejaas Laodikia , Numpa da ka ekanisa loejai togoke .
51004016	Ido naidauniata yesi asoman ebalua lo , kosiomata da kotoma okanisa loka Laodikia ; kosiomata yesi da loebuni koLaodikia .
51004017	Kolimokis da Arikipo ebe , “ Kocoite aijaanakin naibu kodum kotoma Ejakait , tetere itodoli . ”
51004018	Eoŋ Paul ewadikai ayogan na kakakan elopet . Kiitununete akaenio . Asianut kojai mama ijaas .
52001001	Paul ka Siluano ka Timoteo , mama ejai ekanisa loka Isesalonikan kotoma Edeke Papa ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo : Asianut kojai mama ijaas ka ainapakin .
52001002	Kimalaenenei Edeke kanukus kere apaarasia kere , kilimununei yes kotoma ailipikosi ,
52001003	komam kinyeinenei aiitunun kakonyen nuka Edeke Papawok aswamukus naka aiyuun , ka aitaaritoi naka amin , ka atitiŋikin da naka amuno naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo ,
52001004	Naarai iinacan luemina Edeke , kijeni aseuniokus ;
52001005	naarai Akosikiro Nukajokak mam apotu kodolokis yes kotoma akirot bon , dimarai kotoma apedor , ido kotoma Omoyo Lokalaunan , ido kaitogogoŋio naepol , kwape ijeniata epone lokitodiaror tomakus kanukus .
52001006	Ido ipotu koputosi sio ka Ejakait , naarai ijaut akirot kotoma aiticanio naepol , kaiyalama naka Emoyo Lokalaunan ;
52001007	kosodete araun aanyunet mama ejaas luiyuunito kere kotoma Makedonia ka Akaia da .
52001008	Naarai anyoun kamakus epup akirot naka Edeke , mere kotoma Makedonia ka Akaia bon , dimarai isiarakina akusiiyuun kotoma Edeke ŋiniibois kere , emamei bobo sio eipud einer akirot kere .
52001009	Naarai alimosi kesi ikulepek akirokosi kwape kiilomunia mamakus , ido kwape ibelokinotor mama ejai Edeke , kinyeis aputosia , tetere ijaanakinete Edeke lokajaran lokabeit ,
52001010	ka aidareun Okokuke abunore kokuju , lokitajaruni ŋesi kokatwak , ŋes Yesu lokiyuuni oni kotoma anyunyura naebunit .
52002001	Naarai ijenete yesi iinacan , ebe akosilomun mamakus mam kerai atai ;
52002002	konye karaida kiiticanitai ka aiswamakinio da nukepali koPilipi , kwape ijeniata , kipou katitiŋikisi kotoma Edekewok , alimonokin yes Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke kauta naepol .
52002003	Naarai alimonokinikosi mam erai naka aiŋal , karaida naka asilianut , karaida kotoma aimod ,
52002004	konye kwape kicamakinia Edeke isio araut lukimunoi kotoma Akiro Nukajokak , kwape kwaŋin kinerar , mere aitalakar ituŋa , dimarai aitalakar Edeke loiteteni itauonokosi .
52002005	Naarai mam kijaa kakiro nuisupete apakio kere , kwape ijeniata , karaida nuerapete airaŋaanut , erai Edeke ekajenan ;
52002006	mam kipou kamootos aibuses kama kituŋa , karaida kamakus , karaida kama kice , nakipedoria alaŋirikinit yes , kwape ikiyakia luka Kristo .
52002007	Konye kipou keyapeperas kokidiŋikus , kwape akasaan naitani ikedwe alopet .
52002008	Kwaŋin kipodori yes , ketojokata akorakin yes mere Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke bon , konye akosiijar da , naarai iraas iminanakosi noi .
52002009	Naarai , iinacan , iitunito yesi akosiitaaritoi ka ailolony ; nakiswamaenena akuare ka apaaran da , kenyeis alaŋirikin ituŋanan kere kayesi , kalimonokinete yes Akiro Nukajokak nuka Edeke .
52002010	Iraas yesi ikajenak , ka Edeke da , kwape kijaar kamakus luiyuunito kalaunit , ka adolit , komamei aitoronet ;
52002011	kwape ijeniata yesi ebe , kwape icoria papa ikedwe , kipou kecorata ŋinidiopet kayesi , kesinyikokito , ka aitejenun da ,
52002012	tetere ilosenenete kwape luibusakinito Edeke , lokinyarit yes alomar toma ajakanutuke ka aibuses da .
52002013	Kanuka ŋun da kimalaenenei Edeke tiritir , naarai naijauniata akirot naka Edeke naipupunete kamakosi , ipotu kocamut , mere kwape akirot naka ituŋa , konye kwape eraar abeit akirot naka Edeke , naiswamai da kotomakus kaluiyuunito .
52002014	Naarai , iinacan , ipotu koputosi ikanisan luka Edeke lukotoma Kristo Yesu , Iuejaas Yudaya ; naarai apotu ikusituŋa kiticanata yes da , kwape eticaniata Iyudayan lukec ;
52002015	luapotu koarata Ejakait Yesu ka inabin da , ido kireŋeto sio , kwabo mam kes isiyalamikinito Edeke , isuruposi kituŋa kere ,
52002016	kirebokinito da sio alimonokin Imo tetere itajario , kosodete aitodolikin adiakanaretakec apaarasia kere . Konye ekokoikin kes cut anyunyura naka Edeke .
52002017	Konye iinacan , kipou isio katiakasi kayes apak naedit , kakonyen , kwabo mere kotauon , kipou kadunyakis noi noi aanyun akusikonyen kaimue naepol ;
52002018	naarai kipou kakotosi aponare mamakus , eoŋ Paul , irwan nasodit ka nakiareit da , konye kitikok Satan sio .
52002019	Naarai inyo bo amunokosi , arai aiyalama , arai aboko naka aolobob kakonyen nuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu kotoma abunoreke ? Mere yes ?
52002020	Naarai iraas yesi akosiibuses ka aiyalama da .
52003001	Kanuka ŋun namam bobo kipedoria atitiŋikin , kipou ketojokata ainyeinio bon ko Asene ,
52003002	kejukas Timoteo onacekosi ido ekejaanakinan loka Edeke toma Akiro Nukajokak nuka Kristo , tetere iticasi yes ka uitalakar da kotoma aiyuunikus ,
52003003	kinyek ituŋanan kere airiaŋiriaŋa kotoma aiticanio kana . Naarai ijenete yesi ebe kitebeitai ŋin .
52003004	Naarai nakijaar kayes , kipou kekwenyasi yes ebe kidumuni aiticanio ; kwape kedounio da , ido kwape ijeniata .
52003005	Kanuka ŋun namam bobo apedoria atitiŋikin , abu kejuk kasodi ajenun aiyuunikus , kinyek ekacodan acodun yes , aitaaritoikosi da koraun natitai .
52003006	Konye kwana naadolunio Timoteo mamakosi ebuni kamakus , abu koinu sio akiro nukajokak nuka aiyuunikus ka aminakus , ebe da kiitununete yesi sio ejok apaarasia kere , kimuito aanyun sio , kwape sio da yes , —
52003007	kanuka ŋun , iinacan , kitalakaritai kanukus kotoma aridakiniokos kere ka aiticanio , kanuka aiyuunikus ,
52003008	naarai kwana kijari arai ibwoete yesi icasito kotoma Ejakait .
52003009	Naarai aimal anyoin kipedori atacakin Edeke kanukus , kanuka aiyalama kere nakiyalamar kanukus kakonyen nuka Edekewok ,
52003010	kidunyakinit ailip akuare ka apaaran da ebe kaanyut akusikonyen , ka aitemonokin nuiŋoŋara kotoma aiyuunikus ?
52003011	Konye Edeke elopet Papawok ka Ejakaitiwok Yesu kiteten ekosirot aponare mamakus ;
52003012	Ejakait da koinak yes aiyatanakin ka aidilakin aminanar bonik , ka ituŋa kere , kwape sio da kiminar yes ,
52003013	tetere kiticat ikusitauon koraas Iuemamei aitoronet kotoma alaunit kakonyen nuka Edeke Papawok , naebunio Ejakaitiwok Yesu nepepe kalukalaunakake kere .
52004001	Nuesalito , iinacan , kiŋaiŋait yes ka aicor da kotoma Ejakait Yesu , kwape kijauniata kamakosi kwape ibusakinitor yes alosenen ka aisiyalamikinit Edeke , kwape ilosenenoto , kiyatanakinos bobo kwaŋin ,
52004002	Naarai ijenete kwape ejaatar aicorakineta nukipou kainakis yes kanuka Ejakait Yesu .
52004003	Naarai naekoto Edeke ŋes nata , aitalauniokus : kinacata adoteu ;
52004004	kojenu ŋinituŋanan kayesi ajaut kakeberu kotoma alaunite ka ayoŋit ,
52004005	mere kotoma ainekit naka eimiel kwape ikapirin Iumam ejenete Edeke ;
52004006	kinyek ediotuŋanan aibucar karaida airod onaceke kotoma akirot , naarai erai Ejakait ekenyaŋan kotoma kaŋun kere , kwape kipou kekwenyariata yes ka aitejenun da noi .
52004007	Naarai mam Edeke kinyarakinit oni asilianut , dimarai toma alaunit .
52004008	Aso yeneŋeri , mam eŋeri etuŋanan dimarai Edeke , lokiinakini yes Ekemoyo Lokalaunan .
52004009	Konye nuka amin iinacan mam ipudasi eoŋ aiwadikakin yes , naarai kisisianakinit Edeke yes aminanara ;
52004010	naarai iswamanakinete akirot ŋin iinacan kere luejaas Makedonia kere , Konye , iinacan , keŋaiŋait yes kiyatanakinos adepar nen ,
52004011	koŋaŋato aiyapaara , kiswamaenenete nukus bonik , kitaaritos da kakusikanin , kwape kipou kecorakiniata yes ,
52004012	tetere ilosenenete koponesio luejok kama kalukokina komam ilwaritos .
52004013	Konye iinacan , mam kikoto yes aolit nuka ŋul kaluejotoete , tetere mam itururwete kwape ice luemamei amun .
52004014	Naarai arai kiyuunit ebe abu Yesu kotwana , kojaru da , kwape kwaŋin kanuka Yesu eyauni Edeke nepepe kaŋes ŋul luejotoete .
52004015	Naarai kilimokini yes na kakirot naka Ejakait , ebe onilukijari lukipaikinit kiton abunore naka Ejakait , mam kigeikini luejotoete .
52004016	Naarai edokuni Ejakait elopet abunore kotoma akuj kaiworo , keporoto loka emalaika lokapolon , ka arupepe naka Edeke . Ŋul da luketwakete kotoma Kristo , kes eliŋete ajarun ;
52004017	kosodi konyet oni lukijari , lukipaikinit , kiwuruporio nepepe kakes toma odoun , airiamun ka Ejakait toma apak ; kwaŋin kijaenena ka Ejakait apaarasia kere .
52004018	Aso kitalakanaros bonik kakiro kaŋun .
52005001	Konye iinacan , mam ipudasi eoŋ aiwadikakin yes nuka apakio ka ikar .
52005002	Naarai ijenete yesi jokan ebe ebuni apaaran naka Ejakait kwape ekokolan kuare .
52005003	Naineratar ebe , “ Ejai ainapakin ka aiyamakina , ” eŋesakin do kes amudiar kwape eŋesakinor ariebo aberu naidouni , kwa bo mam ekuete nepepec da .
52005004	Konye iinacan , mam ijaas amuton , apaaran ŋin aturiaikin yes kwape ekokolan .
52005005	Naarai iraas yesi kere odwe luka aica , ka odwe luka apaaran ; mam oni kirai luka akuar karaida luka amuton .
52005006	Aso do kenyeisi ajotoor kwape ka ice , konye kakwenyenenete , kenyeis amer ,
52005007	Naarai luejotoete , ejotoete kuare , luemerasi da emerasi kuare .
52005008	Konye do oni kirai luka apaaran , kenyeis amer , kanapa yenikatorob yenika aiyuun ka amin , akopira da korai amun naka aitajario .
52005009	Naarai mam Edeke kibwaikinit oni kanuka anyunyura , dimarai adumun aitajario kanuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo ,
52005010	loabu kotwanik oni tetere kijari nepepe kaŋes , arai kikwenyi , arai bo kijotoi .
52005011	Aso kitalakanaros bonik , kodukonoros ŋinituŋanan kayenice , kwape iswamaata da .
52005012	Konye iinacan , kiŋaiŋait yes ajenun ŋul Iuitaaritos kotomakus , lukiyaito yes kotoma Ejakait , ka lukicorete da ,
52005013	koyoŋito kes noi kamin kanuka aswamukec , Kojaas kainapakina kotomakus .
52005014	Konye iinacan , kiŋaiŋait yes , kicorata luitotolikino , kiticasete luipirisiaros itauon , kisigalikis luekalanyaka , kotitiŋikis ituŋa kere .
52005015	Koanyutu ebe emamei yenetacakini aronis kanuka aronis , konye komootos apaarasia kere aikonanakin lucekus ejok , ka ituŋa da kere .
52005016	Kiyalamasi apaarasia kere ,
52005017	kilipenenete tiritir ,

52005023	Edeke da elopet loka ainapakin kitalau yes cut , kidaritete cut imoyonokus , ka aijarakus , ka awatekus da , komamei aitoronet kiton naebunio Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo .
52005024	Lokinyarit yes erai lomunot , ido ebuni aswam .

53001001	Paul , ka Siluano , ka Timoteo , Mama ejai ekanisa loka Isesalonikan lokotoma Edeke Papawok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo :
53001002	Asianut kojai mama ijaas ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papa ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo .
53001003	Iinacan , kiburao sio aimalaenen Edeke apaarasia kere kanukus , kwape kibusakinitor , naarai iyata noi akusiiyuun , idila da akusiminanar ŋinituŋanan kayesi kere mama kayenice .
53001004	Kiton sio da kiwolobobot kanukus kotoma okanisan luka Edeke kanuka atitiŋikinikus , ka aiyuun kotoma areokus kere , ka aiticanio naiŋirikinito .
53001005	Ŋes aanyunet cut naka etube loedolit loka Edeke , kosodete kitubusikin yes ajakanut naka Edeke , nakiticanere yes kanuke .
53001006	Naarai edolit kakonyen nuka Edeke atacakin aiticanio lukiticanete yes ,
53001007	yes da luiticanio kisiyeŋunio nepepe kasio , kotoma apukorio naka Ejakait Yesu naebunio kotoma akuj nepepe ka imalaikan luka akepedor , kotoma akim naesarani ,
53001008	inyaŋi kama kaŋul lumam ejenete Edeke , ka ŋul da lumam erimarito Akiro Nukajokak nuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu .
53001009	Egelitikec ŋes amudiario naka ikar kere , enyounete kakonyen nuka Ejakait , ka aibuses naka agogoŋuke da ,
53001010	naebunio ŋesi kapaaran kaŋin , tetere itopoloorio kotoma kalukalaunakake , ka aumokinio da kotoma kaluiyuunito kere , naarai iyuunitos yesi akosiitejenun .
53001011	Tape da kilipanakini yes apaarasia kere , tetere kitubusik yes Ewokodeke kanyariteke , kitodolik da kapedor ŋiniwomisioit kere nakajokis , ka aswam da naka aiyuun ,
53001012	tetere itopoloorio ekiror loka Ejakaitiwok Yesu kotomakus , yes da kotomakeŋ , kwape ejaar asianut naka Edekewok ka Ejakait Yesu Kristo .
53002001	Konye iinacan , kiŋaiŋait yes , kakiro nuka abunore naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo , ka atukonokiniwok nepepe kaŋes ,
53002002	kinyeis aisunyit airiaŋiriaŋa kotoma aomisiokus , karaida aiyaloŋoŋ , karaida komoyo , karaida kakirot , karaida kobalua loebuni kamakosi , ebe adolu apaaran naka Ejakait .
53002003	Kinyek idiotuŋanan aitapaar yes kopone kere ; naarai mam apaaran ŋin ebuni , dimarai isiauni atiakatiakaun ajaun , epukorio da etuŋanan ŋol lokepali , okoku loka amudiar ,
53002004	loirebirebi , ido loitopoloor bon aitelekarit ibore kere yenenyaritai edeke , arai yenemaio ; kosodi iboikin oyekalu loka Edeke , kitodiara ebe ŋes Edeke .
53002005	Mam kereka iitunito ebe nakijaar kayes abu kalimok yes ŋun ?
53002006	Ido ijenete yenitikokinit kwana , tetere epukorio ŋes kapakike .
53002007	Naarai ageu aiyeiyea naka epali aswam ; konye loitikokinit kwana iswamai aitodol naelemarere ŋol awai .
53002008	Kosodi konyet epukorio lokepali , eari Ejakait Yesu ŋes keiyeŋane loka aitukuke , ka amudiar da kotoma atakanun naka abunoreke .
53002009	Abunore naka ŋol lokepali naiswamai Satan ejaun kapedor kere , kaanyuneta ka nukaumokin da nukeŋalak ,
53002010	ka aitapaar kere namam adolit mama ejaas ŋul lueoliorito , naarai mam apotu kocamut amin abeit , kosodete aitajario .
53002011	Kanuka ŋun ijukakini kes Edeke aswam naka apaar , tetere iyunete nuka aiŋal ,
53002012	tetere etubokinio kere lumam iyuunito abeit , konye luisiyalamikinito amamus adolit .
53002013	Konye kiburao sio aimalaenen Edeke apaarasia kere kanukus , iinacan luemina Ejakait , naarai abu Edeke koseik yes ameun kageunet aitajario , kanuka aitalaunio naka Emoyo , ka aiyuun da abeit .
53002014	Abu konyarak yes ŋin kanuka Akosikiro Nukajokak , kanuka adumun aibuses naka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo .
53002015	Aso do iinacan , kobwaata kicasito , kikamut iponesio lukisisianakinitai , arai kotoma akirot , arai kotoma obaluakosi .
53002016	Konye Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo elopet , ka Edeke Papawok , lokimina oni , loabu koinak da aitalakar naka ikar kere , ka amun naejok kotoma asianut ,
53002017	kitalaka ikusitauon , kiticat da kotoma kaŋiniswam ka ŋinikirot da naejok .
53003001	Nuesalito , iinacan , kilipanakinai sio , tetere ekeri akirot naka Ejakait , koinakinai aibuses , kwape kotomakus ,
53003002	isio da kayuunos kama ka ituŋa luemamei acoa , ikaronok ; naarai ejaas ice lumam iyuunito .
53003003	Konye erai Ejakait lomunot ; lokiticasi yes , kidari da kama ka lokaronon .
53003004	Konye kija kamun kotoma Ejakait kakirokus , ebe iswamaete , ido ipote aswam nukicorakini .
53003005	Konye kiteten Ejakait ikusitauon toma amin naka Edeke , ka atitiŋikin da naka Kristo .
53003006	Konye iinacan , kicorakini yes kokiror loka Ejakait Yesu Kristo , kinacata onac kere loitotolikino komam elosenenei kwape ejaar epone loipotu kodumut kamakosi .
53003007	Naarai ijenete yesi kwape ibusakinitor yes aputorit sio ; naarai mam sio kitotolikino kamakus ,
53003008	mam kipou kanyama inyamat luka idiotuŋanan atitai , konye kaitaaritoi ka ailolony , kipou keswamata akuare ka apaaran da , tetere mam kilaŋirikini idiotuŋanan kayesi .
53003009	Mere naarai emamei sio apolou , konye kiinakin yes aanyunet tetere kiputorete sio .
53003010	Naarai nakijaar nepepe kayes , kipou kecorakis yes nata ebe : Arai mam ituŋanan ekoto aswam , kinyek ainyam da .
53003011	Naarai kipupi ebe ejaas ice luelosete itotolikino kotomakus , mam iswamaete konye iramaitos nuka luce .
53003012	Kicorakini kotoma Ejakait Yesu Kristo , kikwenyari da luikote nen ebe , kiswamata kaiyapaara , konyamata ikecenyamat kikulepek .
53003013	Konye yes , iinacan , sirikitapalikinos aswam nuejok .
53003014	Konye arai etuŋanan kere mam erimari akirotokosi kotoma obalua kalo , koŋicutu ŋol , kinyeis aimorikikin kaŋes , tetere irumete ileic .
53003015	Sirikimarata ŋes kwape lokasurup , konye kikwenyanarete kwape onac .
53003016	Ejakait da elopet loka ainapakin , koinak yes ainapakin apaarasia kere toma akiro kere . Kojai Ejakait kayes kere .

54001001	Paul ekiyakia loka Kristo Yesu kwape ejaar aicorakinet naka Edeke Eketajaraniwok , ka naka Yesu Kristo amunowok .
54001002	Mama ejai Timoteo , ikakoku obe kotoma aiyuun : Asianut , ka aitim , ka ainapakin nuepote kama ejai Edeke Papa , ka Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok .
54001003	Kwape abu kecorakinia jo asalakin Epeso , naalosio Makedonia , tetere icorakini icetuŋa kinyeis aisisianakin nuegelara ,
54001004	karaida aomoom nuka awaragasia nutai , ka iitabon luka aur lumam edaunos , lueyaunete ipegeta itia aijokokinet naka Edeke naejai toma aiyuun ;
54001005	kwabo awasia naka aicorakinet ŋes amin naelomuni kotau loelai , ka aomisio nuejok ka aiyuun namam esoswai .
54001006	Akudosi icetuŋa apaasi alomar toma akiro nutai ,
54001007	ekotosi araun ikesisianakinak luka ikisila , komam ejenete nuinerasi karaida akiro nuitogogoŋito .
54001008	Konye kijeni ebe ejokuka ikisila , arai kitwasam ituŋanan kes kwape ejaatar ikisila ,
54001009	kojen na ebe mam ibwaikinitai ikisila kanuka yenedolit , dimarai kanuka lukepali ka luetumaaka , kanuka lumam eyoŋito Edeke ka ikadiakanarak , luemamei alaunit , ka luemunaara , luearete lukapapakec , ka luearete nukatotokec , ka luearete iruna ,
54001010	ludotea , iketepak ikiliok , luijoreete ituŋa , ikeŋalak , luiyapoete nuka aiŋal , ka ŋin kere da yenirebirebi aisisianakin naka aijar ,
54001011	kwape ejaatar Akiro Nukajokak nukaibuses nuka Edeke loituritoi nuketitiŋitai .
54001012	Emalai ŋol loketogogoni , ŋes Kristo Yesu Ejakaitiwok naarai abu kaomite eoŋ araun lomunot , kadakak aijaanakin ,
54001013	karaida abu kainyanakini ŋes kolo , kareite , ka amoromor da ; konye aponi ketimi naarai abu keswama kamamus aijen kotoma amamus aiyuun ,
54001014	konye kiyatakin noi asianut naka Ejakaitiwok nepepe kaiyuun ka amin naejai toma Kristo Yesu .
54001015	Namunot akirot na , ido naibusakinit ituŋa kere acamun ebe , Abu Kristo Yesu kobu toma akwap aitajar ikadiakanarak , Eoŋ losodit kakesi .
54001016	Konye kanuka na ŋes ketimere , tetere itodiari Yesu Kristo kotoma eoŋ losodit aketitiŋikin kere , araun aanyunet mama kaŋul luepote aiyuun ŋes kiton aijar naka ikar kere .
54001017	Mama ejai Ekabaka loka ikar , ekabuton , lomam etakani , Edeke ediopet bon , kojai aiturit ka aibuses ikar ka ikar . Amen .
54001018	Ketitiŋi jo , Timoteo okokuka , aicorakinet na kwape ejaatar akiro nuka inabin nukinerakinito jo kolo , tetere ijio kotoma kaŋun ejie lokajokan ,
54001019	kikam aiyuun ka aomisio nuejok . Apotu ice koremosi ŋun , kobila ataker naka aiyuunikec .
54001020	Kotomakec ejai Kumenaio ka Alegesanda , luabu kejaik Satan , tetere isisiaete ainyein ainyanakin .
54002001	Aso nasodit kakere , ecori ebe kiswamaenenete aiŋaiŋa , ka ailip , ka aipur , ka aimal da , kanuka ituŋa kere ,
54002002	kanuka ikabakan ka ŋul kere luejaas apolou , tetere kijaun kaijar naitenera , naiyamakina , toma ayoŋit Edeke , ka aiyaparit kere .
54002003	Ejok ŋun , ido ecamunitai kakonyen nuka Edeke Eketajaraniwok ,
54002004	loekot ituŋa kere aitajario , adolokin da ajenun abeit .
54002005	Naarai ejai Edeke ediopet , ejai da ekadiekan ediopet loka Edeke ka ituŋa , ŋes etuŋanan Kristo Yesu ,
54002006	loabu koluŋakin araun alakunet kanuka kere , aitejenunet naejaun kapakioke .
54002007	Kebwaikinitai eoŋ araun ekalimonokinan , ekiyakia da kanuka ŋun , ( enera abeit , mam eŋalai ) ekesisianakinan loka Imo kotoma aiyuun ka abeit .
54002008	Ŋes akotor ikiliok ailipenen kotoma ŋiniibois , koriorito akanin nukalaunak komamei anyunyura karaida aŋolopa ;
54002009	kwape kwaŋin da aŋor kisirete anapito nuibusak , kaitasono ka acoit , mere kaicip itim , karaida kesabu , karaida ilulun , karaida igoen luketiai ,
54002010	dimarai kaswamisio nuejok , kwape ibusakinitor aŋor nuelimorete ebe eyoŋito Edeke .
54002011	Kisisia aberu kaiyamakina kanonokikinit kere .
54002012	Konye mam esiikinit aberu aisisianakin , karaida ayait ekiliokit , dimarai aiyamaara .
54002013	Naarai kisiau Adam asubio , kosodi konyet Keba .
54002014	Bobo da mam Adam kijodijoditoi , konye Keba ejodijoditoi , kojaikin aibucar .
54002015	Konye itajario aberu kanuka auruun idwe , arai esalete kesi toma aiyuun , ka amin , ka alaunit nepepe kacoit .
54003001	Namunot akirot na ebe : Arai eŋaŋat etuŋanan araun ekaanyanaran , imiela aswam naejok .
54003002	Aso ibusakinit ekaanyanaran araun loemamei aitoronet , ekiliokit loka aberu adiopet , loitikokina , loecoit , loiyapaara , loisukunyikini ipejok , loejeni aisisianakin ,
54003003	lomam emer , lomam ibuŋai ; dimarai lokaiyapepera , lomam eŋolopana , lomam emin apesan ;
54003004	loeyait ejok lukokaleke , loitononokikini ikedwe kaiyapaara kere ;
54003005	naarai arai mam etuŋanan ejeni ayait lukokaleke , ikwaikini ai imukei ekanisa loka Edeke ?
54003006	Mere ekeyuunan lokitetet , kinyek adakunun , ka aibirokin otube loka Satan .
54003007	Konye ibusakinit lukokiŋa aitejen nukajokak kamakeŋ , kinyek aibirokin amorosit , kotoma atacit da naka Satan .
54003008	Ikejaanakinak kwape kwaŋin kiyapaara , mere luideideok , mere luemasete ajon nuipu , mere luiŋobelete apesan ,
54003009	luejai aiyeiyea naka aiyuun kotoma aomisio nuelaete .
54003010	Konye kisiautu ber ŋul da aitemio , kosodete konyet aijaanakin , arai eraas luemamei aitoronet .
54003011	Aŋor da kwape kwaŋin kiyapaara , mere akasabak , nuitikokina , numunon kakiro kere .
54003012	Koraut ikejaanakinak ikiliok luka adiopeberu , lueyaito ejok ikecedwe ka lukokaliakec .
54003013	Naarai luejaanakis ejok , edumakina adoket naejok , ka atitiŋ naepol kotoma aiyuun naejai toma Kristo Yesu .
54003014	Kewadikakini jo nu amuno abunore mamakon atipet ,
54003015	konye arai etumori , tetere ijenuni kwape ibusakinitor ituŋa ajaut kotoma otogo loka Edeke , loerai ekanisa loka Edeke lokajaran , epir ka eigaŋet loka abeit .
54003016	Ido komamei abuonokin , epol noi aiyeiyea naka ayoŋit Edeke : Abu kitodiar kotoma akuan , Kitojokai kotoma Omoyo , Apotu imalaikan koanyut ŋes , Aponi kolimonokinai kotoma atekerin , Aponi kiyuunai kotoma akwapin , Kodakarai kuju toma aibuses .
54004001	Konye inera Emoyo kaitebeikin ebe kotoma apakio nuepote etiakatiakaunos ice ainyein aiyuun , epupete imoyon luepaarete , ka aisisianakin naka ajokin ,
54004002	kanuka aisoswanut naka ikeŋalak , luicweio aomisiokec kemacar loesarani ,
54004003	imikete aimany , italeete lunyaman , luabu Edeke kosub tetere ijaunete luiyuunito ka luejenete noi abeit kaimal .
54004004	Naarai ejok ŋinibore kere yenikesubi Edeke , emamei da ibore yeneŋerio , arai ecamunio kaimal ;
54004005	naarai italaunitai kanuka akirot naka Edeke ka ailip da .
54004006	Arai isiituni iinacan akiro ŋun iraun ekejaanakinan loejok loka Kristo Yesu , kitanete jo akiro nuka aiyuun , ka aisisianakin naejok naibu kotup .
54004007	Kinac awaragasia numam eraas nuka edini , nukabaŋaanut . Konye kitwasama bon kotoma ayoŋit Edeke ;
54004008	naarai aitwasam akuan ejai ameda naedit , konye ayoŋit Edeke ejai ameda kakiro kere , naarai ejai aisumunet naka aijar naka tinenikwana , ka aijar da naebuni .
54004009	Namunot akirot na , ido naibusakinit ituŋa kere acamun .
54004010	Naarai kitaaritoi kiwuta da kanuka ŋun , naarai kimunokina Edeke lokajaran , loerai Eketajaran loka ituŋa kere , aitelekarit loka luiyuunito .
54004011	Kicorak akiro ŋun , kisisianak da kes .

54004013	Aitodol neabunio , kodunyak asoman , ka aicor , ka aisisianakin da .

54004015	Koomitenenei ŋun , kojaenena kotomakec , tetere etakani akonijokiar otuŋa kere .

54005003	Koyoŋit apuserun nueraas apuserun cut .
54005004	Konye apuserut arai ejaas kidwe arai itatai , kisiaunete aisisia ayoŋit Edeke kokaliakec , ka atacakin ikauriakakec ; naarai ecamunitai ŋin kakonyen nuka Edeke .
54005005	Konye ŋin naerai apuserut cut , kinyeinai bon , emunokina Edeke , kosalak aiŋaiŋa ka ailipenen akuare ka apaaran .
54005006	Konye ŋin naeminakinito aboliasio , etwanit karaida kejari .
54005007	Kicorak kes ŋun da , tetere eraas nuemamei aitoronet .
54005008	Konye ituŋanan kere arai mam idari lukeŋ , aitelekarit lukokaleke ilopet , aŋer ŋesi aiyuun , erono da adepar yenimam iyuunit .
54005009	Siriwadikao apuserut namam edolit ikar akaisakanykape , nakerai aberu naka ekiliokit ediopet ;
54005010	itejenunitai kanuka aswamisio nuejok ; arai esait idwe , arai abu kisukuny ipejok , kilot akeje nuka lukalaunak , iŋarakinit luiticanio , arai da edunyit atupit ŋiniswam kere naejok ,
54005011	Konye koŋer aiwadik apuserun nukatumunak ; naarai naiyatakiniata aipaliikin Kristo , ekotosi adukokin ;
54005012	egwaunete akiro naarai enyeis aiyuunikec nasodit .

54005016	Arai ejaas aberu naiyuunit apuserun , kiŋarak ŋin kes , kinyeinai alaŋirikin ekanisa , tetere iŋarakini nueraas apuserun cut .

54005018	naarai ebala naiwadikatai ebe , “ Sirikien aituk naka emoŋ loipudapudai aicom akima . ” Ebe da , “ Ekeswaman ibusakinit ekeropit . ”

54005020	Luediakanarete kitoron kakonyen nuka ituŋa kere , tetere luce da eyoŋete .
54005021	Kecorakinit kakonyen nuka Edeke ka Kristo Yesu , ka imalaikan luseuna koricit ŋun komam isunyit aitub , sirikiswama akirot kere kotiakite ituŋa .

54005023	Sirimasenenei bobo akipi bon , konye komat ediobino kanuka akoikikon , naarai idekanakin da irwan ipu .
54005024	Ideleleete adiakanareta nuka icetuŋa , kiŋarenikinete kiton atubokinio ; konye nuka ice ideleleunete kokau ,
54005025	Kwape kwaŋin da ideleleete aswamisio nuejok ; karaida ŋun numam ideleleete , mam epedorete aibwaio .
54006001	Kere lueraas ibulesin kwap kajookot , koomitos ijakakec araut luibusakinito ayoŋio kere , kinyek ekiror loka Edeke ka aisisianakin da ainyanakinio .
54006002	Ido luejaas ijaka luiyuunito , sirikemwaŋata kes , naarai eraas iinacan , konye gwai kiyatakis aijaanakin kes , naarai luedumunete ajokis naka aswamukec eraas luiyuunito , luminan da . Kisisianakin ŋun , kicor da .
54006003	Arai isisianakini ituŋanan nuegelara komam enupit akiro nuejarete nuka Ejakaitiwok Yesu Kristo , ka aisisianakin da naetupit ayoŋit Edeke ,
54006004	edakunun , komam ejeni akirot , konye edek ipegeta , ka ijiisio luka akiro , mama eponiata ekokote , aŋolopa , ainyanakin , aomoom nueroko ,
54006005	iceleta luka ituŋa luamunaar acoakec , lualemar abeit , lueomito ebe ayoŋit Edeke ŋes adumun ameda .
54006006	Konye ayoŋit Edeke nepepe kalakara ŋes ameda naepol .
54006007	Naarai mam kiyaunit ibore toma akwap , ido mam kipedori ayaŋaar ibore ;

57001007	Naarai abu kadum aiyalama naepol ka aitalakario da kanuka aminakon , onace , naarai ibu kisiyeŋu itauon luka lukalaunak .
57001008	Kanuka ŋun karaida ajai katitiŋ naepol toma Kristo aicorakin jo naipudai ,
57001009	konye gwai kanuka amin , keŋaiŋait-eoŋ loekoni nen Paul ekimat , konye kwana eenat da loka Kristo Yesu , —
57001010	keŋaiŋait jo kanuka ikakoku , Onesimo , loaurit kotoma aenioka .
57001011	Kolo amamei ŋes ajokis mamakon , konye kwana ejai ajokis mamakon ka mamakaŋ da .
57001012	Enyakuni ŋes mamakon , ŋol loerai ekatau .
57001013	Akoto ti aitasal ŋes mamakaŋ , tetere kejaanakin eoŋ kanukon kotoma aenioka kanuka Akiro Nukajokak ,
57001014	konye mam abu kakoto aswam ibore komam jo ijeni , tetere ejaun akonijokis mere kanuka aitiŋaikin , dimarai kanuka akot .
57001015	Diat kanuka ŋun ŋes kitiakere kajo adaun apak , tetere ijaunete kaŋes ikar kere ,
57001016	mere bobo kwape ebulesit , konye adepar ebulesit , onac lominat , aitelekarit mamakaŋ , konye gwai itelekarit ca ma mamakon , toma akuan ido toma Ejakait da .
57001017	Aso arai kidica keoŋ , kisukunyik ŋes kwape kisukunyikinia eoŋ .
57001018	Arai abu kiswamak jo adioronis arai bo ejai apesen , kitepesen eoŋ ŋun .
57001019	Eoŋ Paul ewadikai nu kakakan elopet , atacakini eoŋ-komam alimokini jo ebe ejai jo apesen mamakaŋ , ijo ilopet obe .
57001020	Eebo , onac , akoto adumun ajokis kamakon toma Ejakait . Kisiyeŋu ekatau toma Kristo ,
57001021	Kewadikak jo kajai kamun naka arimanutukon , ajeni da ebe iswamai ijo adepar nuenera eoŋ .
57001022	Bobo da kitemokino aisipejo eoŋ , naarai amuno ebe kanuka ailipikus , kainakinia mamakus .
57001023	Kiyogai jo Epapuras , ekijoreoritono aupaka toma Kristo Yesu .
57001024	Marako da , ka Aristariko , ka Dema , ka Luka , ikeswamak lukaupaka .
57001025	Asianut naka Ejakait Yesu Kristo kojai kimoyonokus .
58001001	Abu kolo Edeke kinera kalukapapaawok koponesio luipu luegelegela kotoma onabin ;
58001002	konye kapaarasia kanu nukawasia ener kaoni kotoma Okoku , loabu kodakak araun ekeruman loka kere , kanukeŋ da abu kosub akwapisinei .
58001003	Erai ŋesi ailore naka aibuses naka Edeke , erai da einono loka ejauteneke , edakit iboro kere kakirot naka akepedor . Nakedaunia aitesegaar adiakanareta , kiboikin akan nakoteten naka Loejai kuju kakuj , kotoma akuj ,
58001004	korau loedeparit noi imalaikan kajokis , kwape erumitor ekiror loedeparit noi lokec kajokis .
58001005	Naarai iŋai bo komalaikan abu Edeke kobala ebe , “ Irai ijo Okokuka , lolo kauri jo ” ? Bobo da ebe , “ Araun eoŋ Papake , ŋes da eraun okokuka ” ?
58001006	Bobo da , naayaunia ekiyai toma akwapin ebala ebe , “ Komaata ŋes imalaikan kere luka Edeke . ”
58001007	Inera nuka imalaikan ebe , “ Loesubi ikemalaikan araut imoyon , Ka ikejaanakinakake da aŋajepa nuka akim . ”
58001008	Konye nuka Okoku ebe , “ Wu Edeke , ejaenena ekoniicoloŋ ikar ka ikar , Ebela da lokadolit , ŋes ebela loka ajakanutuke .
58001009	Ido komina adolit , kolaite da epali , Tape Edeke , Ekonideke , kinyonyoikini jo akinyet naka ailel Adepar lukaupakon . ”
58001010	Bobo da ebe , “ Ijo , wu Ejakait , ameun kageunet , Ibu kopet apetetait naka akwap , Akuj da erai aswam naka akonikanin ;
58001011	Edaunos ŋun , konye jo ibusenenei ; Emojoŋgete da kere kwape anapito ;
58001012	Ido inunuki kes kwape eimukoret , Ilocokinio da kwape anapito . Konye ijo ŋopeŋol , Ikonikar da mam enaŋete . ”
58001013	Konye iŋai bo komalaikan abu ŋesi kobala ebe , “ Kiboikin akanika nakoteten , Aitodol naebwaikinia lukasurupokon Araut iicoloŋ yenika akejekon ” ?
58001014	Mere kereka kes kere imoyon luijaanakinete , luiyakiaritai aijaanakin , kanuka ŋul luepote airum aitajario ?
58002001	Kanuka ŋun ibusakinit oni aiyatakin noi aibwaikin itauon ŋun nukipupu , kenyeis aikaleleorio kamakec .
58002002	Naarai arai icasit akirot nakineras imalaikan , tape eropio kadolit ŋiniibucaret ka ŋiniiulanut ,
58002003	kikwaikini ai kikui oni arai kijali aitajario naetia nen ? Abu Ejakait kogeu alimokin ŋin , kosodete lukiirarete ŋes apotu kitogogoŋoto mamawok .
58002004	Edeke da abu kitejen nepepe kakes kotoma aanyuneta ka nukaumokin , ka nukapedor nuka iponesio luegelegela , kotoma akorakineta da nuka Emoyo Lokalaunan , kwape ejaar akoteke elopet .
58002005	Naarai mam einakinit Edeke akwapin nueponito nukinera , anonokikin imalaikan .
58002006	Konye ejai aibois naitejenunitor ediopet , kinera ebe , “ Inyo bo etuŋanan , tape jo iitunit ŋes ? Arai bo okoku loka etuŋanan , tape jo ianyanari ŋes ?
58002007	Ibu kosub ŋes nepetai airianakin ka imalaikan adaun apak naedit , Itanapit ŋes aboko naka aibuses ka ayoŋio , Isurumit ŋes aswamisio nuka akonikanin .
58002008	Itononokikinit iboro kere aibwaikin kwap kakejeneke . ” “ Alimokini ikainacan ekonikiror , Keturenenei jo , kokidiŋ katukot . ” “ Amunoneno eoŋ ŋes . ” “ Koany , eoŋ ka idwe lukainak Edeke . ”
58002009	Konye kiseseni Yesu loaponi kosubai nepetai airianakin ka imalaikan adaun apak naedit , kanuka aiticanio naka atwanare , aponi kitanapai aboko naka aibuses ka ayoŋio , tetere kanuka asianut naka Edeke , iiri atwanare kanuka ŋinituŋanan .
58002010	Naarai ebusakinit ŋol , loejaas iboro kere kanukeŋ , ido loepote iboro kere kamakeŋ , naeyaunia odwe luipu toma aibuses , aitodolikin ekapeleunan loka aitajariokec kanuka aisiriebio .
58002011	Naarai loitalauni ka luetalaunitai eraas kere luka ediopet . Kanuka ŋun ŋes mam irumiata ŋes ileic anyarit kes iinacan ,
58002012	kinera ebe , “ Alimokini ikainacan ekonikiror , Keturenenei jo , kokidiŋ katukot . ”
58002013	Bobo da ebe , “ Amunoneno eoŋ ŋes . ” Ido bobo ebe , “ Koany , eoŋ ka idwe lukainak Edeke . ”
58002014	Aso naarai imorikikinete idwe aokot ka awat , abu ŋesi da elopet komor kakes ejautenekec , tetere kanuka atwanareke emudiari ŋol loejai apedor naka atwanare , ŋes Satan .
58002015	Tetere elacakini da ŋul kere lukejaas toma obulesene apaarasia kere nuka aijarakec , kanuka akurian atwanare .
58002016	Naarai abeit mam iŋarakinit imalaikan , dimarai iŋarakinit aur naka Aburaam .
58002017	Ŋes iburaa ŋes aitupusio ikeinacan kotoma kere , tetere eraun esasedoti lopeti lokaitim lomunot kotoma akiro nuejaas neejai Edeke , kanuka ailuc adiakanareta nuka ituŋa .
58002018	Aso naarai abu ŋesi da elopet korieba ecodunio , ŋes epedoria aiŋarakin ŋul luecodunio .
58003001	Aso , iinacan lukalaunak , luimorete anyaraunio nakokuju , koomoomata Yesu , Ekiyakia ido Esasedoti lopeti lokilimonori oni .
58003002	Kerai ŋesi lomunot mama ejai ŋol loaseuni ŋes , kwape Musa da keraar lomunot kotogoke kere .
58003003	Naarai ibusakinit Yesu ainakinio aibuses naepol adepar Musa , kwape edumunia loeduki etogo ayoŋio adepar etogo .
58003004	Naarai ejai ŋolitogo ekadukonike , konye loaduki kere ŋes Edeke .
58003005	Musa da kerai lomunot kotogoke kere kwape ebulesit , kanuka aitejenun nuepote ainerio ,
58003006	konye Kristo kerai lomunot kotogoke kwape okoku . Kirai oni etogoke , arai kikamuni kagogoŋ ati tiŋ ka aolobobot naka amun kiton awasia .
58003007	Aso kwape ebalar Emoyo Lokalaunan ebe , “ Lolo , arai kiirasi ekeporoto .
58003008	Sirikitininikata ikusitauon , kwape toma aitunyunyurikinio , Kwape kapaaran naka acodunio toma amodiŋ .
58003009	Nakakoduniata eoŋ lukapapaakus , ketemo , Koanyutu da akaswamisio ikar akaisaoŋon .
58003010	Ŋes abu kanyunyurikinia atur ŋin , Kabala ebe , ‘ Epaarete apaarasia kere kotauonokec ; Komam ejenete ikarotin , ’
58003011	Kwape keyapoikinia kakanyunyura ebe , ‘ Mam cut elomunete aibworareteka . ’ ” “ Lolo , arai kiirasi ekeporoto , Sirikitininikata ikusitauon , kwape toma aitunyunyurikinio . ”
58003012	Kocoito , iinacan , kinyek ajaun kotoma idio kayesi etau loerono lomam iyuunit , lokitonyouni kama ejai Edeke lokajaran .
58003013	Konye kicorenenas ŋinipaaran , naeriŋar enyaritai “ naka lolo ” , kinyek aiŋal naka adiakar aitininik idio kayesi .
58003014	Naarai kirau ikamorak luka Kristo , arai kikamuni kagogoŋ ageunet naka amunowok kiton awasia .
58003015	Kwape eriŋar inerai ebe , “ Lolo , arai kiirasi ekeporoto , Sirikitininikata ikusitauon , kwape toma aitunyunyurikinio . ”
58003016	Naarai lukaŋai bo kiirarete , kitunyunyurikisi ? Mere kereka ŋul kere luanyounete koMisiri kanuka Musa ?
58003017	Ido lukaŋai bo luabu konyunyurik ikar akaisaoŋon ? Mere kereka ŋul luapotu kodiakas , lukibirokinos akecetesin amodiŋ ?
58003018	Ido lukaŋai bo luabu kiyapoik ebe mam cut elomarete aibworareteke , nabarai ŋul lueulakinete ?
58003019	Ido kianyu ebe mam apotu kopedosi alomar kanuka amamus aiyuun .
58004001	Aso , naeriŋar aisumunet naka alomar aibworareteke esalit , kakuriakaros , kinyek idio kayesi atakanun mam edolokinit .
58004002	Naarai oni da kilimonokinitai Akiro Nukajokak kwape kakesi ; konye akirot nakiirarete mam abu koinu kes ajokis , naarai mam aponi kimorikikinai kotoma aiyuun nepepe kaŋul luapotu kiirasi .
58004003	Naarai oni lukidau aiyuun , kilomari toma aibworaret ŋin , kwape abalar ebe , “ Kwape keyapoikinia kakanyunyura ebe , ‘ Mam cut elomunete aibworareteka , ’ ” karaida apotu aswamisioke kodaunos ameun kageunet naka akwapin .
58004004	Naarai ejai neinerar nuka apaaran nakikanyetekaarei ebe , “ Abu Edeke kibwora kapaaran nakikanyetekaarei , kotoma aswamisioke kere . ”
58004005	Bobo da kotoma kana ebe , “ Mam cut elomunete aibworareteka . ”
58004006	Aso naarai esalit ice alomar tomake , ka ŋul da luageunete alimonokinio akiro nukajokak mam elomarete kanuka aiulanut ,
58004007	bobo etiaki ŋesi apaaran ace , ebala kama ka Daudi ketubor apak naetia nen , ebe , “ Lolo , ” kwape abalar sek ebe , “ Lolo arai kiirasi ekeporoto , Sirikitininikata ikusitauon . ”
58004008	Naarai arai kisiyenunit Yosua kes , timam kinera nuka apaaran ace akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun ,
58004009	Aso esalit aibworaret naka asabato mama ejaas ituŋa luka Edeke ;
58004010	naarai yenelomari aibworareteke , eyenu do ŋesi da kotoma aswamisioke , kwape abu Edeke da kiyenunia kotoma nukeŋ ,
58004011	Aso kadunyakis alomar aibworaret ŋin , kinyek Idiotuŋanan aibirokin opone ŋol loka aiulanut .
58004012	Naarai erai akirot naka Edeke nakajaran , nakapedor da , ekwana adepar ŋolikileŋ loekwana kowaitin kere , ipelori da kiton aitiak aijar ka emoyo , ailenyeta ka asum , emisiikin da aomisio ka nuelosikinit etau .
58004013	Kwabo emamei isubat yenimam etakani kakonyeneke , konye imujalalas iboro kere , ido ideleleete kakonyen nuka ŋol loejaas akirowok .
58004014	Aso naarai kija ka esasedoti lopeti lokapolon , lokelomari toma akuj , Yesu Okoku loka Edeke , keketakis noi alimoriwok .
58004015	Naarai emamei oni esasedoti lopeti lomam epedori arieba nepepe kaoni akalanyanutuwok , konye lokecodunio kakiro kere ariaka kaoni , komam adiakar .
58004016	Aso kekunyakis katitiŋ mama ejai eicoloŋ loka asianut , tetere kitimio , kadumutu da asianut nakinarakini oni kapakio nuka eipud .
58005001	Naarai ŋolisasedoti lopeti loketiakunio kotuŋa ibwaikinio kanuka ituŋa kakiro nuka Edeke , tetere ijaikini ainakineta ka asuban da kanuka adiakanar .
58005002	Epedori aiyamiyamar lueolito ka luepaarito , naarai ŋes da elopet igogoleori akalanyanut .
58005003	Kanuka ŋun ŋes da iburao ainakin asuban kanuka adiakarike , kwape kanuka ŋun nuka ituŋa .
58005004	Kwabo emamei etuŋanan kere eyaŋaikin bon apolou ŋin , dimarai ŋol loenyarit Edeke , kwape ka Aaron .
58005005	Kwape kwaŋin Kristo da mam abu kitopoloor bon aluor esasedoti lopeti , dimarai ŋol loabu kolimok ŋes ebe , “ Irai ijo Okokuka , lolo kauru jo . ”
58005006	Kwape inerar kamace da ebe , “ Irai ijo esasedoti kiton ikar kere , Kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek . ”
58005007	Kapaarasia nuka akuanake , abu Yesu kiŋaiŋa kilip da , kaiworo naepol ka akiyo da , mama ejai ŋol loepedori aitajar ŋes katwanare , kopupunoi da kanuka ayoniteke Edeke .
58005008	Karaida kerai Okoku abu kisisia arimanut kanuka ŋun kanuesiriebete ;
58005009	kosodi nakedaunia aitodolikinio , korau loeinakini ŋul kere luerimarete ŋes aitajario naka ikar kere ,
58005010	loamaikini Edeke esasedoti lopeti kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek .
58005011	Kija kakiro nuipu einer kamakeŋ , ido nuetioko aitejenun , naarai ikimiŋakaros yesi .
58005012	Naarai kapak kana tikibusakinit araut ikesisianakinak , kwabo ipudasi bobo yenikisisianakini yes nusodit nuegeunete nuka akiro nuka Edeke . Ido iluoros luipudasi akile kwabo mere inyamat luenyakao .
58005013	Naarai yenemasi akile mam ejeni akirot naka adolit , naarai erai ikoku .
58005014	Konye inyamat luenyakao eraas luka lukapolok , ŋul luiruutooritai acoakec kanuka aitwasam , tetere etiakete nuejok ka nueroko da .
58006001	Kanuka ŋun kenyeis einer akiro nusodit nuka Kristo , keyatakinos apoloor ; kenyeis bobo aipet apetetait naka aitoronikin kanuka aswamisio nuetwakito , ka aiyuun Edeke ,
58006002	aisisianakin naka aibatis , ka aidokokinio akanin , ka ajarun naka lukatwak , ka atubokinio da naka ikar kere ,
58006003	Kiswamai da kwaŋin arai ekoto Edeke .
58006004	Naarai ŋul luadaut kolo ainwakakinio , kiirata da ainakinet nakakuj , luaraunos ikamorak Emoyo Lokalaunan ,
58006005	kiirata da ajokis naka akirot naka Edeke , ka apedor da naka ikar luepote ,
58006006	mam epedorete aiteteun bobo aitoronikin arai kibiroros ainyein ŋun , naarai ebubukis bobo Okoku loka Edeke kanukec , esurumata da ileic kaitebeikin .
58006007	Naarai akwap naamat akiru naetepanakini irwan ipu , kosodi kobwaŋ akui nuibusakinito ŋul luekorionokinio , edumuni arereŋ naebuni kama ejai Edeke .
58006008	Konye arai kitolom ikukwa ka isukukur , eneritoi , ido eapie aikenio ; esaŋeke aicweio .
58006009	Konye luminan , karaida kinera ŋun kwaŋin , kitogogoŋ kamakus akiro nuejok adepar , ido nueraas nuka aitajario .
58006010	Naarai Edeke mam erai lomam edolit aimurwokin aswamukus , ka amin naipotu kitodiasi mama ejai ekirorike naijaanakiniata lukalaunak , ido kwana iroko ijaanakinete .
58006011	Konye kiŋata noi ŋinituŋanan kayesi aitodiar adunyanut ŋipeŋin kanuka aitodolikin cut amun ŋin kiton osaŋe ,
58006012	kinyeis araut luijalijalasi , konye luipusete ŋul luirumete aisumuneta kanuka aiyuun ka atitiŋikin da .
58006013	Naarai naesumunio Edeke Aburaam , naarai amamei loapol aitelekarit ŋes loelimit iyapoi , abu kiyapo kolimite elopet ,
58006014	kobala ebe , “ Abeit kotoma arereŋ kesirereŋenenei jo , ka aiyat keyatanakinenei jo . ”
58006015	Kwape kwaŋin kanuka atitiŋikin abu kodum aisumunet ŋin .
58006016	Naarai iyapoete ituŋa kolimito loepol aitelekarit kes , ido kotoma opegetakec kere , edauni aiyapoet aitogogoŋ ,
58006017	Aso naakotor Edeke aitodikin cut noi ikerumak luka aisumunet kwape mam ijulakinor akekot , abu kodiek kaiyaposit ,
58006018	tetere kanuka akiro aarei numam ijulakinos , numam epedori Edeke aiŋal , kidumuni aitalakario naegogoŋ , oni lukirurukit aikamun amun naibwaikinitai kakonyenewok .
58006019	Kija kaŋin kwape edobo loka aijar , loicasit loegogoŋ , amun naelomari mama ejai naejai toma aigalisit ,
58006020	neabu Yesu koloma kwape ekeŋarenon kanuwok , abu koraun esasedoti lopeti ikar kere kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek
58007001	Naarai Melukisadek ŋol , ekabaka loko Salem , esasedoti loka Edeke Loejai kuju kakuj , loeriamunos ka Aburaam naaboŋunio kajar ikabakan , abu kilipak ŋes arereŋ ;
58007002	loabu Aburaam kokorak idiopet kotomon koboroke kere . Nasodit , arai ijulakini ekekiror , erai ŋesi ekabaka loka adolit , bobo da ekabaka loka Salem , ŋes atemar ebe ekabaka loka ainapakin .
58007003	Emamei ŋes papa , karaida toto , karaida lukapapaake , emamei ageunet naka apaarasiake , karaida esaŋe loka aijarake , konye itupusitoi ka Okoku loka Edeke , esalakinit erai esasedoti apaarasia kere .
58007004	Aso ca koomito etuŋanan ŋol , kwape keraar loepol ! Abu Aburaam papaawok koinak ŋes idiopet kotomon kaluŋatuna .
58007005	Ŋul da lukodwe luka Lebi lueinakinio esasedotene ejaas kaicorakinet ayaŋanar idiopet kotomon kotuŋa kwape ejaatar ikisila , kes iinacanakec , karaida ŋul da kelomunete kotoma akuan naka Aburaam .
58007006	Konye ŋol lomam imaritai lukapapaake kamakec , abu kodum idiopet kotomon kama ka Aburaam , kilipak arereŋ loejaas kaisumuneta .
58007007	Konye emamei epeget nepepec da , ebe , ŋipakini lokapolon lodidi arereŋ .
58007008	Kane da edumunete ituŋa luetwakete idiopet kotomon , konye kalaije , ŋol loiteienunio ebe ejari ,
58007009	Epedorio einer ebe Lebi da , loedumuni idiopet kotomon , abu koinak idiopet kotomon kotoma Aburaam ,
58007010	naarai koriŋa ejai toma akuan naka papaake naeriamunotor Melukisadek kaŋes .
58007011	Aso arai kejai aitodolikinio kanuka esasedotene loka Ilebin , ( naarai apotu ituŋa kodumut ikisila kanuka ŋol , ) kanukinyo ipudare bobo esasedoti ece anyoun kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek , komam imarakinio kwape ejaar epone loka Aaron ?
58007012	Naarai naelocokinere esasedotene , ibusakinit ikisila da ailoeokinio .
58007013	Naarai ŋol loalimitere akiro ŋun kerai loka ateker ace , nemam ebunitor etuŋanan kere lokijaanakini kotem .
58007014	Naarai idelelei ebe elomunit Ejakaitiwok kotoma Yuda , ateker namam apeŋo Musa elimitor akiro nuka esasedotene .
58007015	Bobo da iyatasi ŋun aideleleun noi , arai enyounit esasedoti ece kwape ejaar aput naka Melukisadek ,
58007016	loaraun esasedoti , mere kwape ejaatar ikisila luka aicorakinet naka akuan , dimarai kwape ejaar apedor naka aijar namam edaun .
58007017	Naarai itejenunitai ebe , “ Irai ijo esasedoti kiton ikar kere , Kwape ejaar epone loka Melukisadek . ”
58007018	Naarai kepuai epaluni aicorakinet nageet kanuka akalanyanut ka amamus ajokisike ,
58007019	( naarai emamei ibore yenitodolete ikisila ; ) kepuai da aponi kitolomikin amun naitelekarit ajokis , nakikunyaria mama ejai Edeke .
58007020	Ido mam abu kojau komamei aiyaposit .
58007021	Naarai koraut kesi isasedotin komamei aiyaposit , konye je kitaraunai kaiyaposit kanuka ŋol lokelimokini ŋes ebe , “ Abu Ejakait kiyapo , komam iitokini ebe , ‘ Irai ijo esasedoti kiton ikar kere . ’ ”
58007022	Abu Yesu da korau kwaŋin ekabwoaran loka aitutuket naitelekarit ajokis .
58007023	Kes da aponi kitaraununai isasedotin luipu , naarai etikokinit kes atwanare ajaenena osasedotene ;
58007024	konye ŋol , esasedoteneke mam ikopanar , naarai ejaenena ikar kere .
58007025	Kanuka ŋun ŋes epedoria aitajar cut luepote mama ejai Edeke kotomakeŋ , naarai ebusi ŋesi apaarasia kere apuronokin kes .
58007026	Naarai ibusakinit oni ajaut kesasedoti lopeti loikoni nen , lokalaunan , loemamei aronis , karaida elos , loetiakunitai kama ejaas ikadiakanarak , loitopolooritai da adepar akuj .
58007027	Mam ŋes iburao ŋinipaaran , kwape isasedotin kwi lupeti , ainanakin asuban , naegei kanuka adiakanaretake , kosodi konyet kokau kanuka ŋun nuka ituŋa ; naarai abu ŋesi kiswama , kwaŋin irwan atipet bon naejaikinor elopet .
58007028	Naarai eseunete ikisila ituŋa luekalanyaka , araun isasedotin lupeti ; konye do akirot naka aiyaposit naetupakini ikisila , abu koseu Okoku loitodolikinitoi kiton ikar kere .
58008001	Akirot alopet nakibala ŋes nata ebe : kija kesasedoti lopeti loikoni nen , lokiboikin akan nakoteten naka eicoloŋ naka Lokapolou toma akuj ,
58008002	ekejaanakinan toma aiboisio nukalaunak , ka ewema lokabeit , lokibubukini Ejakait kwabo mere etuŋanan ,
58008003	Naarai ŋolisasedoti lopeti edakakinio tetere einakini ainakineta ka asuban ; kanuka ŋun ibusakinit esasedoti ŋol da lopeti ajaut kibore yeneinakini .
58008004	Aso arai kejai akwap , timam keraun esasedoti nepetai da , naarai ejaas isasedotin lueinakinete ainakineta kwape ejaatar ikisila .
58008005	Ijaanakinete ŋul aput ka etoribe loka aiboisio nukalaunak nukotoma akuj ; kwape kicorakinia Edeke Musa napeapie aiswamaun ewema ebe , “ Kocoite ebe iswamauni iboro kere kwape ejaar aput nakiitodikinio jo koroŋat . ”
58008006	Konye kwana abu Kristo kodum aijaanakin naitelekarit noi , naarai erai ekadiekan loka aitutuket naitelekarit noi ajokis , naisilakinitai kotoma aisumuneta nuitelekarito noi ajokis .
58008007	Naarai arai kerai aitutuket nasodit naemamei aitoronet timam kemoi aibois kanuka nakiareit .
58008008	Naarai itoroni kes naebalar ebe : “ Ebala Ejakait ebe , epote apaarasia , Nuetodolikinio aitutuket nakitetet kekek loka Isirael , Ka ekek loka Yuda .
58008009	Ebala Ejakait ebe , Mere kwape ejaar aitutuket nakolo etutuki ka lukapapaakec Kapaaran naketiŋia kakan aitonyoun kakwap nako Misiri ; Naarai mam ŋul kesalito toma aitutuketeka , Eoŋ da abu kajal kes .
58008010	Ebala Ejakait ebe , Na ŋes aitutuket naetutuki kekek loka Isirael , Akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun ; Epikakini ikakisila aomisiokec , Ewadikakini da otauonokec ; Eoŋ da araun Ekecedeke , Kes da eraunos ikatuŋa .
58008011	Kwabo mam bobo isisianakinos ŋinituŋanan ikeidunyet , Ka ŋinituŋanan da onaceke , kobalas ebe , ‘ Kojen Ejakait , ’ Naarai kajenunete rwaru kere , Ameun ka yenididi aitodol yenikapolon kakesi .
58008012	Naarai etimi kes numam adolitekec , Ido mam bobo eituni akecediakar . ”
58008013	Nainerar ebe Aitutuket nakitetet , itomojoŋi nasodit . Konye ŋin naamojoŋiar , naekokosanit da eapie ailicar .
58009001	Aso aitutuket nasodit da kejaas kaicorakineta nuka aima Edeke ka aibois nakalaunan naka akwap .
58009002	Naarai itemokinitoi ewema losodit , lokejai epir loka atalai , ka emesa , ka imugatin luka aitodikin , nen ŋes kenyaritai Aibois nakalaunan .
58009003	Kau naka aigalisit nakiareit kejai ewema lokenyaritai Aibois nakalaunan noi ,
58009004	lokejai etem loka lukisupurununo lokesabu , ka asaduku naka aitutuket nakiladaaritai kesabu iwaitin kere , nekejai atido nakesabu nakejai emanu , ka ebela loka Aaron loeburukunyit , ka amor da nuka aitutuket ;
58009005	kujuke da Ikerubin luka aibuses , iteriborito eicoloŋ-lokaitim . Emamei apak kwana einer akiro nuka iboro kaŋul idiopet idiopet .
58009006	Aso kedaut iboro ŋul aitemonokinio kwaŋin , elomanarete isasedotin tiritir owema losodit , itodolikinete akiro nuka aijaanakin ;
58009007	konye owema ŋol lokiareit elomanari esasedoti lopeti bon , irwan atipet ŋolikaru , mere komameete aokot nueinakini kanuke , ido kanuka aibucareta nuka aolit naka ituŋa .
58009008	Isideleleuni Emoyo Lokalaunan ebe mam ber erot etakanuna alomar aiboisio nukalaunak , naeriŋar ewema losodit ebwoi .
58009009	Ŋin ŋes aput naka apak nakwana , naejaas ainakineta ka asuban nueinakinio numam epedorete aitodol aomisio nuka yenemai ;
58009010	naarai eraas ikisila luka akuan bon , lunyaman ka lumatan , ka luka ailoŋ naka iponesio luegelegela , lukicorakinio aitodol apak naka aiteteunio .
58009011	Konye kedau Kristo abunore , loerai esasedoti lopeti loka akiro nuejok nuejaunete , kotoma owema loepol aitelekarit loitodolikinio jokan , lomam kiswamao kakanin , ŋes atemar ebe , mere loka akwap kana ,
58009012	kwabo mere kanuka aokot nuka akinei ka itak lurosok , konye kanuka akeokot elopet , abu koloma irwan atipet bon Aibois Nakalaunan , nakedaunia adumun alakun naka ikar kere .
58009013	Naarai arai aokot nuka akinei ka imoŋin , ka ekurwon loka ataok , lukebwatanakinio luemunaara , italaunete kiton aitesegaar akuan ,
58009014	itelekarito cama aokot nuka Kristo , lokeinakin bon mama ejai Edeke kotoma Omoyo loka ikar kere , araun asubanit naemamei akemer , itesegarete aomisiokus kaswamisio nukatwak tetere ijaanakinete Edeke lokajaran .
58009015	Kanuka ŋun erai ekadiekan loka aitutuket nakitetet , tetere edumunete ŋul lukenyaraunitai aisumunet naka airumet naka ikar kere , naarai abu atwanare kojau naelakuni kes kotoma apaanareta nukotoma aitutuket nasodit .
58009016	Naarai neejai aitutuket naka airum , ibusakinit kojai atwanare naka yenikitutuki ŋin .
58009017	Naarai icasit aitutuket naka airum nakejaunia atwanare , naarai emamei ŋes agogoŋ arai eroko ejari yenikitutuki .
58009018	Kanuka ŋun kiton aitutuket nasodit da mam itaŋitai komameete aokot .
58009019	Naarai nakedaunia Musa alimokin ituŋa kere ninikicorakinet kwape ejaatar ikisila , abu kolem aokot nuka itak lurosok ka nuka akinei nepepe kakipi ka eusi loereŋ , ka esop da , kobwatanak eitabo ka ituŋa kere ,
58009020	kobala ebe , “ Nu kes aokot nuka aitutuket nukiicorakini yes Edeke , ”
58009021	kobwatanak aokot kopone kaŋol ewema , ka iboro kere da luka aijaanakin .
58009022	Abeit kotoma ikisila aapiei iboro kere aitesegario kaokot , ido arai emamei abukor aokot emamei aisionio .
58009023	Aso ibusakinit aputosia nuka iboro lukokuju aitesegario kaŋun , konye iboro lukokuju ikulepek ibusakinit aitesegario kasuban nuitelekarito ŋun kajokis .
58009024	Naarai mam Kristo alomarit aibois nakalaunan nakiswamao kakanin , nakeputosi kaŋin kanakabeit , konye toma akuj alopet , atakanu kwana kakonyen nuka Edeke kanuwok .
58009025	Kwabo mere ainanakin bon irwan ipu , kwape elomanaria esasedoti lopeti Aibois Nakalaunan ŋolikaru kaokot numam eraas nuke ;
58009026	naarai tiibusakinit ŋes arieb irwan ipu ameun kaisub akwapin . Konye kwana , atakanu irwan atipet bon kawasia naka ikar alemar adiakanareta kanuka ainakin bon araut asubanit .
58009027	Ido kwape itemokinitere ituŋa atwanare irwan atipet , kosodi akaulo kaŋin atubokinio ,
58009028	kwape kwaŋin Kristo da , nakeinakinere irwan atipet aibwok adiakanareta nuka ikepuak , etakanuni irwan nakiareit komamei adiakar mama kaŋul luidareto ŋes kanuka aitajario ,
58010001	Naarai ejai ikisila etoribe loka ajokisio nuepote , kwabo mere aput obe naka akiro kaŋun , mam epedorete cut aitodolikin ŋul luikunyakinete , kanuka asuban ŋupeŋun nueinanakinete tiritir , ŋolikaru ŋolikaru .
58010002	Arai mere kwaŋin , mam ti do kinyeis ainanakin ? Naarai luemaete naedauniata aitesegario cut irwan atipet , timam bobo kilepilep adiakar .
58010003	Konye kotoma asuban ŋun ejai aisiitunio adiakanareta ŋolikaru , ŋolikaru .
58010004	Naarai mam epedorete aokot nuka imoŋin ka akinei alemar adiakanareta .
58010005	Naarai naalomunia Kristo toma akwapin abala ebe , “ Mam ibu kokoto asubanit ka ainakinet , Konye ibu kitemok akuan kanukaŋ ;
58010006	Mam isiyalamikinit ainakineta nuicweio , karaida ainakineta nuka adiakar .
58010007	Kasodi kener ebe , ‘ Koany , abu eoŋ , ’ ( Iwadikatai nukaŋ oitabo lonunuko ) ‘ Aswam nuikoto ijo , wu Edeke . ’ ”
58010008	Naarai naenerar kokuju ebe , “ Asuban ka ainakineta ka ainakineta nuicweio , ka nuka adiakar , mam ibu kokoto , karaida aisiyalamikin , ” ( ŋun kes nueinanakinio kwape ejaatar ikisila ) ,
58010009	kosodi konyet einer ebe , “ Koany , abu eoŋ aswam nuikoto ijo . ” Elemari nasodit tetere iticasi nakiareit .
58010010	Kotoma akot kaŋin aponi oni kitalaun kanuka ainakinet naka akuan naka Yesu Kristo irwan atipet bon .
58010011	Ŋolisasedoti da ebwoi ŋinipaaran kotoma aijaanakinike , icebokinit ainanakin asuban ŋupeŋun , numam cut epedorete alemar adiakanareta .
58010012	Konye nakedaunia Kristo ainakin asubanit adiopet kanuka adiakanareta naedauni ikar kere , kosodi kiboikin akan nakoteten naka Edeke ,
58010013	ameuni kanen idareunit aitodol naibwaikinere lukasurupoke araun iicoloŋ yenika akejeke ,
58010014	Naarai kotoma ainakinet adiopet abu kitodolik luitalaunio kiton ikar kere .
58010015	Emoyo Lokalaunan da itejenari nuwok , naarai naadaunia einer ebe ,
58010016	“ Ebala Ejakait ebe , Na ŋes aitutuket naetutuki kakes , Akaulo kapaarasia kaŋun , Epikakini ikakisila otauonokec , Ewadikakini da aomisiokec . ” “ Mam bobo eituni adiakanaretakec ka epalikec . ”
58010017	Kosodi konyet ebala ebe , “ Mam bobo eituni adiakanaretakec ka epalikec . ”
58010018	Konye napejaar alemario ŋun , mam bobo einakinio asubanit kanuka adiakar .
58010019	Aso iinacan , naarai kija katitiŋ alomar toma aibois nakalaunan kanuka aokot nuka Yesu ,
58010020	kotoma orot lokitetet ka loejari da , lokicilakini oni kotoma aigalisit , ŋes atemar ebe , akekuan ,
58010021	ido kwape kijaar kesasedoti lokapolon loeyait etogo loka Edeke ,
58010022	kekunyakis ketau lokabeit , ka aiyuun naedoliorit cut , kobwatai itauonowok da ainyein aomisio nueroko , kiloŋai da awatewok kakipi nuelaete .
58010023	Keketakis alimor amunowok komam kiriaŋiriaŋa , naarai lokisumunit erai lomunot .
58010024	Kaomoomas aisinyikokin bonik ka bonik amin ka aswam nuejokuka ,
58010025	kenyeis apalun atukonokin nepepe , kwape iswamaata ice , konye kecoras ; ido keyatanakinito ŋun kwape ianyuniata apaaran ŋin eyapuunit adolun .
58010026	Naarai arai kilosikinit adiakanar nakiidaunia ainakinio ajenun abeit , mam esalit bobo asubanit kanuka adiakanareta ,
58010027	dimarai aidarit kakurian atubokinio , ka adedeŋ naka akim naebunit aicwe lukasurup .
58010028	Yenemwaŋi ikisila luka Musa etwani komam itimio , kanuka ikajenak iarei arai iuni .
58010029	Iwomito biai , nanyoin aiticanet naitelekarit noi naibusakinit ituŋanan yenipudapudai Okoku loka Edeke , komunaa da aokot nuka aitutuket , nuapotu kitalaut ŋes , komor da Emoyo loka asianut ?
58010030	Naarai kijeni ŋol loabu kiner ebe , “ Enyaŋit ŋes lokaŋ , eoŋ ataci . ” Bobo da ebe , “ Irabakini Ejakait iketuŋa . ”
58010031	Erai akirot naesogim aibirokin akanin nuka Edeke lokajaran .
58010032	Konye kiitutu apaarasia nukolo , naidauniata ainwakakinio , nuititiŋikinioto aut naepol naka aisiriebio ,
58010033	acepakio araun lusesena kanuka amoromor ka areio , acepakio da naimorianakinotor kaluiswamakinio ŋun .
58010034	Naarai ipotu kitimoto ienan , ido ipotu kotitiŋikis kalakara aŋatario naka ikusiboro , kojenete ebe ejaas yes iboro luejok adepar ido lueperonorete .
58010035	Aso sirikicakasi atitinikus , naejai eropit loepol .
58010036	Naarai ipudasi atitiŋikin , tetere iswamaete nuekoto Edeke , kosodete kijaut naisumunitai .
58010037	“ Naarai eriŋa esalit apak naedit noi , Kosodi loebuni ebuni komam itumor ;
58010038	Konye ekadolitonika ejari kanuka aiyuun , Ido arai eboŋori kau , Mam ekatau elelakinit ŋes . ”
58010039	Konye mam oni kirai lukibonori kau toma amudiario , konye kirai luka aiyuun kanuka aitajar aijar ,
58011001	Aiyuun ŋes apetetait naka akiro nuemunoi , aitogogoŋet naka akiro numam eanyuna .
58011002	Naarai kotomakeŋ ŋes etejenunere imakio .
58011003	Kanuka aiyuun kijen ebe kesubio akwapin kere kakirot naka Edeke , tetere mam iswamao nueanyuna kotoma kaŋun kanuetakanete .
58011004	Kanuka aiyuun abu Abel koinak Edeke asubanit naitelekarit naka Kain kajokis , kanuka ŋin ŋes kitejenikinere araut loedolit , kitejen Edeke kanuka acamun ainakinetake , ido kanuka aiyuunike , karaida abu kotwana , konye eriŋa inera .
58011005	Kanuka aiyuun aponi koyaŋaarai Enok tetere mam eanyuni atwanare , ido mam abu kotakan , naarai abu Edeke koyaŋa ŋes . Naarai eriŋa eyanaara etejenikinitai ebe abu kitelel Edeke .
58011006	Konye neemamea aiyuun mam epedor aitelel ŋes . Naarai yenikunyakini Edeke ibusakinit aiyuun ebe ejai ŋesi , ido ebe eropi ŋul luemoete ŋes .
58011007	Kanuka aiyuun abu Noa loekwenyarit Edeke kanuka akiro nukeroko etakanuna , koyoŋ ejok , kitemok ataker aitaiaria lukokaleke ; kanuka gin kotubok akwapin aitelekario , koraun ekerunan loka adolit naejai toma aiyuun .
58011008	Kanuka aiyuun abu Aburaam korimak nakenyaraunere alomar toma aibois naelosio ainakin araun airumet ; abu koloma komam ejeni neelosi .
58011009	Kanuka aiyuun abu kiboioror kakwap naka aisumunet , bala akwap namere nakeŋ , iboienenei koweman nepepe ka Isaak ka Yakob ikerumak lukaupake luka aisumunet ŋipeŋin .
58011010	Naarai abu kidareunite ere loejaas apeteta , loapwakun Edeke loaduki da .
58011011	Kanuka aiyuun abu Sara alopet kodum apedor apotuun karaida kedepara ikaruke , naarai abu koomite ŋol loesumuni araut lomunot .
58011012	Kanuka ŋun anyoun kotuŋanan ediopet , ido loasubit bala etwanit , aponi kowuriai lueputosi bala aacer nuka akuj kaipues , ido kwape asiŋe naejai ariri naka aŋolol namam imarun .
58011013	Apotu ŋul kere kotwakikis toma aiyuun , koroko einakina nuesumunitai , konye apotu koanyutu kimalaete da kama elwana , kolimosi ebe keraas imo ka ikalotok kakwap .
58011014	Naarai luinerasi nuikote nen isideleleunito ebe emoete akwap naebeit kes .
58011015	Ido arai kiitunito akwap ŋin naalomuniata , tiejaas kapak aboŋor .
58011016	Konye kwana iŋobeleete akwap naitelekarit ajokis , ŋes nakotoma akuj . Ŋes mam irumiata Edeke ileic anyarao Edekekec , naarai abu kitemok kes ere .
58011017	Kanuka aiyuun , abu Aburaam koinak Isaak , naetemere , ido loabu kodum aisumuneta kalakara etemokino ainakin okokuke loteluna ,
58011018	loaponi kinerai ebe , “ Kotoma Isaak ŋes enyaraere akoniwur . ”
58011019	Koomite ebe epedori Edeke aitajarun , kiton kokatwak da ; neadumunia kotoma aput .
58011020	Kanuka aiyuun abu Isaak kilipak Yakob ka Esau arereŋ kotoma akiro nuepote .
58011021	Kanuka aiyuun keapu Yakob atwanare , abu kilipak odwe luka Yosep kere iarei arereŋ , koma , kokukumi kakou naka ebelake .
58011022	Kanuka aiyuun keapu Yosep atwanare abu kiner nuka anyoun naka idwe luka Isirael , kicorak da nuka akojoke .
58011023	Kanuka aiyuun nakeuriere Musa , apotu ikauriakake kimunonata ŋes ilapio iuni , naarai aanyunito ebe itemelel ikoku ; komam ekuriaka aicorakinet naka ekabaka .
58011024	Kanuka aiyuun nakepoloor Musa , kogir anyarao okoku loka apese naka Parao ,
58011025	koseu aikonakinio erono nepepe kituŋa luka Edeke itia aitalakara kotoma aronis naka apak naedit .
58011026	Koomite amorosit naka Kristo araut abar naepol itia iboro luka akais nuipu luko Misiri , naarai abu kosesen aropio .
58011027	Kanuka aiyuun abu konyou ko Misiri , komam ekuriana adedeŋ naka ekabaka ; naarai abu konirik bala eanyuni lomam etakani .
58011028	Kanuka aiyuun abu koricite Aleleŋ ka aibwat aokot kinyek Ekamudiaran ikiyaik atiror kes .
58011029	Kanuka aiyuun apotu kitoroto Aŋolol Nakareŋan bala akwap naeonit ; konye naketamakiniata Imisirian aitor nen , kolumosi .
58011030	Kanuka aiyuun kotiyaros arwatatin nuka Yeriko , nakedaunere airimor apaarasia akanykaarei .
58011031	Kanuka aiyuun mam Rakab naadote emudiara nepepe ka lumam erimasi , naarai abu kisukunyik ikarotak kainapakin .
58011032	Kener anyoika bobo ? Naarai mam apak kelosikino arai kalimok nuka Gideon , ka Barak , ka Samuson , ka Yeputa , ka Daudi , ka Samuel ka inabin da , —
58011033	lukipikorete ajakanuto kanuka aiyuun , kiswamata adolit , kodumut aisumuneta , kitubutaasi aituke nuka iŋatunyo ,
58011034	kitojonata apedor naka akim , kokuata akwanis naka ekileŋ , kisipedoroi nakekalanyakatar , koraut lukagogoŋ kotoma ojie , kitekerata ajoresio nuka lukacekwapin .
58011035	Apotu aŋor kodumut lukatwakakec kotoma aitajarunio , konye ice aponi kisiriebai kaibworit , komam ecamunete ayuunio , tetere edumunete aitajarunio naejok adepar .
58011036	Aponi ice kitemoi kaisekelio ka aleio , eebo , kiton aeneta ka aidaris da .
58011037	Aponi kibiribiroi kamor , kotuboi kimusumenon , kitemoi , aponi koarai kekileŋ ; apotu kirimirimoto enapito imukulen luka imerekekin ka luka akinei ; apotu kilwaritos , ereitai , kikonakinitai erono , —
58011038	ituŋa lumam ebusakinit akwap , apotu kilokidaete kamodiŋo , ka oroŋan , ka abuai ka apanya da nuka akwap .
58011039	Ituŋa ŋul kere da nakedaunere aitejenun kanuka aiyuunikec , mam edumuna aisumunet ,
58011040	naarai abu Edeke kojenikinite ibore yenejok aitelekarit kanuwok , tetere ŋul mam itodolikinio komam oni .
58012001	Aso naarai kilukunit oni kere elisina loepol loetia nen , loka ikajenak , kalacasi ŋinibore kere yenelaŋir ; adiakar da naepatanikinit aigogo leonor oni , kaboloboloto katitiŋ epeget loibwaikinitai kakonyenewok ,
58012002	kasesenete Yesu , ekagean ka eketodolon loka aiyuuniwok , loabu kotitiŋik emusalaba , komen ileic , kanuka aiyalama naebwaikinitai kakonyeneke , iboie kakan nakoteten naka eicoloŋ loka Edeke .
58012003	Koomoomata do noi ŋol loketitiŋikini asurup naetia nen naka ikadiakanarak kanukeŋ , kinyeis aipas , kiiloros kotauonokus .
58012004	Mam ber ijiito kiton abukor aokot , iwutas kadiakar .
58012005	Bobo kimurwok aicor , nainera kayes kwape odwe ebe , “ Okokuka , sirimwaŋenenei alecor naka Ejakait , Kwabo sirikiilor nakiriemeriemaa ŋesi .
58012006	Naarai elecori Ejakait yenemina , Elei da ŋinikoku yenecamunit ŋesi . ”
58012007	Kanuka alecorio ititiŋikinete . Kiswamakini yes Edeke kwape odwe ; naarai ikoku inyoin yenimam papake elecori ?
58012008	Aso arai mam kilecorio , naimorikikinit kere , kwaŋin iraas lukiwurikinitai okal ! kwabo mere odwe .
58012009	Bobo da ajaas oni lukapapawok luka akuan lukiileconorete , oni da kayoŋito kes . Mam itelekarit noi oni anonokikin Papa loka imoyon , kajara da ?
58012010	Naarai apotu kesi koleconorete oni apaarasia nuikidioko , kwape kekototor , konye ŋol kilecori kanuka ajokis tetere kimori alauniteke .
58012011	Alecorio kere naka apak kana mam esubit bala nakaiyalama , dimarai nakican ; konye kokau erai araito nuinapakina nuka adolit , kama kaŋul kaluituutooritai kaŋin .
